śvaso 'vasīyas. 27. 
śvasa ity asmāt param avasīyo rājādi bhavati, śobhanam avasīyaḥ, śvo 'vasīyasaṃ kalyānam iti.

nisaś ca śreyas. 28.
cakāraḥ śvaso 'nukarṣaṇārthaḥ, nisaḥ śvasaś ca paraṃ śreyo rājādi bhavati, niḥśreyasam, śvaḥśreyasam, kalyāṇam ity arthaḥ.

anvavataptebhyo rahas. 29.
ebhyo raho rājādi bhavati, anurahasam, avarahasam, taptarahasam.

prater uras ādhāraś cet. 30.
yady ādhāraḥ syāt tadā prateḥ para urasśabdo rājādir bhavati, urasi vartate, pratyurasam, urasīty arthaḥ.
ādhāra iti kim? pratyuraḥ.

anugavam āyāmavati. 31.
āyāmo dairghyam.
anugavam atpratyayāntaṃ nipātyate dairghyaṃ cet, gavām anuyātaṃ śakaṭam, anugavam.
āyāmavatīti kim? gavāṃ paścāt, anugu, paścādarthe 'vyayībhāvaḥ.

upasargād adhvan. 32.
prādeḥ paro 'dhvanśabdo rājādir bhavati, pragato 'dhvānam, prādhvo rathaḥ, atyadhvaṃ śakaṭam.
upasargagrahaṇaṃ sukhārthaṃ prader iti siddhatvāt.

udakapāṇḍukṛṣṇebhyo bhūmiḥ. 33.
ebhyo bhūmī rājādir bhavati, udīcī bhūmir yatra, udagbhūmaḥ, evaṃ pāṇḍubhūmaḥ, kṛṣṭabhūmo deśaḥ.

saṃkhyāyā nadīgodāvaryau ca. 34.
ekādayaḥ saṃkhyā, asyāḥ parā nadī godāvarī bhūmiś ca rājādayo bhavanti, pañcanadam, pañcagodāvaram, nadīvācakānāṃ samāhāra avyayībhāvo dṛśyate, dve bhūmī yasya, dvibhūmaḥ prāsādaḥ.

ukteṣu strītvasaṃbhave striyām ād ā. 35.
ukteṣu panthyappura ity ādiṣv atpratyayānte strītvasaṃbhave sati striyām ād ā bhavatīty arthaḥ, sthūlaḥ panthā yasyāḥ sā sthūlapathā nagarī.
strītvasaṃbhava iti kim? lalāṭe puram.

samāhāradvandvaś cavargadaṣahāntaḥ. 36.
samāhāradvandvasamāsasthāś cavargāntadāntaṣāntahāntā rājādayo bhavanti, vāktvacam, śrīsrajam.
dakārānta, samiddṛśadam. 
ṣānta, vāgdviṣam.
hānta, pīṭhacchāttropānaham.
samāhāradvandvasthād iti kim? raktatvacau.

ito 'vyayībhāvaḥ. 37.
itaḥ paro bahuvrīheḥ prāgyo vidhiḥ sa rājādayo vakṣyante, te 'vyayībhāvasamāse bhavantīty adhikriyate.

śaradvipāś-ayascetasmanas-upānahvidaḥ saṃjñāyām. 38.
ete 'vyayībhāvasamāsāntāḥ saṃjñāyāṃ rājādayo bhavanti, śaradaḥ samīpam upaśaradam, upavipāśam, upāyasam, upacetasam, upamanasam, upopānaham, upavidam.

himavant dvidhā. 39.
etau rājādī bhavataḥ, upahimavatam, upadvidham.

anaḍvāh viś catvār yad tad. 40.
avyayībhāvasamāsa ete rājādayo bhavanti, upānaḍuham, upaviśam, upacaturam, upayadam, upatadam.

jarā jaraś ca. 41.
jarāśabdo rājādir bhavati nirdiṣṭasya jarāśabdasya jarasādeśaś ca, upajarasam.

pratisamanubhyo 'kṣi. 42.
ebhyo 'kṣiśabdo rājādir bhavati, pratyakṣam, samakṣam, anvakṣam.

upaśvan. 43.
upād eva śvanśabdo rājādir bhavati, nānyasmād iti, upaśunam.
niyamaḥ kim? adhiśva.

saharajas. 44.
sahāt paro rajasśabdo rājādir bhavati, sarajasam abhyavaharati, sākalye 'vyayībhāvaḥ.

annantaḥ. 45.
annantaśabdo rājādir bhavati, adhyātmam, uparājam.

napuṃsakaṃ vā. 46.
napuṃsakaliṅgam anantaṃ rājādi bhavati vā, upacarmam, upacarma.

dhuḍantaḥ. 47.
napuṃsakam iti na vartate, adhikārasyeṣṭaviṣayatvāt, dhuḍantaśabdo rājādir bhavati vā, upasamidham, upasamit, upadṛśadam, upadṛśat.

giri nadī paurṇamāsī āgrahāyaṇī. 48.
ete catvāro rājādayo bhavanti vā, upagiram, upagiri, upanadam, upanadi, upapaurṇamāsam, upapaurṇamāsi, upāgrahāyaṇam, upāgrahāyaṇi.

ito bahuvrīhiḥ. 49. 
itaḥ paraṃ ya adantā vakṣyante te bahuvrīhau samāse bhavantīty arthaḥ.

sakthyakṣiṇī svāṅge. 50. 
etau svāṅge vartamānau rājādī bhavataḥ, dīrghaṃ sakthy asya, dīrghasakthaḥ, evaṃ viśālākṣaḥ.
svāṅga iti kim? dīrghasakthiḥ, sthūlākṣirikṣuḥ, aprāṇisthatvād asvāṅgatā.

dāruṇy aṅguliḥ. 51.
dāruṇi vartamāno 'ṅgulyanto bahuvrīhau rājādir bhavati, dve aṅgulī yasya, dvyaṅgulaṃ dāru.

dvitribhyāṃ mūrdhan. 52.
ābhyāṃ mūrdhanśabdo bahuvrīhau rājādir bhavati, dvau mūrdhānau yasya sa dvimūrdhaḥ, evaṃ trimūrdhaḥ.

ukteṣu strītvasaṃbhave nadāditvād ī. 53.
ukteṣu sakthyakṣiṇī svāṅga ity ādiṣu ya adantās tebhyo nadāditvād īpratyayo bhavatīty arthaḥ, dīrghasakthī, viśālākṣīty ādi.

pūraṇīpramāṇyau. 54.
pūraṇapratyayāntā strī pūraṇī, pūraṇīpramāṇīśabdau rājādī bhavataḥ, sā ced bahuvrīhis tasyām eva pūraṇyām anyapadārthatve na vartate.
tad etan mukhyapūraṇīgrahaṇāt, kalyāṇīpañcamā rātrayaḥ.
mukhyapūraṇīti kim? kalyāṇapañcamīkaḥ pakṣaḥ, strīpramāṇāḥ kuṭumbinaḥ, pramāṇaśabdenaiva siddhe kapratyayabādhanārtho 'yam, yathā kalyāṇapañcamīkaḥ pakṣaḥ.

antarbahirbhyāṃ loman. 55.
ābhyāṃ lomanśabdo rājādir bhavati, antarlomaḥ, bahirlomaḥ.

nakṣatrān netṛ. 56.
nakṣatram aśvinyādi, nakṣatravācakāc chabdāt paro netṛśabdo rājādir bhavati, mṛganetrā rātriḥ, puṣyanetrā.
nakṣatrād iti kim? Devadattanetrakaḥ.

nañsuvyupatribhyaś catvāraḥ. 57.
ebhyaś catvārśabdo rājādir bhavati, acaturaḥ, sucaturaḥ, vicaturaḥ, upacaturaḥ, tricaturaḥ.
ebhya iti kim? pañcacatvāraḥ.

saṃjñāyāṃ nābhiḥ. 58.
bahuvrīhau nābhī rājādir bhavati, saṃjñāyāṃ gamyamānāyām, padmanābhaḥ, vajranābhaḥ.
saṃjñājām iti kim? padmanābhiḥ.

nañsudurbhyaḥ sakthi vā. 59.
ebhyaḥ sakthi rājādi bhavati vā.
asakthaḥ, asakthiḥ, susakthaḥ, susakthiḥ, duḥsakthaḥ, duḥsakthiḥ.

iti ratneśvaracakravartiviracitarājādivṛttiḥ samāptā.
rājādir ākṛtigaṇo 'yam.
以下已翻译

ḍānubandhe 'ntyasvarāder lopaḥ. Kāt_2,6.42. 

ḍānubandhe pratyaye pare 'ntyasvarāder avayavasya lopo bhavati, catvāriṃśataḥ pūraṇaḥ, catvāriṃśaḥ, evaṃ pañcāśaḥ, sarasijam, jalajam, saptamīpañcamyante janer ḍaḥ.


ter viṃśater api. Kāt_2,6.43

ḍānubandhe pratyaye pare viṃśater api ter lopo bhavati, viṃśateḥ pūraṇaḥ, viṃśaḥ.


ivarṇāvarṇayor lopaḥ svare pratyaye ye ca. Kāt_2,6.44

ivarṇāvarṇayor lopo bhavati, taddhite svare ye ca pratyaye parataḥ, ātreyaḥ, drauṇeyaḥ, dākṣiḥ, plākṣiḥ, gāṅgeyaḥ, gārgyaḥ, tulyaḥ.
punar lopagrahaṇād avyayānām antyasvarāder lopo lakṣyataḥ, sāyaṃprātarbhavaḥ, sāyaṃprātikaḥ, paunaḥpunikaḥ, bāhyam ity ādayaḥ.


nas tu kva cit. Kāt_2,6.45

nakārasya lopo bhavati kva cil lakṣyānurodhāt, taddhite svare pare, auḍulomiḥ, āgniśarmiḥ, dve ahanī samāhūte, dvyahaḥ, tryahaḥ.


uvarṇas tv otvam āpādyaḥ. Kāt_2,6.46

uvarṇas tv otvam āpādanīyaḥ, taddhite svare ye ca pratyaye parataḥ.
aupagavaḥ, bābhravyaḥ.


eye 'kadrvās tu lupyate. Kāt_2,6.47

uvarṇas tu lupyate, eye pratyaye pare, na tu kadrūśabdasya, kāmaṇḍaleyaḥ, mādrabāheyaḥ.
akadrvā iti kim? kādraveyā nāgāḥ.


kāryāv avāvāv ādeśāv aukāraukārayor api. Kāt_2,6.48

okāraukārayoḥ sthāne 'vāvāvādeśau kāryau, taddhite svare ye ca pratyaye pare, aupagavaḥ, gavyam, nāvyam.


vṛddhir ādau saṇe. Kāt_2,6.49

svarāṇāṃ madhya ādau svarasya vṛddhir bhavati, saṇakārānubandhe taddhite pratyaye pare, śaivaḥ, aupagavaḥ, kārpaṇyam.
kathaṃ vāsiṣṭhaḥ, ādāv ity ākārapraśleṣāt.
kva cid adhikārād uttarapadasyāpi lakṣyataḥ, avayavād ṛtūnām, pūrvavārṣikam, aparahaimantam, varṣaikadeśe hemantaikadeśe varṣāhemantau.
susarvārdhebhyo janapadasya ca, supāñcālikaḥ, sarvapāñcālikaḥ, ardhapāñcālikaḥ.
kva cid ubhayapadasyāpi, saubhāgyam, sauhārdam, saktupradhānāḥ sindhavaḥ, tatrabhavaḥ sāktusaindhavaḥ, evam anye 'py anusartavyāḥ.


na yvoḥ padādyor vṛddhir āgamaḥ. Kāt_2,6.50

iha pratiṣedho vidhiś ca gamyate, ādiśabdaḥ samīpavacanaḥ, padasyādyor yakāravakārayoḥ samīpe vṛddhir na bhavati, tayoś cādau vṛddhir āgamo bhavati, saṇakārānubandhe taddhite, sthāne 'ntaratama iti nyāyād yakārasyaikāro vakārasyaukāraḥ.
vyasane bhavaḥ, vaiyasanaḥ, vyudayasyāpatyam, vaiyudayaḥ, svaśvasyāpatyam, sauvaśviḥ, vyākaraṇaṃ vettyadhīte vā vaiyākaraṇaḥ.
yvoḥ samīpa iti kim? dādhyaśviḥ, mādhvaśviḥ, tannimitto vṛddhir āgamo na syāt.
punar vṛddhigrahaṇaṃ vardhanād vṛddhir iti jñāpanārtham.
kva cid adhikārād dvārādīnāṃ cāpadādyor api vṛddhipratiṣedho vṛddhir āgamaś ca, dvāre niyukto dauvārikaḥ.
dvāra, dvārapāla, svara, vyalkasa, svasti, svar, svargamana, sphyakṛta, svādumṛdu, śvan, sva, evam anye 'py anusartavyāḥ.

iti daurgasiṃhyāṃ vṛttau nāmni catuṣṭaye taddhitapādaḥ samāptaḥ.



athākhyātam.

atha parasmaipadāni. Kāt_3,1.1

athānantarāṇi tyādīni syāmahiparyantāni parasmaipadasaṃjñakāni bhavanti, nava parāṇy ātmana ity uktibādhayā pūrvāṇi navaiva vacanāni sarvāsāṃ vibhaktīnām iti.
arthasya vibhañjanād vibhaktaya iti, ti tas anti, si thas tha, mi vas mas, evaṃ sarvatra, parasmaipadapradeśāḥ, śeṣāt kartari parasmaipadam [Kāt_3,2.47] ity evam ādayaḥ.


nava parāṇy ātmane. Kāt_3,1.2

atha parāṇi nava nava vacanāny ātmanepadasaṃjñakāni bhavanti, padānīti gamyate.
te āte ante, se āthe dhve, e vahe mahe, evaṃ sarvatra.
ātmanepadapradeśāḥ, ātmanepadāni bhāvakarmaṇoḥ [Kāt_3,2.40] ity evam ādayaḥ.


trīṇi trīṇi prathamamadhyamottamāḥ. Kāt_3,1.3

parasmaipadānām ātmanepadānāṃ ca trīṇi trīṇi vacanāni prathamamadhyamottamasaṃjñakāni bhavanti yathāsaṃkhyam, ti, tas, anti, iti prathamaḥ.
si, thas, tha, iti madhyamaḥ.
mi, vas, mas, ity uttamaḥ.
te, āte, ante, iti prathamaḥ.
se, āthe, dhve, iti madhyamaḥ.
e, vahe, mahe, ity uttamaḥ, evaṃ sarvatra.
saṃjñāpradeśāḥ, nāmni prayujyamāne 'pi prathamaḥ, yuṣmadi madhyamaḥ, asmady uttamaḥ [Kāt_3,1.5-7] ity evam ādayaḥ.


yugapadvacane paraḥ puruṣāṇām. Kāt_3,1.4

yugapad ekakālārthaḥ, yugapadvacana ekakriyākālābhidhāne puruṣāṇāṃ madhye yaḥ paraḥ sa bhavati, sa ca tvaṃ cāhaṃ ca pacāmaḥ, sa ca tvaṃ cāhaṃ cāpākṣma, sa ca tvaṃ cāhaṃ ca pakṣyāmaḥ.
vacanam atantram, sa ca tvaṃ ca pacathaḥ, tvaṃ cāhaṃ ca pacāvaḥ.
yugapadvacana iti kim? sa pacati, tvaṃ pakṣyasi, aham apākṣam iti bhinnakāloktau vayam apākṣmeti mā bhūt.
vacanagrahaṇaṃ yugapadviṣaye mā bhūt, sa pacati, tvaṃ pacasi, ahaṃ pacāmīty evaṃ prāpnoti.
apravṛttau paryāye vā prāpte paribhāṣeyam.


nāmni prayujyamāne 'pi prathamaḥ. Kāt_3,1.5

nāmni prayujyamāne 'prayujyamāne 'pi prathamaḥ puruṣo bhavati, sa pacati, tau pacataḥ, te pacanti, sa pacate, tau pacete, te pacante, evaṃ pacyate ghaṭaḥ, pacyete ghaṭau, pacyante ghaṭāḥ.
aprayujyamāne 'pi, pacati, pacataḥ, pacanti, evaṃ sarvatra.
prayujyamānagrahaṇaṃ kim? dhātunā yukte yathā syāt, tena devadattena hanyase tvam, madhyama eva yuṣmadyogāt.


yuṣmadi madhyamaḥ. Kāt_3,1.6

yuṣmadi prayujyamāne 'prayujyamāne 'pi madhyamaḥ puruṣo bhavati, tvaṃ pacasi, yuvāṃ pacathaḥ, yūyaṃ pacatha.
aprayujyamāne 'pi, pacasi, pacathaḥ, pacatha, evaṃ sarvatra.
prayujyamānagrahaṇaṃ kim? tvayā pacyata odanaḥ.


asmady uttamaḥ. Kāt_3,1.7

asmadi prayujyamāne 'prayujyamāne 'py uttamaḥ puruṣo bhavati, ahaṃ pacāmi, āvāṃ pacāvaḥ, vayaṃ pacāmaḥ.
aprayujyamāne 'pi, pacāmi, pacāvaḥ, pacāmaḥ, evaṃ sarvatra.

atvaṃ tvaṃ saṃpadyate, anaham ahaṃ saṃpadyate, tvadbhavati, madbhavatīti bhavitavyam eva, yuṣmadasmador gauṇatvāt, tvanmadī tu śabdamātrāśrayatvāt.
ehi manye rathena yāsyasi.
yātas te piteti, svaviṣaya eva madhyamottamau.


adāb dādhau dā. Kāt_3,1.8

dāpdaipau varjayitvā dādhāv ity etau dāsaṃjñakau bhavataḥ, dīyate, dhīyate.
adāb iti kim? dāyante vrīhayaḥ, nidāyante bhājanāni, pakāro 'yaṃ gaṇe pratiṣedhārtha eva nirdiśyate.


kriyābhāvo dhātuḥ. Kāt_3,1.9

yaḥ śabdaḥ kriyāṃ bhāvayati pratipādayati sa dhātusaṃjño bhavati, bhavati, atti, juhoti, dīvyati, sunoti, tudati, ruṇaddhi, tanoti, krīṇāti, corayati.
kriyata iti kriyā sādhyam ucyate, sā ca pūrvāparībhūtāvayavaiva.
kathaṃ tarhi? asti, naśyati, śvetate prāsādaḥ, saṃyujyate, samavaiti, sattā nityatā, abhāvo nāśaḥ, śvetasaṃyogāv api guṇau, samavāyo 'py arthāntaram, satyam iha hi sādhanāyattodayaṃ sarvam atas tad adhīnatayā siddham api kriyātvenāvabhāsate, kriyākārakavyavahṛter buddhyavasthānibandhanāt, tathā gati vadanaikadeśe vidhy avayave 'pi, aṅkuro jāyata iti janma cābhūt, prādurbhāva eveti, athavā jāyate viśeṣeṇopalabhyate, ato 'ṅkurasya kartṛtvam, tathā coktam.

yāvat siddham asiddhaṃ vā sādhyatvena pratīyate,
āśritakramarūpatvāt sā kriyety abhidhīyate.

dhātupradeśāḥ, dhātoś ca hetau [Kāt_3,2.10] ity evam ādayaḥ.


kāle. Kāt_3,1.10

kāla iti saptamyantam anukṛtam, kāla ity adhikṛtaṃ veditavyam, tena sādhane vartamāne 'tīte bhaviṣyati ca na syāt, grāmaṃ gato gamiṣyati cāyaṃ Devadattaḥ, Rāmo vanam agacchat, Balir Indro bhaviṣyati.
vartamānādibhiḥ kim? dhātor viśeṣaṇaṃ dravyasya veti saṃdehe 'yam adhikāraḥ, nityo vyāpī saṃpratibhūtabhaviṣyatkriyāyogād ākāśakalpa eko dravyastho bhidyate kālaḥ.


saṃprati vartamānā. Kāt_3,1.11

saṃprati kāle vartamānā vibhaktir bhavati, pacati, yajate.
svasaṃjñayaiva kālo viśiṣyate.
saṃpratīti kim? tasthuḥ, sthāsyanti girayaḥ.


smenātīte. Kāt_3,1.12

smaśabdena yoge 'tīte kāle vartamānā vibhaktir bhavati, dahati sma tripuraṃ Haraḥ, iti sma janaḥ kathayati.
atītaviṣayāṇāṃ bādhako 'yam.


parokṣā. Kāt_3,1.13

atīte kāle parokṣā vibhaktir bhavati, jaghāna kaṃsaṃ kila Vāsudevaḥ, kaṭaṃ cakre Devadattaḥ.


bhūtakaraṇavatyaś ca. Kāt_3,1.14

bhūtakālaḥ karaṇaṃ tad vidyate yāsām iti pāriśeṣyād hy astanyadyatanīkriyātipattaya eva rūḍhāḥ, etā bhūtakaraṇavatyas tisro vibhaktayo 'tīte kāle bhavanti, akarot, akārṣīt, akariṣyat.


bhaviṣyati bhaviṣyantyāśīḥśvastanyaḥ. Kāt_3,1.15

bhaviṣyati kāle bhaviṣyantyāśīḥśvastanyas tisro vibhaktayo bhavanti, kaṭaṃ kariṣyati, śakraṃ vadhyāt, odanaṃ bhoktā.


tāsāṃ svasaṃjñābhiḥ kālaviśeṣaḥ. Kāt_3,1.16

tāsāṃ vartamānādīnāṃ svasaṃjñābhiḥ kālasya viśeṣo jñeyaḥ, tena vartamāne kāle vartamānā, vartata iti vartamānaḥ, prārambho 'parisamāptiḥ.
māṃsaṃ na khādati, iha kumārāḥ krīḍanti, tiṣṭhanti parvatāḥ, kadāgato 'si, eṣa āgacchāmi, kadā gamiṣyasi, eṣa gacchāmi.

parokṣe 'tīte kāle parokṣeti, akṣāṇāṃ paraṃ parokṣam, indriyāṇām aviṣaya ity arthaḥ.
kathaṃ supto 'haṃ kiṃ vilalāpa, matto 'haṃ kiṃ vicacāra, cittasya vikṣepāt.
nāhaṃ Kaliṅgaṃ jagāma, iti gamanadoṣabhayāt pratyakṣam apy apahnute.
parokṣe lokavijñāte prayoktur darśanayogyatvāt parokṣasyāvivakṣāyāṃ hy astany api, ayajat, iyāja, sato 'pi cāvivakṣā, yathānudarā kanyeti.

hyastane 'tīte kāle hyastanī, hyobhavaḥ kālo hyastanaḥ, adya hyo vābhukṣmahīti vyāmiśre saṃnidhānād adyatanī.

adyatane 'tīte mātre 'dyatanī, adyabhāvo 'dyatanaḥ, ā nyāyyād utthānād ā nyāyyāc ca saṃveśanād ahaḥ, ubhayato 'rdharātraṃ vā lokataḥ siddham.
katham amutrāvātsaṃ sakalāṃ rātriṃ jāgaritaḥ, rātrer aprabhāvatvād adyatanam iva kālaṃ manyate, yo muhūrtam api suptaḥ so 'nadyatanaṃ jānann amutrāvasam ity āha.
agamāma ghoṣān, apāma paya iti hyastanasyāvivakṣaiva, hyo 'gamāma ghoṣān iti padārthahyastane hyastanī na vākyārtha iti matam.

kriyātipattāv atīte kāle kriyātipattir iti, edhāṃś ced alapsyata, odanam apakṣyat, bhaviṣyati kriyātipatane bhaviṣyanty eva.

bhaviṣyati kāle bhaviṣyantī, bhaviṣyatkālasya bhaviṣyadviśeṣaṇāt, adya śvo vā gamiṣyatīti śvastanīm api bādhate.

āśīryukte bhaviṣyati kāla āśīḥ, anāgatasyeṣṭārthasya lābhenāviṣkaraṇam āśīḥ, arthād bhaviṣyad viṣayaiva, yad asyā bhaviṣyadvidhānaṃ tat sukhapratipattyartham.

śvobhavaḥ kālaḥ śvastanaḥ, sa cārthād bhaviṣyan, yad asyā bhaviṣyadvidhānaṃ tat sāmānyapratipattyartham, śvo gamiṣyati, māsena gamiṣyatīti padasaṃskārāt.
anvarthasaṃjñāyāḥ prāyovṛttitvāt śaṅkaraḥ syād iti, paribhāṣeyam.


prayogataś ca. Kāt_3,1.17

prayujyata iti prayogaḥ, prayogād avadheḥ kālasya viśeṣo jñeyaḥ, arthāt padāntarasaṃbandhe, yāvad bhuṅkte tato vrajati, bhaviṣyattā gamyate, bhaviṣyantīvivakṣāyāṃ tu yāvacchabdasyāprayoga eva.
adhīṣva māṇavaka purā vidyotate vidyut, kṣipraṃ kuru kaṭaṃ purā gacchasi grāmam, vartamānasāmīpyasya tadgrahaṇena grahaṇam, purāśabdād bhaviṣyadavagame sati tadā tasya vartamānatā vā.
kadākarhiyoge vartamānābhaviṣyantīśvastanyaḥ, kadā bhuṅkte, kadā bhokṣyate, kadā bhoktā, karhi bhuṅkte, karhi bhokṣyate, karhi bhoktā.
bhaviṣyati parokṣādayo 'pi, kadā bubhuje, kadā bhuktaḥ, kadā bhuktavān.
tathā kimo vibhaktiḍataraḍatamāntasya prayoge lipsāyāṃ gamyamānāyām, bhaviṣyati bhaviṣyati sāmānye, ko bhavatāṃ bhikṣāṃ dadāti dāsyati dātā vā, kataro bhavatāṃ katamo bhavatāṃ bhikṣāṃ dadāti dāsyati dātā vā.
bhūtavihitā api dṛśyante, ko bhavatāṃ pāṭaliputram agacchat, agamad iti vā.
tathā lipsyamānāt siddhāv api, yo bhavatāṃ bhikṣāṃ dadāti dāsyati dātā vā sa svargalokaṃ yāti yāsyati yātā vā, yo bhavatāṃ bhikṣām adāt sa svargalokam agamad iti, evam anye 'py anusartavyāḥ.


pañcamy anumatau. Kāt_3,1.18

kartum icchato 'nujñānumatiḥ, sā ca vartamānabhaviṣyadvisayaiva, anumatau vartamānād dhātoḥ pañcamī bhavati, evaṃ kuru, kaṭaṃ kuru, tṛṣṇāṃ chinddhi, bhaja kṣamām, kuru dayām.


samarthanāśiṣoś ca. Kāt_3,1.19

parair aśakyasya vastuno 'dhyavasāyaḥ samarthanā, iṣṭārthasyāśaṃsanam āśīḥ, samarthanāśiṣoś ca vartamānād dhātoḥ pañcamī bhavati, parvatam apy utpāṭayāni.
samudram api śoṣayāṇi, kaś cid āha, samudraḥ śoṣayitum aśakyaḥ, sa āha, samudram api śoṣayāṇīti samarthyati matam asya.
āśiṣi ca, jīvatu bhavān, nandatu bhavān, api śirasā parvataṃ bhindyāt, api siñcen mūlasahasram iti vidhau saptamī, apiśabdo 'tra saṃbhāvane prayogataś ceti siddham.
nanv iṣṭāśaṃsanam api prārthanam eva, satyam, āśīrvibhaktyā bādhitā pañcamī yathā syād iti vacanam.


vidhyādiṣu saptamī ca. Kāt_3,1.20

vidhyādiṣu vartamānād dhātoḥ saptamī bhavati pañcamī ca, vidhir ajñātajñāpanam eva, kaṭaṃ kuryāt, kaṭaṃ karotu bhavān. yatra pratyākhyāne pratyavāyas tan nimantraṇam, iha bhuñjīta, iha bhuṅktāṃ bhavān.
yatra pratyākhyāne kāmacāras tad āmantraṇam, ihāsīta, ihāstāṃ bhavān.
satkārapūrvako vyāpāro 'dhyeṣaṇam, māṇavakam adhyāpayed adhyāpayatu bhavān.
nirūpaṇā saṃpraśnaḥ, kiṃ nu khalu bho vyākaraṇam adhīyīya, uta cchando 'dhīyīya, kiṃ nu khalu bho vyākaraṇam adhyayai, uta cchando 'dhyayai.
yācñā prārthanā, labheya bhikṣām, dehi me bhikṣām.
praiṣyaprāptakālayor api saptamī pañcamī syād eveti matam, preṣitas tvaṃ grāmaṃ gaccheḥ, grāmaṃ gaccha, prāptas te kālaḥ kaṭakaraṇe, kaṭaṃ kuryāt kaṭaṃ karotu bhavān.
kathaṃ vidadhyāt, nimantrayet, āmantrayet, adhīcchet, saṃpṛcchet, prārthayet, kṛtyarūpeṣu vidhyādiṣu tayor vidhānāt, yadā tu prakṛtyarthasya na kartavyatā tadā vidadhātīty ādayaḥ siddhāḥ.


kriyāsamabhihāre sarvakāleṣu madhyamaikavacanaṃ pañcamyāḥ. Kāt_3,1.21

kriyāyāḥ samabhihāraḥ paunaḥpunyaṃ bhṛśārtho vā, kriyāsamabhihāre vartamānād dhātoḥ sarvakriyākāleṣu madhyamaikavacanaṃ bhavati pañcamyāḥ, lunīhi lunīhi, ity evāyaṃ lunāti, lunītaḥ, lunanti, lunāsi, lunīthaḥ, lunītha, lunāmi, lunīvaḥ, lunīmaḥ, alunāt, laviṣyati.
adhīṣvādhīṣva, ity evāyam adhīte, adhyaita, adhyeṣyate.
sarvakriyākāleṣv iti vacanāt saṃkhyāviśeṣo na gamyata ity anuprayogaḥ, pratyāsattes tenaiva dhātunā kārakeṇeti sukhārtham evedam, anyathā, evam asau tvarāvān yad anyān api prerayan kriyāṃ karotīti vivakṣayā sidhyati.
tathā, lunīta lunīta, ity evāyaṃ yūyaṃ lunītha, adhīdhvam adhīdhvam ity evāyaṃ yūyam adhīdhve.
tathā bhrāṣṭram aṭa, maṭham aṭa, khadūram aṭa, sthānyapidhānam aṭa, ity evāyam aṭatīty ādayo vivakṣāḥ.


māyoge 'dyatanī. Kāt_3,1.22

māśabdena yoge dhātor adyatanī bhavati, mā kārṣīt, mā bhavān pākṣīt.
kathaṃ mā bhavatu, tasya pāpaṃ mā kariṣyatīti niranubandhagrahaṇāt.
ṅānubandhamāyoge na syād iti ke cit.
vartamānabhaviṣyadviṣayāṇāṃ bādhako 'yam.


māsmayoge hyastanī ca. Kāt_3,1.23

māsmaśabdena yoge dhātor hyastanī bhavati, cakārād adyatanī ca, mā sma karot, mā sma kārṣīt.
vyaste 'pīcchanti ke cit, sma karon mā.
pṛthagyogāt kevalamāyoge na syāt.


vartamānā. Kāt_3,1.24

ti tas anti, si thas tha, mi vas mas.
te āte ante, se āthe dhve, e vahe mahe.
imāni vacanāni vartamānāsaṃjñakāni bhavanti.
vartamānāpradeśāḥ, saṃprati vartamānā [Kāt_3,1.11] ity evam ādayaḥ.


saptamī. Kāt_3,1.25

yāt yātām yus, yās yātam yāta, yām yāva yāma.
īta īyātām īran, īthās īyāthām īdhvam, īya īvahi īmahi.
imāni vacanāni saptamīsaṃjñakāni bhavanti.
saptamīpradeśāḥ, vidhyādiṣu saptamī ca [Kāt_3,1.20] ity evam ādayaḥ.


pañcamī. Kāt_3,1.26

tu tām antu, hi tam ta, āni āva āma.
tām ātām antām, sva āthām dhvam, ai āvahai āmahai.
imāni vacanāni pañcamīsaṃjñakāni bhavanti.
pañcamīpradeśāḥ, pañcamy anumatau [Kāt_3,1.18] ity evam ādayaḥ.


hyastanī. Kāt_3,1.27

di tām an, si tam ta, am va ma.
ta ātām anta, thās āthām dhvam, i vahi mahi.
imāni vacanāni hyastanīsaṃjñakāni bhavanti.
hyastanīpradeśāḥ, māsmayoge hyastanī [Kāt_3,1.23] ity evam ādayaḥ.


evam evādyatanī. Kāt_3,1.28

evam evādyatanī bhavati.
adyatanīpradeśāḥ, māyoge 'dyatanī [Kāt_3,1.22] ity evam ādayaḥ.


parokṣā. Kāt_3,1.29

aṭ atus us, thal athus a, aṭ va ma.
e āte ire, se āthe dhve, e vahe mahe.
imāni vacanāni parokṣāsaṃjñakāni bhavanti.
parokṣāpradeśāḥ, parokṣā [Kāt_3,1.13] ity evam ādayaḥ.


śvastanī. Kāt_3,1.30

tā tārau tāras, tāsi tāsthas tāstha, tāsmi tāsvas tāsmas.
tā tārau tāras, tāse tāsāthe tādhve, tāhe tāsvahe tāsmahe.
imāni vacanāni śvastanīsaṃjñakāni bhavanti.
śvastanīpradeśāḥ, bhaviṣyati bhaviṣyantyāśīḥśvastanyaḥ [Kāt_3,1.15] ity evam ādayaḥ.


āśīḥ. Kāt_3,1.31

yāt yāstām yāsus, yās yāstam yāsta, yāsam yāsva yāsma.
sīṣta sīyāstām sīran, sīṣṭhās sīyāsthām sīdhvam, sīya sīvahi sīmahi.
imāni vacanāny āśīḥsaṃjñakāni bhavanti.
āśīḥpradeśāḥ, āśiṣi ca parasmai [Kāt_3,5.22] ity evam ādayaḥ.


syasaṃhitāni tyādīni bhaviṣyantī. Kāt_3,1.32

dhātoḥ parāṇi syena saṃhitāni tyādīni bhaviṣyantīsaṃjñakāni bhavanti, syati syatas syanti, syasi syathas syatha, syāmi syāvas syāmas.
syate syete syante, syase, syethe syadhve, sye syāvahe syāmahe.
bhaviṣyantīpradeśāḥ, bhaviṣyati bhaviṣyantyāśīḥśvastanyaḥ [Kāt_3,1.15] ity evam ādayaḥ.


dyādīni kriyātipattiḥ. Kāt_3,1.33

dhātoḥ parāṇi syena saṃhitāni dyādīni kriyātipattisaṃjñakāni bhavanti, syat syatām(←tyatām) syan, syas syatam syata, syam syāva syāma.
syata syetām syanta, syathās syethām syadhvam, sye syāvahi syāmahi.
kriyātipattipradeśāḥ, aḍ dhātvādir hyastanyadyatanīkriyātipattiṣu [Kāt_3,8.16] ity evam ādayaḥ.
etāḥ pūrvācāryaprasiddhāḥ saṃjñā anvarthā iha jñāpyante.


ṣaḍādyāḥ sārvadhātukam. Kāt_3,1.34

ṣaṇṇāṃ vibhaktīnām ādyā vartamānāsaptamīpañcamīhyastanyaḥ sārvadhātukasaṃjñā bhavanti.
sārvadhātukapradeśāḥ, juhotyādīnāṃ sārvadhātuke [Kāt_3,3.8] ity evam ādayaḥ.

iti daurgasiṃhyāṃ vṛttāv ākhyāte prathamaḥ pādaḥ samāptaḥ.



pratyayaḥ paraḥ. Kāt_3,2.1

pratīyate yenārthaḥ sa pratyaya iti rūḍhiḥ, yathāpratyayāt prathamaṃ kriyata iti prakṛtiḥ, prakṛteḥ paraḥ pratyayo veditavyaḥ, vṛkṣaḥ, aśvakaḥ, yāvakaḥ, khaṭvā, aupagavaḥ, jugupsate, gopāyati, kartā, kartavyaḥ.
aniyame prāpte paribhāṣeyaṃ vidhyaṅgaśeṣabhūtā vā.


guptijkidbhyaḥ san. Kāt_3,2.2

guptijkidbhyaḥ san paro bhavati svārthe, jugupsate mām, titikṣate tapas tāpasaḥ, vicikitsati me manaḥ, cikitsaty āturaṃ vaidyaḥ, ripuṃ cikitsati, cikitsyāni kṣetre tṛṇāni.

gupo badheś ca nindāyāṃ kṣayāyāṃ ca tathā tijaḥ,
saṃśaye ca pratīkāre kitaḥ sann abhidhīyate.

akāroccāraṇaṃ kim? svarāder dvitīyasya [Kāt_3,3.2] iti dvirvacanārtham, tenārthān pratīṣiṣati.


mānbadhdānśānbhyo dīrghaś cābhyāsasya. Kāt_3,2.3

mānādibhyaḥ san paro bhavati svārthe, dīrghaś caiṣām abhyāsasyeto bhavati, mīmāṃsate, bībhatsate, dīdāṃsate, śīśāṃsate.
abhyāsavikāreṣv apavādo notsargaṃ bādhate.
katham avadānam, niśānam iti dyateḥ śyateś ca yuṭā siddham.
caurādikena mānaḥ, mānayati.
dān śān ubhayam, kit parasmai.


dhātor vā tumantād icchatinaikakartṛkāt. Kāt_3,2.4

vā tumanto yasyeti vigrahaḥ, vā tumantād dhātor icchatinaikakartṛkāt san paro bhavati, kartum icchati, cikīrṣati, bhoktum icchati, bubhukṣate.
sanā dyotitatvād iṣer aprayogaḥ, ke cit sani cāniṭi [Kāt_3,5.7] iti jñāpakāt tumaviṣayād ity āhuḥ.
dhātor iti kim? prācikīrṣat. 
tumantād iti kim? bhojanam icchati.
icchāyām iti siddha ekakartṛkād iti spaṣṭārtham.
icchāsanantāt san na bhavati svātmani kriyāvirodhāt.
kathaṃ nadīkūlaṃ pipatiṣati, śvā mumūrṣati, yathā vākyaṃ tathedaṃ vivakṣayeti matam.


nāmna ātmecchāyāṃ yin. Kāt_3,2.5

nāmna ātmecchāyām arthe yin paro bhavati, putram icchati, putrīyati, evaṃ ghaṭīyati.
ātmaśabdo 'trādhyātmavacana eva mandadhiyāṃ sukhārthaḥ, bhrātuḥ putram icchati, mahāntaṃ putram icchati, ātmanaḥ putram icchatīti sāpekṣatvāt, bhrātṛputrīyatīti yuktārthatvāt.
icchayā nāmnaḥ saṃbandhād dātreṇecchatīty akarmaṇo na syāt sāpekṣatvāt.
vyavasthitavāsmaraṇād māntāvyayābhyāṃ na syāt, kim icchati, svar icchati.


kāmya ca. Kāt_3,2.6

nāmna ātmecchāyām arthe kāmyaḥ paro bhavati, cakārād yiṃś ca, etac cottarārtham evānantaraḥ kāmyo mā bhūd iti, putram icchati, putrakāmyati, idaṃkāmyati, svaḥkāmyati.


upamānād ācāre. Kāt_3,2.7

upamānān nāmna ācāre 'bhidheye yin paro bhavati, putram ivācarati, putrīyati māṇavakam, māṇavakād viśeṣe dvitīyā noktārtheti.
ādhārād api syād nirapekṣatvāt, kuṭyām ivācarati, kuṭīyati prāsāde.


kartur āyiḥ salopaś ca. Kāt_3,2.8

kartur upamānān nāmna ācāre 'bhidheya āyiḥ paro bhavati salopaś ca yathāsaṃbhavam, śyena ivācarati, śyenāyate, evaṃ sārasāyate, ojāyate, apsarāyate, payāyate, payasyate, vāśabdasyeṣṭārthatvāt.
āyeś ca lopaḥ, gardabha ivācarati, gardabhati, aśvatīti matam.
kathaṃ galbhate, klīvate, hoḍate, eta ātmanepadinaḥ, pratyayāntatvād ām iṣyata eva.

ojaso 'psaraso nityaṃ payaso tu vibhāṣayā,
āyilopaś ca vijñeyo na cāśvo gardabhaty api.

tathā cvyarthe bhṛśādes tasor lopaś ceti, abhṛśo bhṛśo bhavati, bhṛśāyate, evam unmanāyate, durmanāyate.
vehat, vehāyate.
śaśvat, śaśvāyate.
vāvacanāc cvir api, bhṛśībhavati, abhṛśo yo bhṛśo bhavati sa bhṛśa ivācarati, sādṛśyād abhedo vastuna iti matam, talopeṣṭir iti.
tathā ḍājlohitādibhyaś cvyarthe, paṭapaṭāyati, paṭapaṭāyate, lohitāyati, lohitāyate, yajādiṣu pāṭha iṣyate.
kaṣṭāya karmaṇe krāmati, kaṣṭāyate, evaṃ pāpāyate, kakṣāyate, satrāyate, gahanāyate.
pāpavṛttibhyo 'nyatra na bhavati, kaṣṭāya tapase krāmati.
romanthaṃ vartayati, romanthāyate gauḥ, hanucalana eveha na syāt, kīṭo romanthaṃ vartayati.
bāṣpam udvamati, bāṣpāyate, evam uṣmāyate, phenāyate.
sukhādīni vedayate, sukhaṃ vedayate, sukhāyate, evaṃ duḥkhāyate.
śabdādīni karoti, śabdaṃ karoti, śabdāyate, evaṃ vairāyate, kalahāyate.
namastapovarivasas tu yin, namaskaroti, namasyati devān, evaṃ tapasyati śatrūn, varivasyati gurūn.
citraṅ āścarye, āścaryaṃ citraṃ karoti, citrīyate.
kaṇḍvādibhyo yan, kaṇḍūñ, kaṇḍūṃ karoti, kaṇḍūyati, kaṇḍūyate.
mahīṅ, mahīyate, ity ādayo 'py anusartavyāḥ, etat sarvaṃ vāśabdena bahulārthena vā siddham.


in kāritaṃ dhātvarthe. Kāt_3,2.9

dhātvarthe kriyānāmna in paro bhavati dhātvarthe sa ca kāritasaṃjñakaḥ, haliṃ kaliṃ gṛhṇāti, halayati, kalayati, evaṃ kṛtayati, varṇayati, tvacayati.
tūstāni vihanti, vitūstayati.
vastraṃ samācchādayati, saṃvastrayati.
varmaṇā saṃnahyati, saṃvarmayati.
cūrṇair avadhvasate, avacūrṇayati.

tat karoti, tad ācaṣṭe.
muṇḍaṃ karoti, muṇḍayati, evaṃ miśrayati, ślakṣṇayati, lavaṇayati, sūtrayati, payo vratayati, payo bhuṅkta iti gamyate, vṛṣalānnaṃ vratayati, bhuṅkta ity arthaḥ.
satyam ācaṣṭe, satyāpayati, evam arthāpayati, vedāpayati.
priyam ācaṣṭe, prāpayati, ābāgamaś ca.
tenātikrāmati, hastinātikrāmati, atihastayati.
kartṛkaraṇārthe, vīṇayopagāyati, upavīṇayati, tūlair avakuṣṇāti, avatūlayati, ślokair upastauti, upaślokayati, senayābhiyāti, abhiṣeṇayati.
kadā cid darśane, rūpaṃ paśyati, nirūpayati, bahulam etan nidarśanam.
tathā inaṅ aṅganirasane 'pi, hastau nirasyati, hastayate.
pādau nirasyati, pādayate.
evaṃ puccham utkṣipati, utpucchayate gauḥ.
pucchaṃ parikṣipati, paripucchayate.
evaṃ bhāṇḍāni samācinoti, saṃbhāṇḍayate vaṇik, cīvaraṃ saṃmārjayati paridadhāti vā, saṃcīvarayate bhikṣuḥ.
diṅmātram idaṃ gaṇakāravacanād apy ūhyam.


dhātoś ca hetau. Kāt_3,2.10

hetuśabdena hetukartṛvyāpāro 'rthād gamyate, dhātvarthaṃ vartayanty anye, hetukartṛvyāpāre vartamānād dhātoś cen paro bhavati sa ca kāritasaṃjñakaḥ, kurvantaṃ prayuṅkte, kārayati.
pacantaṃ prayuṅkte, pācayati.
tathā bhikṣāṃ vāsayati, kārīṣo 'dhyāpayati.

tathā kathakaḥ kaṃsaṃ ghātayati, sītāṃ hārayati, rājānam āgamati, tathā ca kiṃ gatena hataḥ kaṃsa iti lokavivakṣā.
tathā rātriṃ vivāsayati, vipūrvo vasir atikrame.
ujjayi(<-a)nyāḥ prasthito māhiṣmatyāṃ sūryam udgamayati, tathā puṣyeṇa candraṃ yojayati.


curādeś ca. Kāt_3,2.11

cur ity evam ādibhyaś cen paro bhavati, svārthe, sa ca kāritasaṃjñakaḥ, corayati, cintayati. kāritapradeśāḥ, kāritasyānām iḍ vikaraṇe [Kāt_3,6.44] ity evam ādayaḥ.


ini liṅgasyānekākṣarasyāntyasvarāder lopaḥ. Kāt_3,2.12

svarāṇāṃ madhye yo 'ntyasvarādis tasyāvayavasyeti vigrahaḥ, na kṣarati, na calatīti pradhānatvād akṣaraṃ svara ucyate, ini pare liṅgasyānekākṣarasya yo 'vayavo 'ntyasvarādis tasya lopo bhavati, atihastayati, upavīṇayati.
anekākṣarasyeti kim? vācayati.
śvetāśvāśvataragāloḍitahvarakāṇām aśvataretakalopaś ceti gaṇakāravacanād eva, śvetāśvam ācaṣṭe, śvetayati.
aśvataram ācaṣṭe, aśvayati.
gāloḍitam ācaṣṭe, gāloḍayati.
hvarakam ācaṣṭe, hvarayati.
tadvad iṣṭh(<-ṭ)emeyaḥsu bahulam, paṭiṣṭhaḥ, paṭimā, paṭīyān.
mantuvantuvīṇāṃ luk ceti gaṇe, īṇmantam ācaṣṭe, īśayati, srugvantam ācaṣṭe, srucayati, sragviṇam ācaṣṭe, srajayati.


raśabda ṛto laghor vyañjanādeḥ. Kāt_3,2.13

vyañjanāder liṅgasyānekākṣarasya ṛto lagho raśabdādeśo bhavati, ini pare, pṛthu prathayati, mṛdu mradayati, dṛḍha draḍhayati, kṛśa kraśayati, bhṛśa bhraśayati, parivṛḍha parivraḍhayati, eṣām evābhidhānam.


dhātor yaśabdaś cekrīyitaṃ kriyāsamabhihāre. Kāt_3,2.14

kriyāyāḥ samabhihāraḥ paunaḥpunyaṃ bhṛśārtho vā, kriyāsamabhihāre vartamānād dhātor vyañjanāder yaśabdaḥ paro bhavati, sa ca cekrīyi(<-a)tasaṃjñakaḥ, punaḥ punaḥ pacati, pāpacyate, bhṛśaṃ jvalayati, jājvalyate.
pākādīnāṃ pradhānakriyāṇāṃ paunaḥpunyaṃ pradhānakriyopakārakāṇām adhiśrayaṇādīnāṃ ca bhṛśatā phalātireko vā, vyavasthitavādhikārād ekasvarāt, tena punaḥ punar jāgarti.
ṛprabhṛtibhyaś ca, arāryate, aṭāṭyate, aśa bhojane, aśāśyate, prorṇonūyate, sosūcyate, momūtryate.
śubhirucibhyāṃ na syāt, bhṛśaṃ śobhate, bhṛśaṃ rocate.
gatyarthāt kauṭilya eva, bhṛśaṃ punaḥ punar vā kuṭilaṃ krāmati, caṃkramyate.
lupāder garhyāt, bhṛśaṃ punaḥ punar vā garhitaṃ lumpati, lolupyate, evaṃ sāsadyate, caṃcūryate, jaṃjapyate, jaṃjabhyate, daṃdahyate, daṃdaśyate, nijegilyate.


gupūdhūpavicchipaṇipaner āya. Kāt_3,2.15

gupūprabhṛtibhya āyaḥ paro bhavati svārthe, gopāyati, dhūpāyati, vicchāyati, paṇāyati, panāyate, panisahacarita iha paṇiḥ stutyartha ity anye.
ṛter nīyaṅ vaktavyaḥ, ṛtīyate, ṅakāra ātmanepadārthaḥ, nakāro 'guṇārthaḥ.
kamer inaṅ kāritaṃ ca.
kāmayate, vyavasthitavādhikārād āyādayo 'sārvadhātuke vā bhavanti, gopāyitā, goptā, gopāyā, guptiḥ, ṛtīyitā, artitā, kāmayitā, kamitā.


te dhātavaḥ. Kāt_3,2.16

te sanādyantā dhātusaṃjñā bhavanti, jugupsate, mīmāṃsate, cikīrṣati, putrīyati, putrakāmyati, śyenāyate, upavīṇayati, pāpacyate, gopāyati, ṛtīyate, kāmayate.
dhātutvād dhātukāryam, aśuddhakriyatvād vacanam, itareṣāṃ gaṇe 'prasiddhatvāt sukhārtham.


cakāsakāsapratyayāntebhya ām parokṣāyām. Kāt_3,2.17

cakāsakāsapratyayāntebhya ām paro bhavati parokṣāyām, cakāsāṃcakāra, kāsāṃcakre, lolūyāṃcakre, cikīrṣāṃcakāra.
cakāsagrahaṇam anekasvaropalakṣaṇam.
tena daridrāṃcakāra, culumpāṃcakāra.
pratyayāntagrahaṇam ekasvarārtham apīti matam, tena svam ivācacāra, svāṃcakāra.


dayayāsaś ca. Kāt_3,2.18

daya, aya, āsa, ebhya ām paro bhavati parokṣāyāṃ parabhūtāyām, dayāṃcakre, palāyāṃcakre, āsāṃcakre.


nāmyāder gurumato 'nṛchaḥ. Kāt_3,2.19

nāmyāder gurumato dhātor ṛchavarjitād ām paro bhavati parokṣāyāṃ parataḥ, īhāṃcakre, ubjāṃcakāra, uñchāṃcakāra.
katham iyeṣa, uvoṣa, dhātusaṃjñāto nityaṃ gurumān.
anṛcha iti kim? ānarccha.
vyavasthitavādhikārāt prorṇunāva.

dvirvacanam anabhyāsasyaikasvarasyādyasya. Kāt_3,3.1

dhātor avayavasyānabhyāsasyaikasvarasyādyasya dvirvacanaṃ bhavatīty adhikṛtaṃ veditavyam, papāca, juhoti.
vacanagrahaṇaṃ dve rūpe bhavata iti sthānitvāśaṅkānirāsārtham, tena jaghāṃsati, āṭiṭat, ghatvakāritalopapratipattigauravaṃ syāt.

ekasvarasyeti bahu(<-ū)vrīhiḥ kim? vyañjanena saha dvirvacanārtham, tena didaridrāsati.

tathā, hā priyā me gatagatā naṣṭanaṣṭā, sati saṃbhave puṃvad bhāvo 'pi pīḍāyāṃ gamyamānāyām.
tathā, paṭupaṭuḥ, paṭupaṭvī, paṇḍitapaṇḍitaḥ, paṇḍitapaṇḍitā, sādṛśye guṇavacanasyāguṇavacanasyāpi, bhītabhītaḥ, cakitacakitaḥ.

kva cid dvitīyatṛtīyayor api, aśiśvīyiṣati, aśvīyiyiṣati.


na nabadarāḥ saṃyogādayo 'ye. Kāt_3,3.3

svarāder dhātor dvitīyasyāvayavasyaikasvarasyānabhyāsasya nabadarāḥ saṃyogādayo na dvir ucyante, na tu ye pare, undidiṣati, ubjijiṣati, aḍḍiḍiṣati, arciciṣati.
nāmadhātuṣv api, indrīyitum icchati, indidrīyiṣati, evam anye 'py anusartavyāḥ.
aya iti kim? arāryate, aryam ākhyātavān, āraryad ity api syāt.
kathaṃ prorṇonūyate, nāyaṃ ye parataḥ, svarād ādyād dvitīyo 'vayavo vacanād gamyate.


pūrvo 'bhyāsaḥ. Kāt_3,3.4

dhātor dviruktasya yaḥ pūrvaḥ so 'bhyāsasaṃjño bhavati, papāca, dehi.
abhyāsapradeśāḥ, abhyāsasyādir vyañjanam avaśeṣyam [Kāt_3,3.9] ity evam ādayaḥ.


dvayam abhyastam. Kāt_3,3.5

dhātor abhyāsa itaraś ca dvayam abhyastasaṃjñaṃ bhavati, dadati, aiyaruḥ.
dvayam iti kim? paramātrasya mā bhūt, anyathā juhūṣatīty atrābhyastasya ca [Kāt_3,4.15] ity abhyāsasya saṃprasāraṇaṃ na syāt.
abhyastapradeśāḥ, abhyastānām ākārasya [Kāt_3,4.42] ity evam ādayaḥ.


jakṣādiś ca. Kāt_3,3.6

jakṣādir anabhyasto 'py abhyastasaṃjño bhavati, jakṣati, jāgrati, daridrati, cakāsati, śāsati.
pañcaite bhāṣāyāṃ vyavasthitā iti.


caṇparokṣācekrīyitasananteṣu. Kāt_3,3.7

caṇādyanteṣu dvirvacanaṃ bhavaty adhikāravaśāt, apīpacat, aundidat, papāca, pāpacyate, prorṇonūyate, pipakṣati, aṭiṭiṣati.
antagrahaṇaṃ saṃścekrīyitayor api dvirvacanārtham, tenārthān pratīṣiṣati, aṭāṭyate.


juhotyādīnāṃ sārvadhātuke. Kāt_3,3.8

juhotyādīnāṃ sārvadhātuke pare dvirvacanaṃ bhavati, juhoti, ajuhot, juhavāni, jajanāni, jajanyāt, ajajan.
ciklidacaklasacarācaracalācalapatāpatavadāvadaghanāghanapāṭupaṭā vā, iti nāmabhūtāḥ saṃjñā rūḍhāḥ, na ca klider nāmyupadhatvāt kaḥ, klasicaricalipativadihanipāṭayatibhyo nācpratyayo dvirvacanaṃ nipātanaṃ ceti.


abhyāsasyādir vyañjanam avaśeṣyam. Kāt_3,3.9

abhyāsasyādir vyañjanam avaśeṣyaṃ rakṣaṇīyaṃ bhavati, anādir lopanīyam ity arthaḥ, śiśrāya, jaglau, baṃbhramyate.
vyañjanagrahaṇam anādivarṇamātrasya lopo mā bhūt, katham āṭatuḥ, abhyāsajāter avagataṃ śeṣyam, śeṣyaśabdo nivṛttipradhānāṃ sthitim āhety anye.


śiṭparo 'ghoṣaḥ. Kāt_3,3.10

śiṭaḥ paro 'ghoṣo 'vaśeṣyo bhavati, śiṭo lopa ity arthaḥ, cuścyota, tiṣṭheva, caskanda.
śiṭpara iti kim? papsau.
anādyartho 'yam ārambhaḥ.


dvitīyacaturthayoḥ prathamatṛtīyau. Kāt_3,3.11

abhyāsadvitīyacaturthayoḥ sthāne prathamatṛtīyau bhavataḥ, yathāsaṃkhyam āntaratamyāt, cakhāna, ciccheda, ṭiṭhakārayiṣati, tasthau, jughoṣa, paphāla, ḍuḍhauke, dadhyau, babhāra.
katham ūḍham ākhyātavān, aujaḍhat, asiddhaṃ bahiraṅgam antaraṅga ity eke.


ho jaḥ. Kāt_3,3.12

abhyāsahakārasya jakāro bhavati, jaghāna, juhoti.


kavargasya cavargaḥ. Kāt_3,3.13

abhyāsakavargasya cavargo bhavati yathāsaṃkhyam, cakāra, cakhāna, jagāma, jaghāsa, ñuṅuve.


na kavateś cekrīyite. Kāt_3,3.14

kavater abhyāsasya cavargo na bhavati cekrīyite pare, kokūyate kharaḥ. svavikaraṇanirdeśāt kautikuvatyor mā bhūt, cokūyate.


hrasvaḥ. Kāt_3,3.15

svarāntasyābhyāsasya hrasvo bhavati, tasthau, lulūṣati, ḍuḍhauke.


ṛvarṇasyākāraḥ. Kāt_3,3.16

abhyāsa ṛvarṇasya akāro bhavati, vavṛdhe, cakratuḥ.


dīrgha iṇaḥ parokṣāyām aguṇe. Kāt_3,3.17

iṇo dhātor abhyāsasya parokṣāyām aguṇe dīrgho bhavati, īyatuḥ, īyuḥ.
kṛte dvirvacana iyo bādhakaṃ yatvam iti vacanam.
aguṇa iti kim? iyayitha.


asyādeḥ sarvatra. Kāt_3,3.18

parokṣāyāṃ sarvatra guṇiny aguṇe cābhyāsasyāder asya dīrgho bhavati, āṭitha, āṭatuḥ.
asyeti kim? iyeṣa, uvoṣa.
āder iti kim? papāca.


tasmān nāgamaḥ parādir antaś cet saṃyogaḥ. Kāt_3,3.19

tasmād dīrghībhūtād abhyāsāt parādir nakārāgamo bhavati, dhātor antaś cet saṃyogaḥ syāt, parokṣāyāṃ parataḥ, ānarccha, ānarcchatuḥ, ānarcchuḥ, ānañja, ānañjatuḥ, ānañjuḥ.
tasmād iti kim? āñcha, āñchatuḥ, āñchuḥ, nāyam akāralopasya bādhako dīrghaḥ.
antaś cet saṃyoga iti kim? āṭatuḥ.


ṛkāre ca. Kāt_3,3.20

tasmād dīrghībhūtād abhyāsāt parādir nakārāgamo bhavati parokṣāyām ṛkāre ca parataḥ, ānṛdhe, ānṛdhāte, ānṛdhire.
katham ārathuḥ, nimittābhāvāt.


aśnoteś ca. Kāt_3,3.21

tasmād dīrghībhūtād abhyāsād aśnoteś ca parādir nakārāgamo bhavati, parokṣāyāṃ parataḥ, vyānaśe, vyānaśāte, vyānaśire.
svavikaraṇanirdeśād aśnāter na syāt, āśatuḥ.


bhavater aḥ. Kāt_3,3.22

bhavater abhyāsasya parokṣāyām akāro bhavati, babhūva, babhūvatuḥ, babhūvuḥ.


nijivijiviṣāṃ guṇaḥ sārvadhātuke. Kāt_3,3.23

nijyādīnām abhyāsasya sārvadhātuke guṇo bhavati, arthād ikārasya, nenekti, nenijyāt, vevekti, vevijyāt, anenek, avevek, veveṣṭi, veveṣṭu.


bhṛñhāṅmāṅām it. Kāt_3,3.24

bhṛñhāṅmāṅām abhyāsasya sārvadhātuke para id bhavati, bibharti, bibhṛyāt, jihīte, ajihīta, mimīte, amimīta.


arttipipartyoś ca. Kāt_3,3.25

anayor abhyāsasya id bhavati sārvadhātuke pare, iyartti, iyṛyāt, pipartti, pipṛyāt.
pṛthagyogo vaicitryārthaḥ.


sany avarṇasya. Kāt_3,3.26

sani pare yo 'bhyāsas tasyāvarṇasye(<-a i)d bhavati, pipakṣati, pipāsati.
sany abhyāsasyeti kim? pāpaciṣate.


uvarṇasya jāntaḥsthāpavargaparasyāvarṇe. Kāt_3,3.27

sani parato yo 'bhyāsas tasyovarṇasya jāntaḥsthāpavargaparasyāvarṇe para id bhavati, ju iti sautro 'yaṃ dhātuḥ, jijāvayiṣati.
yu, yiyāvayiṣati, yiyaviṣati.
ru, rirāvayiṣati.
lū, lilāvayiṣati.
pūñ, pipāvayiṣati, pūṅas tu, pipaviṣate.
bhū, bibhāvayiṣati.
uvarṇasyeti kim? bobhaviṣati.
vacanam idaṃ jñāpanārtham, ini yat kṛtaṃ tat sarvasthānivad iti tena juhāvayiṣatīty ādayaḥ siddhāḥ.

śrusrudrupruplucyuṅāṃ vā vaktavyam, śiśrāvayiṣati, śuśrāvayiṣati, sisrāvayiṣati, susrāvayiṣati, didrāvayiṣati, dudrāvayiṣati, p(<-v)iprāvayiṣati, puprāvayiṣati, piplāvayiṣati, puplāvayiṣati, cicyāvayiṣati, cucyāvayiṣati.


guṇaś cekrīyite. Kāt_3,3.28

cekrīyite yo 'bhyāsas tasya guṇo bhavati, cecīyate, popūyate, bebhiditā.
varṇāntatvād nāmina eva.


dīrgho 'nāgamasya. Kāt_3,3.29

cekrīyite yo 'bhyāsas tasyānāgamasya dīrgho bhavati, pāpacyate.
anāgamasyeti kim? vanīvacyate, varīvṛścyate.
anāgamasyeti vacanam abhyāsavikāreṣv apavādo notsargaṃ bādhata iti jñāpanārtham, tena mīmāṃsate.


vancisransidhvansibhransikasipatipadiskandām anto nī. Kāt_3,3.30

eṣāṃ cekrīyite yo 'bhyāsas tasyāto 'nto nīr bhavati, vanīvacyate, sanīsrasyate, danīdhvasyate, banībhrasyate, canīkasyate, panīpatyate, panīpadyate, canīskadyate.
dīrghavidhānād guṇo nāśaṅkate.


ato 'nto 'nusvāro 'nunāsikāntasya. Kāt_3,3.31

anunāsikāntasya dhātoś cekrīyite pare yo 'bhyāsas tasyāto 'nto 'nusvāro bhavati, baṃbhaṇyate, baṃbhaṇitā, yaṃyamyate, yaṃyamitā.
takāra uccāraṇārthaḥ.
pratipadoktagrahaṇāt, bābhāmyate.
punar antagrahaṇam anusvārasyāpi sthityartham.


japādīnāṃ ca. Kāt_3,3.32

japa ity evam ādīnāṃ cekrīyate yo 'bhyāsas tasyāto 'nto 'nusvāro bhavati, jaṃjapyate, jaṃjapitā, jaṃjabhyate, jaṃjabhitā.
japa, jabha, daha, danśa, bhanja, paśa, ṣaḍ ete japādayaḥ.


caraphalor uc ca parasyāsya. Kāt_3,3.33

caraphaloś cekrīyite yo 'bhyāsas tasyāto 'nto 'nusvāro bhavati, parasyāsyoś ca bhavati, caṃcūryate, caṃcuritā, paṃphulyate, paṃphulitā.


ṛmato rīḥ. Kāt_3,3.34

ṛmato dhātoś cekrīyite yo 'bhyāsas tasyāto 'nto rīr bhavati, narīnṛtyate, parīpṛcchyate.


alope samānasya sanval laghunīni caṇpare. Kāt_3,3.35

samānasaṃjñakasyālope sati laghuni dhātvakṣare 'bhyāsasya ini caṇpare sanvat kāryaṃ bhavati, apīpacat, alīlavat, aśiśravat.
alope samānasyeti kim? acakathat.
kathaṃ paṭum ākhyātavān, apīpaṭat, vṛddhau sandhyakṣaralopaḥ.
laghunīti kim? atatakṣat.
katham ajījāgarat, anekavarṇavyavadhāne 'pi laghuni syād eveti matam, at tvarādīnāṃ ca [Kāt_3,3.37] iti vacanāt.
inīti kim? acakamata.
inīti jātinirdeśāt, vāditavantaṃ prayojitavān, avīvadad vīṇāṃ parivādakeneti, inīno lope 'pi syāt.
caṇpara iti kim? riramayiṣati, dīrgho laghor mā bhūt.


dīrgho laghoḥ. Kāt_3,3.36

samānasaṃjñakasyālope sati laghvantasyābhyāsasya laghuni dhātvakṣara ini caṇpare dīrgho bhavati, apīpacat, ajūhavat.
laghor iti kim? atitrapat.


at tvarādīnāṃ ca. Kāt_3,3.37

tvarādīnām abhyāsasya laghuni dhātvakṣara ini caṇpare 'd bhavati, atatvarat, asasmarat.
tvara, smṛ, dṝ, pratha, mrada, stṛ, spaśa.
vā veṣṭiceṣṭī.
īc ca gaṇaḥ.


ito lopo 'bhyāsasya. Kāt_3,3.38

itaḥ sūtrād ārabhyābhyāsasya lopo bhavaty adhikṛtaṃ veditavyam, tena pūrvokte sanvadbhāve saty ayaṃ na syāt, amīmapat, adīdapat.
punar abhyāsagrahaṇaṃ samastalopārtham.


sani mimīmādārabhalabhaśakapatapadām is svarasya. Kāt_3,3.39

miṅādīnāṃ svarasya sani para is ādeśo bhavati, abhyāsalopaś ca, ḍumiṅ, mitsati, mīñ mīṅ vā, pramitsati, pramitsate.
mā iti meṅmāṅor api grahaṇam, pramitsate, upamitsate.
dāsaṃjñakaḥ, ditsati, dhitsati.
rabha, āripsate.
labha, ālipsate.
śakḷ śaka, śikṣati.
patḷ pitsati.
pada pitsate.
kathaṃ pipatiṣati, sanīti dvisakāro 'yaṃ nirdeśo vyaktir veti.

pratiritsatīti vaktavyam, pratipūrvo rādho hiṃsāyām iti.


āpnoter īḥ. Kāt_3,3.40

āpnoteḥ svarasya īr bhavati sani pare 'bhyāsalopaś ca, īpsati.
ṛdhijñapyor īrītau vaktavyau sani sakārādau, īrtsati, jñīpsati.


danbher ic ca. Kāt_3,3.41

danbheḥ svarasya id bhavati, cakārād īc ca, sani sakārādau, abhyāsalopaś ca, dhipsati, dhīpsati.

muco 'karmakasyaud vā vaktavyaḥ, mokṣate vatsaḥ svayam eva, mumukṣate vatsaḥ svayam eva, ānukūlyāt karmakartṛtvam.


digi dayateḥ parokṣāyām. Kāt_3,3.42

deṅaḥ parokṣāyāṃ digy ādeśo bhavati, abhyāsalopaś ca, tipā dhātur eva nirdiśyate, digye, digyāte, digyire.
daya dāna ity asyāmā vyavadhānāt, dayāṃcakre.


iti daurgasiṃhyāṃ vṛttāv ākhyāte tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ samāptaḥ.



saparasvarāyāḥ saṃprasāraṇam antaḥsthāyāḥ. Kāt_3,4.1

saha pareṇa dhātusvareṇāntaḥsthāyāḥ saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavaty adhikṛtaṃ veditavyam, pareṇaiva sasvaratvaṃ lokataḥ siddham, paragrahaṇaṃ spaṣṭārtham, saṃprasāraṇaṃ yvṛto 'ntaḥsthānimittā nityatvena sthitā anvākhyāsyante.
antaḥsthāgrahaṇam abhyāsavikārabādhanārtham, tena vivyathe, vivyādhe, ity ādīnāṃ yasyābhyāse saṃprasāraṇaṃ siddham.


grahijyāvayivyadhivaṣṭivyacipracchivraścibhrasjīnām aguṇe. Kāt_3,4.2

grahyādīnām antaḥsthāyāḥ saparasvarāyāḥ saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavati, aguṇe pratyaye pare, gṛhyate, gṛhṇāti.
jīyate, jināti.
ūyatuḥ, ūyuḥ, na vāśvyor aguṇe ca [Kāt_3,4.6] iti pratiṣedhabādhanārthaṃ veño vayir ucyate.
vidhyate, vidhyati.
ūśuḥ, uśanti.
vicyate, vicati, kuṭāditvād aguṇatvam, katham uruvyacāḥ, asun auṇādikatvāt. pṛcchyate, pṛcchati, kathaṃ praśnaḥ, praśnākhyānayoḥ [Kāt_4,5.90] iti vacanāt.
vṛścyate, vṛścati.
bhṛjjyate, bhṛjjati.
aguṇa iti kim? grahītā.


svapivaciyajādīnāṃ yaṇparokṣāśīḥṣu. Kāt_3,4.3

svapivacyor yajādīnām antaḥsthāyāḥ saparasvarāyāḥ saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavati, yaṇi parokṣāyām āśiṣi cāguṇe parataḥ, supyate, suṣupatuḥ, supyāt.
ucyate, ūcatuḥ, ucyāt.
ijyate, ījatuḥ, ijyāt.

yajo vapo vahaś caiva veñvyeñau hvayatis tathā,
vadvasau śvayatiś caiva nava yajādayaḥ smṛtāḥ.


parokṣāyām abhyāsasyobhayeṣām. Kāt_3,4.4

ubhayeṣāṃ grahādisvapādīnām abhyāsasyāntaḥsthāyāḥ saparasvarāyāḥ saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavati, parokṣāyāṃ parataḥ, guṇyartho 'yam, jagrāha, jagrahitha, jijyau, jijyitha, uvāya, uvayitha.
svapādīnāṃ ca, suṣvāpa, suṣvapitha, uvāca, uvacitha, iyāja, iyajitha.
parokṣāyām iti kim? vivakṣati, vāvacyate.


vyatheś ca. Kāt_3,4.5

vyather abhyāsasyāntaḥsthāyāḥ saparasvarāyāḥ saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavati parokṣāyāṃ parataḥ, vivyathe, vivyathāte, vivyathire.
parokṣāyām iti kim? vāvyathyate.


na vāśvyor aguṇe ca. Kāt_3,4.6

veñ, śvi, ity etayor abhyāsasyāntaḥsthāyāḥ saparasvarāyāḥ saṃprasāraṇaṃ na bhavati, parokṣāyām aguṇe guṇini ca, vavau, vavitha, vavatuḥ, vavuḥ, śiśvāya, śiśvayitha, śiśviyatuḥ, śiśviyuḥ.
aguṇa iti vacanād veño 'nabhyāso 'pi gṛhyate.
śvayater vā [Kāt_3,4.12] iti parasya vibhāṣāsty eva.


svapisyamivyeñāṃ cekrīyite. Kāt_3,4.7

svapisyamivyeñām aprāptaṃ saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavati cekrīyite pare, soṣupyate, sesimyate, vevīyate.


svāpeś caṇi. Kāt_3,4.8

svāper inantasya caṇi parataḥ saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavati, asūṣupat.
svāper inantasyeti kim? svāpam akarot, asuṣupat.


grahisvapipracchāṃ sani. Kāt_3,4.9

eṣāṃ sani pare saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavati, jighṛkṣati, suṣupsati, pipṛcchiṣati.


cāyaḥ kiś cekrīyite. Kāt_3,4.10

cāyaś cekrīyite pare kir bhavati, cekīyate.


pyāyaḥ piḥ parokṣāyām. Kāt_3,4.11

pyāyaś cekrīyite pare parokṣāyāṃ ca pir bhavati, pepīyate, āpipye, āpipyāte, āpipyire.


śvayater vā. Kāt_3,4.12

śvayateś cekrīyite pare parokṣāyāṃ ca saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavati vā, śośūyate, śeśvīyate, śuśāva, śuśuvatuḥ, śiśvāya, śiśviyatuḥ.


kārite ca saṃścaṇoḥ. Kāt_3,4.13

śvayateḥ saṃścaṇor yat kāritaṃ tasmin saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavati vā, śuśāvayiṣati, śiśvāyayiṣati, aśūśavat, aśiśvayat.
ini kṛtasya sthānivadbhāvāc chudvirvacanam.


hvayater nityam. Kāt_3,4.14

hvayateḥ saṃścaṇor yat kāritaṃ tasmin nityaṃ saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavati, juhāvayiṣati, ajūhavat.
dvirvacananimitte kāritavyavadhāna eva yathā syād iti vacan, hvāyakayitum icchati, jihvāyakayiṣati, ajahvāyakat, iti.


abhyastasya ca. Kāt_3,4.15

hvayater abhyastamātrasyāntaḥsthāyāḥ saparasvarāyāḥ saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavati, juhāva, johūyate, juhūṣati.


dyutisvāpyor abhyāsasya. Kāt_3,4.16

dyutisvāpyor abhyāsasya saṃprasāraṇaṃ bhavati, didyute, didyutyate, didyotiṣate, adidyutat, suṣvāpayiṣati.
svāper inantasya grahaṇād na ghañādau, tena siṣvāpayiṣati(<-siāṣvaº).


na saṃprasāraṇe. Kāt_3,4.17

saṃprasāraṇe kṛte punaḥ saṃprasāraṇaṃ na bhavati, vidhyate, vevidhyate, vivyathe, vividhatuḥ, vividhuḥ, saṃvivyatuḥ, saṃvivyuḥ.
ekadeśavikṛtasyānanyavadbhāvād vyaktau jātau ca vacanam.


vaśeś cekrīyite. Kāt_3,4.18

vaśeś cekrīyite pare saṃprasāraṇaṃ na bhavati, vāvaśyate.


pracchādīnāṃ parokṣāyām. Kāt_3,4.19

pracchivraścibhrasjīnāṃ parokṣāyāṃ saṃprasāraṇaṃ na bhavati, papracchatuḥ, papracchuḥ, vavraścatuḥ, vavraścuḥ, babhrajjatuḥ, babhrajjuḥ.

mlai, mlātā.

smijikrīṅām ini. Kāt_3,4.24

eṣām ini para ākāro bhavati, vismāpayate, jāpayati, krāpayati, adhyāpayati.

jṝṣ, jarayati.

ici vā. Kāt_3,4.66

mānubandhānāṃ dhātūnāṃ kārita ici pare hrasvo bhavati vā, aghaṭi, aghāṭi, avyathi, avyāthi.
kṣaji gatau dāne ca, dakṣa hiṃsāyām iti ghaṭādipāṭhabalād anupadhāyā api dīrghatvam, tena akṣañji, akṣāñji.
adakṣi, adākṣi.


janibadhyoś ca. Kāt_3,4.67

ijmātram iha vartate, janibadhyor ici pare nityaṃ hrasvo bhavati, ajani, abadhi.
yady api bandhane badhis tathāpīci hiṃsāyām, tathā ca bhakṣakaś cen nāsti badhako 'pi na vidyate.
vadhiḥ prakṛtyantaram ity eke.


oto yin-āyī svaravat. Kāt_3,4.68

otaḥ parau yin-āyī svaravad bhavataḥ, gavyati, gavyate.
avo 'pi na syāt, gavājinavad iṣṭatvāt.


autaś ca. Kāt_3,4.69

autaḥ parau yin-āyī svaravad bhavataḥ, nāvyati, nāvyate, yathāsaṃkhyabhayāt pṛthag ucyate.


nāmyantānāṃ yaṇ-āyiyin-āśīścvicekrīyiteṣu ye dīrghaḥ. Kāt_3,4.70

nāmyantānāṃ dhātūnāṃ yaṇādiṣu ye cvau ca parata āntaratamyād dīrgho bhavati, cīyate, mantūyati, agnīyate, paṭūyati, cīyāt.
cvau ca, paṭūkaroti.
cecīyate.
ya iti kim? kṛṣīṣṭa, nāmīti saṃbhavadarśanārtham idam.


iṇo 'nupasṛṣṭasya. Kāt_3,4.71

iṇo dhātor anupasṛṣṭasyaivāśiṣi ye dīrgho bhavati.
īyāt, īyāstām.
anupasṛṣṭasyeti kim? anviyāt.
yaṇo vyavahitapāṭhān nehānuvṛttir iti gamyate, tena samīyate, niyamo na syāt.


ṛta īdantaś cvicekrīyitayin-āyiṣu. Kāt_3,4.72

ṛdantasya cvicekrīyitayin-āyiṣu parata īdanto bhavati, mātrīkaroti, jehīyate, svasrīyati, duhitrīyate.
ṛta iti kim? cekīryate.


ir any aguṇe. Kāt_3,4.73

ṛdantasyāni vikaraṇe 'guṇa ikāro bhavati, ādriyate, ādhriyate.
ṛta iti kim? kirati, girati.
aguṇa iti kim? smarati, ādeśād āgamo vidhir balavān iti.


yaṇāśiṣor ye. Kāt_3,4.74

ṛdantasya yaṇāśiṣor ye para ikāro 'nto bhavati, kriyate, kriyāt.
ya iti kim? kṛṣīṣṭa.


guṇo 'rtisaṃyogādyoḥ. Kāt_3,4.75

arteḥ saṃyogādeś ca dhātor yaṇāśiṣor ye pare guṇo bhavati, aryate, aryāt, smaryate, smaryāt.
asiddhaṃ bahiraṅgam antaraṅga iti saṃskriyate, saṃskriyāt.


cekrīyite ca. Kāt_3,4.76

arteḥ saṃyogādeś ca dhātoś cekrīyite(<-cekrīyate) pare guṇo bhavati, arāryate, sāsmaryate.


ghrādhmor ī. Kāt_3,4.77

ghrā, dhmā, ity etayoś cekrīyite para īkāro bhavati, jeghrīyate, dedhmīyate.
hanter ghnīr vā vaktavyam, jeghnīyate, jaṃghanyate.


yiny avarṇasya. Kāt_3,4.78

yini pare 'varṇasya īkāro bhavati, vastrīyati, mālīyati.
cvau ca, dīrghībhavati, mālīsyāt.

aśanāyodanyadhanāyā bubhukṣāpipāsākāṅkṣāsu nipātā rūḍhāḥ, aśanam icchati bhoktum, aśanāyati.
udakam icchati pātum, udanyati.
dhanam icchati tṛṣṇak, dhanāyati.


ader ghasḷ sanadyatanyoḥ. Kāt_3,4.79

adeḥ sthāne sanadyatanyoḥ parato ghasḷr ādeśo bhavati, ḷd aṇarthaḥ, jighatsati, aghasat.


vā parokṣāyām. Kāt_3,4.80

parokṣāyāṃ parato 'der ghasḷr ādeśo bhavati vā, āda, ādatuḥ, jaghāsa, jakṣatuḥ.
ghasḷ adane, sautro 'yaṃ bhāṣāyāṃ maragviṣaya eva. 


veñaś ca vayiḥ. Kāt_3,4.81

veño dhātoḥ parokṣāyāṃ parato vayir bhavati vā, uvāya, ūyatuḥ, vavau, vavatuḥ.
ikāraḥ svarūpagrāhakaḥ.


hanter vadhir āśiṣi. Kāt_3,4.82

hanter vadhir bhavati, āśiṣi parataḥ, vadhyāt, vadhyāstām.


adyatanyāṃ ca. Kāt_3,4.83

hanter adyatanyāṃ ca parato vadhir bhavati, avadhīt, avadhiṣṭām.
anāntatvād iṭi kṛte vā dīrgho na syāt, ijnirdeśasya svarūpagrāhakatvāt.
vāśabdo vyavasthāvācīha smaryate, tenātmanepade vā, āhata, āhasātām, āvadhiṣṭa, āvadhiṣātām.


iṇo gā. Kāt_3,4.84

iṇo dhātor adyatanyāṃ gādeśo bhavati, agāt, agātām.
iṇvad iko 'pi, adhyagāt.


iṅaḥ parokṣāyām. Kāt_3,4.85

iṅaḥ parokṣāyāṃ gādeśo bhavati, adhijage, adhijagāte, adhijagire.
iṅa iti kim? iṭ gatau, udiyāya.
adyatanīkriyātipattyor vā gīr ādeśa iṣyate, adhyagīṣṭa, adhyaiṣṭa, adhyagīṣyata, adhyaiṣyata.
ini saṃścaṇor api gāyater adhyayane 'pi vṛttiḥ, adhijigāpayiṣati, adhyajīgapat.
iṅas tu, adhyāpipayiṣati, adhyāpipat.


sanīṇ-iṅor gamiḥ. Kāt_3,4.86

sani pare iṇ-iṅor gamir ādeśo bhavati, grāmaṃ jigamiṣati, vedān adhijigāṃsate.
iko 'pi, adhijigamiṣati.
gamḷ bodhane sani nābhidhīyate cet tathāyam api, arthān pratīṣiṣati.
iṭ gatau bodhane 'pi dṛśyate, gamayati, adhigamayati, gaminaiva siddham, arthān pratyāyayati, śāstram adhyāpayatīti bhavitavyam eva.


aster bhūr asārvadhātuke. Kāt_3,4.87

aster bhūr ādeśo bhavati, asārvadhātukaviṣaye, bhavitā, bhūtaḥ, bhaviṣyati, bhavyam, svarād yaḥ [Kāt_4,2.10]. tipā nirdeśaḥ kim? asitā.


bruvo vaciḥ. Kāt_3,4.88

bruvo dhātor vacir bhavati, asārvadhātukaviṣaye, vaktā, vakṣyati, vācyam, ṛvarṇavyañjanāntād ghyaṇ [Kāt_4,2.35].


cakṣiṅaḥ khyāñ. Kāt_3,4.89

cakṣiṅaḥ khyāñ ādeśo bhavati, asārvadhātukaviṣaye, ākhyātā, ākhyāsyati, ākhyāsyate, ñanubandhatvād ubhayapadam.
ākhyeyam, āt khanor ic ca [Kāt_4,2.12] iti. kathaṃ saṃcakṣyo durjano, varjanīya ity arthaḥ, nṛcakṣā rākṣasaḥ, asuna auṇādikatvāt, vicakṣaṇo vidvān lokataḥ siddhaḥ.


vā parokṣāyām. Kāt_3,4.90

cakṣiṅaḥ parokṣāyāṃ khyāñ ādeśo bhavati vā, ācakhyau, ācakhye, ācacakṣe.


ajer vī. Kāt_3,4.91

ajer vīr ādeśo bhavati, asārvadhātukaviṣaye, vivyatuḥ, vayanīyam, vītaḥ, vītavān.
vyañjanādau veti ke cit, prājitā, pravetā, prājiṣyate, praveṣyate, prājitum, pravetum.
ghañ-al-kyapsu ca na syāt, samājaḥ, udajaḥ, samajyā, prājano daṇḍaḥ, vādhikārād iyam iṣṭasiddhiḥ.


adāder lug vikaraṇasya. Kāt_3,4.92

adāder gaṇād vikaraṇasya lug bhavati, atti, hanti, juhoti, bibheti, juhutaḥ, bibhītaḥ.
luglopatvān na guṇaḥ.
vikaraṇasyeti kim? aghnan.
adādyantargaṇo juhotyādir iti.


iṇ-sthādāpibatibhūbhyaḥ sicaḥ parasmai. Kāt_3,4.93

iṇādibhyaḥ parasya sico lug bhavati parasmaipade parataḥ, agāt, adhyagāt, asthāt, adāt, adhāt, apāt, abhūt.
pibater iti kim? pā rakṣaṇe, apāsīt.
parasmā iti kim? samasthiṣata, adiṣata.

ghrāśāchāsādheṭāṃ vā vaktavyam, aghrāt, aghrāsīt, aśāt, aśāsīt, acchāt, acchāsīt, asāt, asāsīt, adhāt, adhāsīt.

iti daurgasiṃhyāṃ vṛttāv ākhyāte caturthaḥ pādaḥ samāptaḥ.



nāmyantayor dhātuvikaraṇayor guṇaḥ. Kāt_3,5.1

nāmyantayor dhātuvikaraṇayor antaratamo guṇo bhavati, arthāt pratyaye pare, etā, cetā, netā, stotā, kartā, bhavitā, sunoti, tanoti.
nāmyantayor iti kim? umbhitā, krīṇāti.
glāyati, mlāyati, aikāropadeśabalān na guṇaḥ.
nībhyām, lūbhyām iti gauṇatvāt.


nāminaś copadhāyā laghoḥ. Kāt_3,5.2

dhātor upadhāyā nāmino laghor guṇo bhavati, koṣitā, koṣiṣyate, vartitā, vartiṣyate.
bhettā, chetteti pratyaye pare dhātor upadhaiva.
cakāra uttarārthaḥ.


ani ca vikaraṇe. Kāt_3,5.3

nāmina upadhāyā nāmyantasya cāny eva vikāraṇe guṇo bhavati, rocate, vartate, bhavati, nayati.
any eva vikaraṇa iti kim? nṛtyati, sunoti, krīṇāti, puṣāṇa. 
vikaraṇa iti kim? aduhan.


karoteḥ. Kāt_3,5.4

karoteḥ svavikaraṇe guṇo bhavaty eva, karoti, karotu.
tanādyupalakṣaṇaṃ karotir iti ke cit. tena samarṇoti.


mideḥ. Kāt_3,5.5

mideḥ svavikaraṇe guṇo bhavaty eva, medyati.
bhauvādikasya medater ani siddha eva.


abhyastānām usi. Kāt_3,5.6

abhyastānām usi pare nāmino guṇo bhavati, dvitvabahutvayoś ca parasmā iti pratiṣedhe prāpte vacanam, abibhayuḥ, ajuhavuḥ, abibharuḥ, ajāgaruḥ.
abhyastānām usīti kim? juhuvuḥ.


na ṇakārānubandhacekrīyitayoḥ. Kāt_3,5.7

nāmyantānāṃ nāmyupadhānāṃ ca ṇakārānubandhe cekrīyite ca pare guṇo na bhavati, aśiśriyat, apuṣat, aghukṣat, nīyate, duṣyate.
narīnṛtyate, lolūyate.


abhyastasya copadhāyā nāminaḥ svare guṇini sārvadhātuke. Kāt_3,5.8

abhyastasya copadhāyā nāminaḥ svarādau guṇini sārvadhātuke pare guṇo na bhavati, nenijāni, anenijam.
viśeṣanāmigrahaṇāj jajanānīty alopo na syāt, evam uttaratrāpi yojyam.
guṇinīti kim? guṇiny api guṇo mā bhūt, anenijuḥ.


sani cāniṭi. Kāt_3,5.9

nāmina upadhāyā aniṭi sani guṇo na bhavati, bibhitsati, ditsā, bubhukṣate, jighṛkṣati.
cakārād anāmino 'pi kva cit, tena dhīpsati, nalopaḥ syāt.
aniṭīti kim? cukoṣiṣati.


sijāśiṣoś cātmane. Kāt_3,5.10

nāmina upadhāyāḥ sicy ātmanepada āśiṣi cāniṭi guṇo na bhavati, abhitta, acchitta, abhitsātām, aduhvahi, adugdha, adugdhāḥ, duhadihalihaguhām ātmane vatavarge vā saṇ eva tatra vyavasthitavānuvṛtteḥ sico 'dyatanyupalakṣaṇatvāt siddham.
bhitsīṣṭa, bhukṣīṣṭa.
aniṭīti kim? avardhiṣṭa, vardhiṣīṣṭa.
ihātmanegrahaṇaṃ guṇabādhikā vṛddhir iti jñāpanārtham, tena nyanuvīt, nyadhuvīt, kuṭāditvād aguṇe vṛddhir na syāt.


ṛdantānāṃ ca. Kāt_3,5.11

ṛdantānāṃ ca dhātūnāṃ sijāśiṣoś cātmanepade 'niṭi guṇo na bhavati, akṛta, akṛṣātām, kṛṣīṣṭa. 
aniṭīti kim? prāvariṣṭa, pravariṣīṣṭa.
kathaṃ tṝ, atīrṣṭa, tīrṣīṣṭa, stṝ, astīrṣṭa, stīrṣīṣṭa, pṝ, apūrṣṭa, pūrṣīṣṭa, sijāśiṣoś cātmana iḍvikalpeṣṭir ity ṛkārasyopalakṣaṇatvāt.


sthādoś ca. Kāt_3,5.12

sthādāsaṃjñakayoś ca nāminaḥ sicy ātmanepade guṇo na bhavati, samasthiṣata, samasthiṣātām, adita, adiṣātām, adhita, adhiṣātām.
nāmina iti kim? sthāsīṣṭa, dāsīṣṭa.


bhuvaḥ sij-luki. Kāt_3,5.13

bhuvo dhātoḥ sijluki sati guṇo na bhavati, abhūt, abhūtām.
bhuva iti kim? asthāt.
sijlukīti vacanān nāmino nivṛttir veti śaṅkyate.


sūteḥ pañcamyām. Kāt_3,5.14

sūteḥ pañcamyuttame guṇo na bhavati, sūṅ, suvai, suvāvahai, suvāmahai.


dīdhīvevyoś ca. Kāt_3,5.15

chāndasāv etau dhātū ity eke, pañcamyām iti nehānuvṛttiḥ pṛthagyogāt, dīdhīvevyoś ca guṇo na bhavati, ādīdhyai, āvevyai, ādīdhyanam, āvevyanam, ādīdhyakaḥ, āvevyakaḥ.


rudavidamuṣāṃ sani. Kāt_3,5.16

rudādīnāṃ sani guṇo na bhavati, rurudiṣati, vividiṣati, mumuṣiṣati.
pāriśeṣyād vidir jñānārthaḥ.
sani vyañjanāder vyupadhatvād vikalpeṣṭau vacanaṃ nityā(<-a)rtham.


nāmyantānām aniṭām. Kāt_3,5.17

nāmyantānāṃ dhātūnām aniṭāṃ sani guṇo na bhavati, cicīṣati, ninīṣati, tuṣṭūṣati, lulūṣati, cikīrṣati, bubhūrṣati.
aniṭām iti kim? śiśrayiṣati.
jñīpsatīti nityatvāt kāritalopaḥ syāt.

dīrghāṇāṃ ca kṛto dīrgho guṇaṃ bādheta cet tadā,
dīrghajāv irurau nāma inā lopas tu durlabhaḥ. 


sarveṣām ātmane sārvadhātuke 'nuttame pañcamyāḥ. Kāt_3,5.18

sarveṣāṃ dhātūnāṃ vikaraṇānāṃ ca nāmina upadhāyā nāmyantasya ca sārvadhātuke pañcamyuttamavarjita ātmanepade guṇo na bhavati, dugdhe, stute, cinute, kurute.
sārvadhātuka iti kim? dhokṣyate, stoṣyate.
anuttame pañcamyā iti kim? stavai, karavai.


dvitvabahutvayoś ca parasmai. Kāt_3,5.19

sarveṣāṃ dhātūnāṃ vikaraṇānāṃ ca s(<-c)ārvadhātuke pañcamyuttamavarjite dvitvabahutvayoś ca parasmaipade guṇo na bhavati, dugdhaḥ, duhanti, stutaḥ, stuvanti, cinutaḥ, cinvanti, kurutaḥ, kurvanti.
dvitvabahutvayor iti kim? dogdhi, stauti, karoti, cinoti.
anuttame pañcamyā iti kim? dohāva, dohāma, cinavāva, cinavāma.


parokṣāyāṃ ca. Kāt_3,5.20

sarveṣāṃ dhātūnāṃ parokṣāyāṃ ca dvitvabahutvayoś ca parasmaipade guṇo na bhavati, duduhatuḥ, duduhuḥ, vivyatuḥ, vivyuḥ.
dvitvabahutvayor iti kim? dudoha, ninayitha.


sarvatrātmane. Kāt_3,5.21

sarveṣāṃ dhātūnāṃ parokṣāyāṃ ca sarvasminn ātmanepade guṇo na bhavati, duduhe, duduhāte, duduhire, cakre, cakrāte, cakrire.


āśiṣi ca parasmai. Kāt_3,5.22

sarveṣāṃ dhātūnāṃ sarvatrāśiṣi parasmaipade guṇo na bhavati, cīyāt, cīyāstām, duhyāt, duhyāstām.
parasmā iti kim? ceṣīṣṭa, dhoṣīṣṭa.


saptamyāṃ ca. Kāt_3,5.23

sarveṣāṃ dhātūnāṃ saptamyāṃ ca parasmaipade guṇo na bhavati, stuyāt, cinuyāt, duhyāt.


hau ca. Kāt_3,5.24

sarveṣāṃ dhātūnāṃ hau pare guṇo na bhavati, nuhi, dugdhi, prāpnuhi, cinu, sunu, pratyayalopalakṣaṇatvāt.
katham ehi, āṅa etvam iti.


tudāder ani. Kāt_3,5.25

tudāder ani guṇo na bhavati, tudati, nudati.


āmi vider eva. Kāt_3,5.26

vider evāmi pare guṇo na bhavati, vida jñāne, vidāñcakāra.
vider eveti kim? oṣāñcakāra, jāgarāñcakāra.


kuṭāder aninicaṭsu. Kāt_3,5.27

kuṭāder gaṇasya inicaṭo varjayitvānyeṣu pratyayeṣu guṇo na bhavati, utkuṭitā, utkuṭitum, utkuṭiṣyati, utpuṭitā, utpuṭitum, utpuṭiṣyati.
kuṭāder iti kim? lekhanīyam.
aninicaṭsv iti kim? utkoṭayati, udakoṭi, uccukoṭa.
kathaṃ pṛcchanīyam, rūḍhitvāt.


vijer iṭi. Kāt_3,5.28

vijer iṭi pare guṇo na bhavati, ovijī, udvijitā, udvijitum, udvijiṣyate.
katham udvejitā, inā siddham.


sthādor ir adyatanyām ātmane. Kāt_3,5.29

sthādāsaṃjñakayor adyatanyām ātmanepada ir bhavati, samasthita, samasthiṣātām, adita, adiṣātām, adhita, adhiṣātām.
ātmana iti kim? asthāt, adāt, adhāt.


mucāder āgamo nakāraḥ svarād ani vikaraṇe. Kāt_3,5.30

mucāder gaṇasya svarāt paro nakārāgamo bhavati, ani vikaraṇe pare, muñcati, lumpati.
vikaraṇa iti kim? amucan.


masjinaśor dhuṭi. Kāt_3,5.31

masjinaśoḥ svarāt paro nakārāgamo bhavati dhuṭi pare, maṅktā, maṅkṣyati, naṃṣṭā, naṅkṣyati.


radhijabhoḥ svare. Kāt_3,5.32

radhijabhoḥ svarāt paro nakārāgamo bhavati svare pare, randhayati, arandhi, jambhayati, ajambhi.


neṭi radher aparokṣāyām. Kāt_3,5.33

radher iṭi pare nakārāgamo na bhavati, aparokṣāyām, radhitā, radhiṣyati, radhitavyam. aparokṣāyām iti kim? rarandhiva, rarandhima.


rabhilabhor avikaraṇaparokṣayoḥ. Kāt_3,5.34

rabhilabhoḥ svarāt paro nakārāgamo bhavati, avikaraṇaparokṣayoḥ svare pare, ārambhayati, ārambhi, ārambho vartate, ālambhayati, ālambhi.
avikaraṇaparokṣayor <ar> iti kim? ārabhate, ālabhate, rebhe, lebhe.


hudhuḍbhyāṃ her dhiḥ. Kāt_3,5.35

hudhuḍbhyāṃ parasya her dhir bhavati, juhudhi, cakāddhi, bhinddhi, chinddhi.
bhinttāt, chinttāt, paratvāt tātaṇ.
bhinddhaki, chinddhaki, paścād ak.
kathaṃ rudihi, svapihi, seṭkatvāt.


asteḥ. Kāt_3,5.36

asteḥ parasya her dhir bhavati, asa, edhi, nityatvād antaraṅgatvād etve sati vacanam.


śā śāsteś ca. Kāt_3,5.37

śāsteḥ parasya her dhir bhavati, śāsteś ca śā bhavati, śādhi.
ac ceti kṛta itvaṃ syāt.


lopo 'bhyastād antinaḥ. Kāt_3,5.38

abhyastāt parasyānter nakārasya lopo bhavati, dadati, dadatu, jāgrati, jāgratu.
nalopaḥ sādhya ity anukṛtaḥ.


ātmane cānakārāt. Kāt_3,5.39

anakārāc cātmanepade 'nter nakārasya lopo bhavati, kurvate, kurvatām, lunate, lunatām, vyatilāte, vyatilātām.
anakārād iti kim? pacante, pacyante.


śete rir anter ādiḥ. Kāt_3,5.40

śeteḥ parasyānter ādi rir bhavati, śerate, śeratām, aśerata.
antigrahaṇam antino rir ādir mā bhūt.

vetter vā vaktavyam, saṃvidate, saṃvidrate.


ākārād aṭ au. Kāt_3,5.41

ākārāt parasya aṭa aur bhavati, papau, tasthau.

āśiṣi tuhyos tātaṇ vā vaktavyam, jīvatu, jīvatāt, jīva tvam, nandatu, nandatāt, nanda tvam, chinttāt, kurutāt.
ṇakār(<-t)o 'guṇārthaḥ.


ṝdantasyer aguṇe. Kāt_3,5.42

ṝdantasya dhātoḥ śrutasya sthānino 'ntaratamo 'guṇe pratyaye para ī(<-i)r bhavati, cikīrṣati, jihīrṣati, titīrṣati.
ṝdantasyeti kim? cakratuḥ.
kīrtīṣoḥ ktiś ca [Kāt_4,5.86] iti nirdeśāt, kīrtayati.

anidanubandhānām aguṇe 'nuṣaṅgalopaḥ. Kāt_3,6.1

anidanubandhānāṃ dhātūnām aguṇe pratyaye pare 'nuṣaṅgalopo bhavati, śrasyate, dhvasyate, naṣṭaḥ, naṣṭavān.
anidanubandhānām iti kim? śaṅkyate, vaṅkyate, ata eva varjanād idanubandhānāṃ no 'stīti.
tathā ca vṛṃhaṇam iti svarāntatvān natvaṃ syāt, nañā nirdiṣṭasyānityāt.

laṅgikampyor upatāpaśarīravikārayoḥ syāt, vilagitaḥ, vikapitaḥ.

tṛnphādīnāṃ śunphāntānām ani na ca lupyate, tṛpha tṛnpha tṛptau, tṛmphatīty ādi.


naśabdāc ca vikaraṇāt. Kāt_3,6.2

parokṣāyām indhiśranthigranthidanbhīnām aguṇe. Kāt_3,6.3

indhyādīnāṃ parokṣāyām aguṇe parato 'nuṣaṅgasya lopo bhavati, samīdhe, samīdhāte, samīdhire, vacanād ām nāsti. śrethtuḥ, grethatuḥ, debhatuḥ.
indhyādīnām eveti niyamāt, śaśraṃse, babhañjatuḥ.


danśisanjisvanjiranjīnām ani. Kāt_3,6.4

danśyādīnām ani vikaraṇe 'nuṣaṅgasya lopo bhavati, daśati, sajati, pariṣvajate, rajati.

danśa daśana iti nirdeśāt, daśanam.

asyopadhāyā dīrgho vṛddhir nāminām inicaṭsu. Kāt_3,6.5

dhātor upadhāyā asya dīrgho bhavati, nāmināṃ ca vṛddhir bhavati, in, ic, aṭ, eṣu parataḥ, pācayati, apāci, papāca, lāvayati, alāvi, lulāva, nāyayati, anāyi, nināya, kārayati, akāri, cakāra.
dhātor iti kim? tvacayati.
kathaṃ paṭum ākhyātavān, apīpaṭat, vṛddhau sandhyakṣaralopaḥ, dhātor nāmino guṇe saty upadhāyā dīrghaḥ siddhaḥ.
nāmigrahaṇaṃ liṅgārtham eva bahuvacanaṃ vā.
katham acakalat, ajahalat, saṃjñāpūrvakatvād vṛddhir anityeti samānalopatvāt sanvadbhāvo na syāt.
tathā, aṭy uttame vā, ahaṃ papaca, ahaṃ papāca, ahaṃ ninaya, ahaṃ nināya, ahaṃ lulava, ahaṃ lulāva, ahaṃ cakara, ahaṃ cakāra.


sici parasmai svarāntānām. Kāt_3,6.6

arthāt svarāntagrahaṇam upadeśārthaṃ tena, udavoḍhām.
sicīti kim? navāva.
parasmā iti kim? acyoṣṭa.

ūrṇoter vā, praurṇāvīt, praurṇavīt.

asya ca dīrghaḥ. Kāt_3,6.8

vadavrajaralantānām. Kāt_3,6.9

āmiḍvikaraṇād anyasmin pratyaye kāritasya lopo bhavati, acīkarat, acīkamata, ararakṣat, kāryate, kāraṇā, udapādi, yatvādayo bādhyante.

yasyāpatyapratyayasyāsvarapūrvasya yin-āyiṣu. Kāt_3,6.45

yin-āyī dvau bahuvacanaṃ gaṇārtham, yasyety akāra uccāraṇārthaḥ, apatyapratyayasaṃbandhino yasyāsvarapūrvasya yin-āyitaddhitānātsvaracvistrīkāreṣu lopo bhavati, gārgīyati, gārgīyate, gārgye sādhurgārgya iti śruterabhedāt, kurornakārādeśca rūḍhādapatyamātre gargāditvād ṇyaḥ, kauravyasyāpatyamitīn kauraviḥ, naiṣādiḥ, gārgyasyāyaṃ gārgīyaḥ, gārgāṇāṃ samūho gārgakam, samūhe 'kaṇ, kathaṃ rājanyakam, gaṇakṛtamanityamiti gārgī syāt, gārgī strīgaṇe.
anātsvara iti kim? gārgyāyaṇaḥ.
yin-āyīṣviti nyāyyaḥ pāṭhaḥ, taddhitānām ākṛtipradhānatvāt, tathā ca somo devatā 'syāḥ saumī ṛk ca dṛśyate.
asvarapūrvasyeti kim? ātreyīyati, ātreyāyate, ātreyīsyāt, ātreyī strī.

matsyasya yasya strīkāra īye cāgastyasūryayoḥ,
tiṣyapuṣyayornakṣatre ani yasya vibhañjanāt.

matsī, agastyasyāpatyamityaṇ, āgastyasyāyam āgastīyaḥ, āgastyasyeyam āgastī, sūryasyāyaṃ sauryaḥ, tatra bhavaḥ saurīyaḥ, sūryasyeyaṃ sauro dik, taiṣamahaḥ, taiṣī rātriḥ, pauṣamahaḥ, pauṣī rātriḥ, gaṇātpṛthagāyiruttarārthaḥ.


nalopaś ca. Kāt_3,6.46

nakāro lupyate yena sa nalopo yogaḥ, arthād yin-āyyor nalopa eva karaṇīyaḥ, viduṣyati, viduṣyate, evaṃ rājīyati, pathīyati.
puṃsyatītyapi.
niyamaḥ kim, dīvyatītyapi.
kathaṃ caturyati, anuḍuhyati, gīryati, dhūryati, śabdāśrayatvādviniyamaḥ.
sarpiṣyati, dhanuṣyati, ṣatvaṃ syādeva.
gomatyatīti kvip, kathaṃ gomān, pacan, pumān, yin-āyyordhuṭi pratyayalopasyānityatvādudanubandhaśantṛṅpuṃsāmeveti.


vyañjanād disyoḥ. Kāt_3,6.47

dhātor vyañjanād disyor lopo bhavati, adhok, aleṭ.
kathaṃ haṃsi, sāhacaryāt.


yasyānani. Kāt_3,6.48

yasyety akāra uccāraṇārthaḥ, vyañjanāt parasya dhātor yasyānani pratyaye pare lopo bhavati, bebhiditā.
dṛśadam icchaty ācarati vā, dṛśaditā.
bhiṣajyadhātuḥ kaṇḍūyādau, bhiṣajitā.
yin-āyyornecchantyeke, tenobhayapramāṇatvād vikalpa iti vakṣyamāṇalopokterdviyakārapāṭhādvā mavyādīnāmadoṣaḥ, mavyitā, sūrkṣyitā, īrṣyitā.
vyañjanāditi kim? lolūyitā, ino lope 'yādeśe ca, momūtritā, śāśayitā.
dhātoryasyeti kim? pacyate.
ananīti kim? pāpacyate.


asya ca lopaḥ. Kāt_3,6.49

dhātor akārasyānani pratyaye pare lopo bhavati, cikīrṣitā.
kusubhaṃ magadhaṃ kartā, kusubhitā, magadhitā.
viṣayamaptamyapi, kaṇḍūḥ, lolūḥ, yāyāvaraḥ, tenāsya ca lope yalopaḥ syāt.


sico dhakāre. Kāt_3,6.50

sico dhakāre pare lopo bhavati, alaviḍhvam, acyoḍhvam.
ayandhvam iti sasya tṛtīye 'pi dhva uccāraṇasyābhedāt.


dhuṭaś ca dhuṭi. Kāt_3,6.51

dhuṭaḥ parasya sico lopo bhavati, dhuṭi pare, abhitta, abhitthāḥ.
dhuṭa iti kim? amaṃsta.
dhuṭīti kim? abhitsātām.


hrasvāc cāniṭaḥ. Kāt_3,6.52

hrasvāt parasyāniṭaḥ sico lopo bhavati, dhuṭi pare, akṛta, akṛthāḥ, samasthita, āhata.
hrasvād iti kim? acyoṣṭa.
neṭaḥ parasya veti sukhārtham, tena, avāriṣṭām, vyadyotiṣṭa.


iṭaś ceṭi. Kāt_3,6.53

iṭaḥ parasya sico lopo bhavati, īṭi pare, alāvīt, akoṣīt.
iṭa iti kim? abhaitsīt.
īṭīti kim? akaniṣam.


skoḥ saṃyogādyor ante ca. Kāt_3,6.54

dhātoḥ saṃyogādyoḥ sakārakakārayor lopo bhavati dhūṭyante ca, āripsate, ālipsate, ācaṣṭe, bhraṣṭā, bhrakṣyati.
tvakṣu, tvaṣṭiḥ, ktau neṭ.
ante cetyuttarārtham, bhāṣāyām api cekrīyitalugantam ity eke, abābhraṭ.
skor iti kim? akārṣṭām, mṛja amārṭ.
dhuṭyanta iti kim? bhṛjjate, ācakṣmahe.


cavargasya kir asavarṇe. Kāt_3,6.55

cavargasya kir bhavati, asavarṇe dhuṭy ante ca.
vaktā, yoktā, anenek, avevek.
asavarṇa iti kim? uñchati, ujjhati.


ho ḍhaḥ. Kāt_3,6.56

dhātor hakārasya ḍho bhavati dhuṭy ante ca, leḍhā, lekṣyati, aleṭ.


dāder ghaḥ. Kāt_3,6.57

dhātor dāder avayavasya hasya gho bhavati dhuṭy ante ca, adhokṣyat, adhok.
kathaṃ dogdhā, ādyantavadbhāvāt.


naher dhaḥ. Kāt_3,6.58

naher hasya dho bhavati dhuṭy ante ca, naddhā, natsyati, anānat.


bhṛjādīnāṃ ṣaḥ. Kāt_3,6.59

bhṛjādīnām antaḥ ṣo bhavati dhuṭyante ca, bhraṣṭā, bhrakṣyati, sraṣṭā, srakṣyati, mārṣṭā, amārṣṭa, mārkṣyati, yaja yaṣṭā, rājṛ rāṣṭiḥ, bhrājṛ bhrāṣṭiḥ.
bhrasjer bhṛjirihopalakṣaṇam, nipātanasyeṣṭavixsayatvāt saṃprasāraṇādanyatra vibhāṣā, bhraṣṭā, bharṣṭā, bhrajjanam, bharjjanam, bharjjanam.
saṃprasāraṇe tu, bhṛjjati, bhṛjjate.


chaśoś ca. Kāt_3,6.60

chaśoś ca ṣo bhavati dhuṭy ante ca, praṣṭā, prakṣyati, kroṣṭā, krokṣyati, acokroṭ.
nimittābhāvād dvirvā pāṭhaḥ.


bhāṣitapuṃskaṃ puṃvad āyau. Kāt_3,6.61

bhāṣitapuṃskaṃ puṃvad bhavati, āyau pare, brāhmaṇīvācarati, brāhmaṇāyate, śyenī śyetāyate, hariṇī haritāyate, enī etāyate, lohinī lohitāyate, śyetaitaharitalohitebhyas to na iti nadādau.
cvyarthe tu na bhavati gauṇatvāt, alohinī lohinī bhavati, lohinīyate, ity anye.
pumāniva puṃvat strīti lokataḥ siddham, tatrādhikārabalād amukhyam api napuṃsakaṃ puṃvaditi, tenātinūyate.
bhāṣitaḥ pumānyasminnartha iti samāsāt, droṇīyate.
kathaṃ śvaśrūyate, śvaśurasya śvaśrūruṅanto nipātanāt, nāptībhāvatvaṃ śvaśuratvam api tu viśiṣṭam eva rūḍham.
kathaṃ garbhīyate śāliḥ, antarvartitvamātravivakṣayeti. 


ād ātāmāthām āder iḥ. Kāt_3,6.62

akārāt parayor ātāmātham ity etayor āder ir bhavati, pacetām, pacethām.
akārād iti kim? vyatyapātām.


āte āthe iti ca. Kāt_3,6.63

akārāt parayor āte āthe ity etayor āder ir bhavati, pacete, pacethe.
avikṛtanirdeśāt svare vikṛtirnāstīti, iti caivaṃprakāre draṣṭavyaḥ, tena pacāvahe āvām iti svare vikṛtirnāstīti, iti caivaṃprakāre draṣṭavyaḥ, tena pacāvahe āvām iti svare vikṛtinaṃ syāt.


yāśabdasya ca saptamyāḥ. Kāt_3,6.64

akārāt parasya yāśabdasya saptamyā ir bhavati, pacet, pacetām, paceḥ.

yāmyusor iyamiyusau. Kāt_3,6.65

akārāt parayor yām-yusor iyamiyusau bhavataḥ, yathāsaṃkhyam, paceyaṃ, paceyuḥ.
katham āha, āhatuḥ, āhuḥ, āttha, āhathuḥ, bruvastyādiṣu pañcasu nipātā vā.
tathā vidernavasu, veda, vidatuḥ, viduḥ, vettha, vidathuḥ, vida, veda, vidva, vidma.


śamādīnāṃ dīrgho yani. Kāt_3,6.66

śamādīnāṃ dīrgho bhavati yani pare, śāmyati, dāmyati.

ṣṭhivuklamvācamām ani. Kāt_3,6.67

kathaṃ krāma, herlopāt.
parasmā iti kim? parākramate, upakramate.


gamiṣyamāṃ chaḥ. Kāt_3,6.69

sāmānyam anuvartate, eṣām antasya cho bhavati, ani pare, gacchati, saṃgacchate, icchati, yacchati, āyacchate.


paḥ pibaḥ. Kāt_3,6.70

pādhātor ani pare pibādeśo bhavati, pibati.
adanto vā, ani pārūpasyeti kim? pai ovai, pāyati.

tiv nirdeśārtha eva.


sarter dhāvaḥ. Kāt_3,6.78

śadeḥ śīyaḥ. Kāt_3,6.79

śader ani pare śīyādeśo bhavati, śīyate.


sadeḥ sīdaḥ. Kāt_3,6.80

jā janer vikaraṇe. Kāt_3,6.81

janer vikaraṇe jādeśo bhavati, janī, jāyate.
yaṇi tu ye vā syāt, jāyate, janyate.


jñaś ca. Kāt_3,6.82

jñaś ca vikaraṇe jādeśo bhavati, jānāti.


pvādīnāṃ hrasvaḥ. Kāt_3,6.83

uto vṛddhir vyañjanādau guṇini sārvadhātuke. Kāt_3,6.84

dhātor uto vṛddhir bhavati, vyañjanādau guṇini sārvadhātuke pare, rauti, rauṣi, raumi, evaṃ nauti, stauti.

ūrṇoter guṇaḥ. Kāt_3,6.85

hyastanyāṃ ca. Kāt_3,6.86

ūrṇoter vyañjanādau guṇini hyastanyāṃ ca nityaṃ guṇo bhavati, praurṇot, praurṇoḥ.

praurṇāvīt, praurṇuvīt, ity api syāt.


tṛher iḍ vikaraṇāt. Kāt_3,6.87

prakṛtatvāt sārvadhātukam anuvartate, tṛher vikaraṇāt para iḍ āgamo bhavati, vyañjanādau guṇini sārvadhātuke pare, tṛṇeḍhi, tṛṇekṣi, tṛṇehmi.


bruva īḍ vacanādiḥ. Kāt_3,6.88

bruva īḍ bhavati vacanādir bhūtvā vyañjanādau guṇini sārvadhātuke pare, bravīti, bravītu, abravīt.

carkarītādveti kecit, bobhavīti bobhoti.


aster disyoḥ. Kāt_3,6.89

rudādibhyaś ca. Kāt_3,6.91

rudādibhyaḥ parayor disyor vacanādir īḍ bhavati, arodīt, arodīḥ, asvapīt, asvapīḥ, aśvasīt, aśvasīḥ, prāṇīt, prāṇīḥ, ajakṣīt, ajakṣīḥ, pañcaite rūdādayaḥ.


ado 'ṭ. Kāt_3,6.92

adaḥ parayor disyor vacanādir aḍ bhavati, ādat, ādaḥ.
rudāder api ke cit, arodat, arodaḥ.


sasya se 'sārvadhātuke taḥ. Kāt_3,6.93

sasya takāro bhavati, asārvadhātukaviṣaye se, jighatsati, vatsyati.
asārvadhātuka iti kim? vasse.


aṇi vacer od upadhāyāḥ. Kāt_3,6.94

vacer upadhāyā od bhavati, aṇi pare, avocat, avocaḥ.
kathaṃ pustakavācaḥ, asārvadhātuka iti viśeṣanāt, evam uttaratrāpi.


asyateḥ stho 'ntaḥ. Kāt_3,6.95

asyater antaḥ stho bhavati, aṇi pare, apāsthat.


pateḥ paptiḥ. Kāt_3,6.96

pateḥ paptir bhavati, aṇi pare, apaptat.
śverad vaktavyaḥ, aśvat.


kṛpe ro laḥ. Kāt_3,6.97

kṛpe rephasya lakāro bhavati, kalptā, kalpayati, kalpaḥ.
kathaṃ kḷptaḥ, kḷptir iti raśruterlaśrutir iti vaktavyaṃ vā, iha ṛkārasthasya rephasyāvarṇātmana ḷkārastho lakāro 'varṇātmantaratamyād bhavan, ṛkārasthasya ḷkāra eva syād avyatiriktatvāt.
kathaṃ kṛpā, lākṣaṇikatvāt, kṛpaṇādayo hyauṇādikā iti.


girateś cekrīyite. Kāt_3,6.98

girate rephasya lakāro bhavati, cekrīyate pare, garhitaṃ girati, nijegilyate.


vā svare. Kāt_3,6.99

girate rephasya latvaṃ bhavati vā svare pare, girati, gilati, nigaraṇam, nigalanam.
nigālyata itīnaḥ sthānivadbhāvāt.
galaḥ prāṇyaṅge viṣe tu gara iti.
kapirikāderlokataḥ siddhiḥ, kapirikā, kapilikā, rohiṇī, lohiṇī, roma, loma, paryaṅkaḥ, palyaṅkaḥ, parighaḥ, palighaḥ, pariyogaḥ, paliyogaḥ, cūḍā, cūlā, vaḍabhī, valabhī, jaḍam, jalam, jaḍadhiḥ, jaladhiḥ, ḍalayorekatvam.
tathopasargasyāyatau, parāyate, palāyate.
nirduror vā syāt, nirayaṇam, nilayanam, durayaṇam, dulayanam.
ativyavahite neṣṭam, pratyayate.


tutīyāder ghaḍhadhabhāntasya dhātor ādicaturthatvaṃ sadhavoḥ. Kāt_3,6.100

dhātor avayavasya tṛtīyāder ghaḍhadhabhāntasyādicaturthatvaṃ bhavati, āntaratamyāt, sakāre dhve ca parataḥ, dudhukṣati, adhugdhvam, aghukṣata, aghūdhvam, bubhutsate, abhuddhvam, dhīpsati, bhotsyate, nighokṣyate, ityādyantavadbhāvāt.
sadhvoriti kim? didambhiṣati, dugdhaḥ, dugdhavān.
punardhātugrahaṇam iha sukhārthaṃ ca.


lope ca disyoḥ. Kāt_3,6.101

dhātor avayavasya tṛtīyāder ghaḍhadhabhāntasyādeś caturthatvaṃ bhavati, disyor lope ca sati, adhok, ajoghoṭ, abobhīt.
dasyor iti kim? adhugdhāḥ, varṇāśrayatvāt pratyayalopalakṣaṇaṃ nāstīti.


t(<-s)athoś ca dadhāteḥ. Kāt_3,6.102

dadhāter dhāntasyādeś caturthatvaṃ bhavati, tathoḥ sadhvoś ca parataḥ, dhattaḥ, dhatthaḥ, dhatse, dhaddhve.
dhāntasyeti kim? dadhāti, dadhāsi.

iḍ āgamo 'sārvadhātukasyādir vyañjanāder ayakārādeḥ. Kāt_3,7.1

dhātor vihitasyāsārvadhātukasya vyañjanāder ayakārāder ādir iḍ āgamo bhavati, bhavitā, bhaviṣyati, bhavitavyam.
punar dhātvadhikāro dhātusaṃjjāśritāsārvadhātukārthaḥ, tena gṛhṇāti, vṛṇoti, jugupsate, mīmāṃsate.
asārvadhātukasyeti kim? śete, vetti.
ṭakāra iṭi ca [Kāt_3,4.28] ityādau viśeṣārthaḥ.
vyañjanāder iti kim? babhūva.
ayakārāder iti kim? bhūyāt.


snukramibhyāṃ parasmai. Kāt_3,7.2 

parasmaipadaviṣaye yau snukramī tābhyāṃ parasyāsārvadhātukasya vyañjanāderayakārāderādiriḍāgamo bhavati, prasnavitā, prasnaviṣyati, kramitā, kramiṣyati, cikramiṣati.
parasmaipadaviṣaya eveti niyamāt, vyatisnoṣyate, pracikraṃsate, upacikraṃsate, propābhyāṃ kramī rucādirādikarmaṇi.
prasnavitavyam, prakramitavyam, ityasamānaviṣayatvādiṭ.
kathaṃ prakrantā, upakrantā, ātmanepadaviṣayasya krameḥ kartari kṛtīṭpratiṣedhaḥ.
prasnavitevācarati, prasnavitrīyate, āyirayamātmanepadī.


rudādeḥ sārvadhātuke. Kāt_3,7.3

rudāder gaṇāt sārvadhātuke vyañjanāder ayakārāder ādir iḍ āgamo bhavati, roditi, ruditaḥ, svapiti, svapitaḥ, śvasiti, śvasitaḥ, prāṇiti, prāṇitaḥ, jakṣiti, jakṣitaḥ.
rudyata iti rapatvād yaṇā bhavitavyam.

roditiḥ svapitiścaiva śvasitiḥ prāṇitistathā, 
jakṣitiścaiva vijñeyo rudādiḥ pañcako gaṇaḥ.


īśaḥ se. Kāt_3,7.4

īśaḥ sādau sārvadhātuka ādir iḍ āgamo bhavati, īśiṣe, īśiṣva.


īḍjanoḥ sadhve ca. Kāt_3,7.5

īḍjanoḥ sadhve ca sārvadhātuke para ādir iḍ āgamo bhavati, īḍiṣe, īḍiṣva, īḍidhve, īḍidhvam, vyatijajñiṣe, vyatijajñdhve, vyatijñidhvam.
jana janane, na janī yanā vyavahitatvāt.
sadhve ceti paṭhitatvāccakāreṇa īśiranukṛṣyate, īśidhve, īśidhvam.


se gamaḥ parasmai. Kāt_3,7.6

parasmaipadasya yo gamis tasmāt sa ādir iḍ āgamo bhavati, gamiṣyate, jigamiṣati, adhijigamiṣa tvam, jigamiṣā, jigamiṣuḥ, jigamiṣitavyam.
parasmaipadasyeti kim? adhijigāṃsate, saṃgaṃsīṣṭa.
kecid yogaṃ vibhajyātmanepada iṭamicchanti, tanmatena saṃjigamiṣuḥ, adhijigamiṣitavyam.
aniṅgamaḥ kṛtītyeke, tadā, adhijigāṃsuriti.


hanṛdantāt sye. Kāt_3,7.7

varṇagrahaṇaṃ kim? udavoḍhām, sicy asya dīrghatve 'pi na syāt.


dhuṭāṃ tṛtīyaś caturtheṣu. Kāt_3,8.8

dhātūnāṃ dhuṭāṃ caturtheṣv eva tṛtīyo bhavati, dogdhā, dviḍṭhi, cakāddhi, labdhā.
caturbheṣv eveti niyamāt, śaṅkyate, dviṣṭaḥ.


aghoṣeṣv aśiṭāṃ prathamaḥ. Kāt_3,8.9

aghoṣeṣu parato dhātūnām aśiṭāṃ dhuṭāṃ prathamo bhavati, dhokṣi, bhettā, yuyutsate, āripsate.
aśiṭāmeveti kim? asti.


bhṛjaḥ svarāt svare dviḥ. Kāt_3,8.10

bhṛjaḥ svarāt parasya svare dvir bhavati, bhṛjī, babhrajje, babhrajjāte, babhrajjire.
ādyavyākaraṇamatametat.


asya vamor dīrghaḥ. Kāt_3,8.11

akārasya vamoḥ parato dīrgho bhavati, pacāmi, pacāvaḥ, pacāmaḥ, dīvyāmi, dīvyāvaḥ, dīvyāmaḥ.
asyeti kim? dadhvaḥ, dadhmaḥ, yadi syāddīrghastadālopo na syāt.
kathaṃ pacamānaḥ, apacam, vamorvarṇayorādyayoḥ sāhacaryāt.


svarāntānāṃ sani. Kāt_3,8.12

svarāntānāṃ dhātūnāṃ sani pare dīrgho bhavati, cikīrṣati.
juhūṣati, cicīṣati.
śiśrayiṣati, vibhaviṣatīti guṇenāghrātatvāt svarāntānām iti sukhārtham eva.


haniṅgamor upadhāyāḥ. Kāt_3,8.13

iṅo gamaḥ iṅgamaḥ, haniṅgamor upadhāyā dīrgho bhavati sani pare, jighāṃsati, adhijigāṃsate.
iṅo gama iti kim? saṃjigaṃsate.
titāṃsati, titaniṣatīti vā vaktavyam.


nāmino rvor akurchuror vyañjane. Kāt_3,8.14

nātra tadantaviśeṣaṇam, rvor upadhāyā dhātor nāmino dīrgho bhavati vyañjane pare, na tu kurchuroḥ, cikīrṣati, bubhūrṣati, dīvyati, mīvyati, kūrdate, khūrdate.
dhātor iti kim? kurkuraḥ.
kathaṃ kurkurīyate, nāmadhātutvāt.
nāmina iti kim? kartā, bhavyam.
rvoriti kim? nṛtyati. 
akurchuror iti kim? kuryāt, dīrghavidhiṃ prati na sthānivad iti, churyate.
kathaṃ rī reṣaṇe, riryatuḥ.
vī prajane, vivyatur iti, abhyāsapratiṣedha iti.
vyañjana iti kim? kirati, luvati.


sasya hyastanyāṃ dau taḥ. Kāt_3,8.15

sasya hyastanyāṃ dau pare to bhavati, acakāt, anvaśāt.
hyastanyām iti kim? abhaitsīt, īṭastadgrahaṇena grahaṇāt.
hyastanyāṃ sau vā vaktavyam, acakāstvam, acakāttvam.


aḍ dhātvādir hyastanyadyatanīkriyātipattiṣu. Kāt_3,8.16

hyastanyādiṣu parato dhātor ādir aḍ āgamo bhavati, akarīt, akārṣīt, akariṣyat.
dhātor iti kim? nyaviśata.


svarādīnāṃ vṛddhir ādeḥ. Kāt_3,8.17

svarādīnāṃ dhātūnāṃ hyastanyādiṣv ādeḥ svarasya vṛddhir bhavati, āntaratamyāt, aidhata, aidhiṣṭa, aidhiṣyata.
katham aijyata, aupyata, auhyata, antaraṅgatvādaḍāgame yaṇi saṃprasāraṇe sandhau ca vṛddhiḥ, padāntaraṅgā vā yaṇādayaḥ.


avarṇasyākāraḥ. Kāt_3,8.18

svarādīnāṃ dhātūnām āder avarṇasyākāro bhavati hyastanyādiṣu parataḥ, āṭat, āṭīt, āṭiṣyat, āpnot, āpat, āpsyat.
avarṇaḥ sarvamukhasthānam iti eke, ekadeśenāntaratamyāt, sarvā vṛddhayo mā bhūvanniti varṇagrahaṇam.


asteḥ. Kāt_3,8.19

aster hyastanyām aguṇe 'varṇasyākāro bhavati, āstām, āsan, vyatyāsta, paro 'pyavarṇasyākāro lope na bādhyate 'stimātrāśrayatvāt.


eter ye. Kāt_3,8.20

eter ye hyastanyani pare 'ṭo 'varṇasyākāro bhavati, āyan, adhyāyan.
parāpi vṛddhir iṇmātrāśritena yatvena bādhyate.
ya iti kim? agāt.


na māmāsmayoge. Kāt_3,8.21

māyoge māsmayoge ca hyastanyādiṣv aḍ āgamo na bhavati, mā bhavān karot, mā sma karot, jugupsata smainamaduṣṭabhāvaṃ maivaṃ bhavānakṣatasādhuvṛtta iti matam. 
mā bhavān kārṣīt, mā sma kārṣīt, saṃyukte na syād iti māsmagrahaṇam.
sāhacaryānmado na syāt, mā bhavānapaśyat.


nāmyantād dhātor āśīradyatanīparokṣāsu dho ḍhaḥ. Kāt_3,8.22

nāmyantād dhātor āśīradyatanīparokṣāsu yo dhakāras tasya ḍhakāro bhavati, ceṣīḍhvam, kṛṣīḍhvam, adhyagīḍhvam, samasthiḍhvam, tuṣṭuḍhve, cakṛḍhve.
antagrahaṇaṃ bhūtapūrvanāmyantārtham, tena prāvariṣīḍhvam, alaviḍhvam, luluviḍhve.
dhātor iti saṃjñāpūrvakatvād anityārtham, tenāsu seṭsu vibhāṣā siddhā, prāvariṣīḍhvam, prāvariṣīdhvam, alaviḍhvam, alavidhvam, didīyiḍhve, didīyidhva ity api.


marjo mārjiḥ. Kāt_3,8.23

marja ity etasya mārjir ādeśo bhavati, mārṣṭā, mārkṣyati, amārṭ, mārjo vartate.
marja iti kim? mṛṣṭaḥ.

aguṇe svare vā vaktavyam, parimṛjanti, parimārjanti.


dhātvādeḥ ṣaḥ saḥ. Kāt_3,8.24

dhātor ādyavayavasya ṣakārasya sakāro bhavati, ṣaha, sahate.
ṣic, siñcati.
dhātor iti kim? ṣaṭ, ṣaṇḍaḥ.
āder iti kim? laṣitum.
kathaṃ ṣaṇḍīyati, nāmadhātutvād dhātoś cārambhako yan na ṣakāra iti.
ṣṭhivuklambācamāmani [Kāt_3,6.67] iti nirdeśāt, ṣṭhīvati, ṣṭhiver api ṣakāraṣṭhakāraparathakāra paro veti matam, tena ṭeṣṭhīvyate, teṣṭhīvyata iti siddham.

ṣvakkerna syād iti vaktavyam, ṣvakkate, nimittādvikārasthasya sakārasya ṣatvārthaḥ ṣopadeśo dhātūnām iti, tatra ca svaradantyaparāḥ sādayaḥ ṣopadeśāḥ, ṣmiṅsvidiṣvadiṣvapayaśca sṛpisṛjistṝstyāsīkṛsekṛvarjam.


ṇo naḥ. Kāt_3,8.25

dhātvāder ṇakārasya nakāro bhavati, ṇīñ nayati, ṇama namati.
dhātvāder iti kim? kvaṇati.
kathaṃ ṇakārīyati, nāmadhātutvāt.
ihāpyupasargādasamāse ṇopadeśasya ṇatvārtho nakārapāṭhaḥ.
sarve nādayo ṇopadeśāḥ, nṛtinandinardinakkināṭinaṭinṝnāthṛnādhṛvarjam.


nimittāt pratyayavikārāgamasthaḥ saḥ ṣatvam. Kāt_3,8.26

antyārtho 'yam ārambhaḥ, nimittān nāmikarāt paraḥ pratyayavikārāgamasthaḥ saḥ ṣatvam āpadyate.
nāminas tāvat, cicīṣati, lulūṣati, sarpiṣyati, dhanuṣyati.
kāt, śakṣyati, vivakṣati.
rāt, cikīrṣati.
vikārasthaḥ, siṣeva, suṣvāpa.
āgamasthaḥ, pariṣkaroti, vacanād bhinnapade 'pivyapadeśivadbhāvāt.
pratyayavikārāgamastha iti kim? sṛpḷ, sisṛpsati.
sekṛ, sisekiṣate, tasyaivāpiśabdasyāyaṃ prapañcaḥ.

tathopasargāt sunotisuvatisyatistautistobhatīnām aḍantaro  'pi, abhiṣuṇoti, abhyaṣuṇot, abhiṣuvati, abhyaṣuvat, abhiṣyati, abhyaṣyat, abhiṣṭauti, abhyaṣṭaut, abhiṣṭobhate, abhyaṣṭobhata.

sthāsenisedhatisicasanjasvanjām aḍabhyāsāntaro 'pi, abhiṣṭhāsyati, abhyaṣṭhāt, abhitaṣṭhau.
senayā hyabhiyāti, abhiṣeṇayati, abhyaṣeṇayati, abhyaṣeṇayat, abhiṣiṣeṇayiṣati.
abhiṣedhati, abhyaṣedhat, pratiṣiṣedhayiṣati, pratyaṣedhat, pratiṣiṣedhiṣati.
abhiṣiñcati, abhyaṣiñcat, abhiṣiṣikṣati.
abhiṣajati, abhyaṣajat, abhiṣiṣaṅkṣati.
pariṣvajate, paryaṣvajata, pariṣiṣvaṅkṣate.

saderaprateḥ.
niṣīdati, nyaṣīdat, niṣiṣatsati.
aprateriti kim? pratisīdati, pratyasīdat, pratisiṣatsati.

praterapi stanbheḥ.
pratiṣṭabhnāti, pratyaṣṭabhnāt, pratitaṣṭambha.
evam abhiṣṭabhnāti, abhyaṣṭabhnāt, abhitaṣṭambha.
avād aurjityanikaṭāśrayeṣu, mallasyāvaṣṭambhaḥ, avaṣṭabdhā senā, daṇḍamavaṣṭabhyāste.
eṣviti kim? avastabdho vṛṣalaḥ, śītena saṃkucita ity arthaḥ.

veśca svano bhojane.
viṣvaṇati, avaṣvaṇati, vyaṣvaṇat, avāṣvaṇat, viṣaṣvāṇa, avaṣaṣvāṇa, saśabdaṃ bhuṅkta ity arthaḥ. evam anye 'py anusartavyāḥ.


śāsivasighasīnāṃ ca. Kāt_3,8.27

nimittāt paraḥ śāsivasighasīnāṃ ca saḥ ṣatvam āpadyate, śiṣyate, uṣyate, jakṣatuḥ.
avikārastha ity ārambhaḥ.


stautīnantayor eva sani. Kāt_3,8.28

nimittāt paraḥ pratyayavikārāgamasthaḥ stautīnantayor eva sani ṣatvabhūte saḥ ṣatvam āpadyate, tuṣṭūṣati, siṣedhayiṣati, suṣvāpayiṣati.
stautīnantayor iti kim? sisikṣati, susūṣati.
ṣatvabhūta iti kim? tiṣṭhāsati, suṣupsati.
kathaṃ soṣupiṣate, cekrīyite ṣatvaṃ paścāt san.
arthān pratīṣiṣati, sano 'vayavasyānabhyāsasthānnimittāt ṣatvaṃ syād eva.

svidisvadisahīnāminantānāṃ neṣyate, sisvedayiṣati, sisvādayiṣati, sisāhayiṣati.
tenaivāpi śabdenānyadapi vyabhicāryate, tathā sicaescekrīyite na syāt, sesicyate.
sunoteḥ sye, abhisoṣyate.
sedhatergatau, abhisedhayati gām, gamayatītyarthaḥ.
evam anye 'py anusartavyāḥ.


luglope na pratyayakṛtam. Kāt_3,8.29

lukā lope sati pratyaye pare yat kāryaṃ prakṛtes tan na bhavati, lukā lopo yasyeti vigrahaḥ, aṅgāḥ, vaṅgāḥ, kaliṅgāḥ, pañca, kati, dugdhe, vikaraṇaluki na guṇaḥ, lukīti na kṛtaṃ luglopayorviśeṣapratipattyartham, tena pratyayalope pratyayalakṣaṇamavadhāryate, abhitta, acchitta.
pratyayakṛtam iti kim? parasyāna us, udaguḥ, aduḥ.
katīha, pañcātra.


svaravidhiḥ svare dvirvacananimitte kṛte dvirvacane. Kāt_3,8.30

dvirvacananimitte svarādau pratyaye pare prakṛteḥ pūrvasmin parasmin vā dvirvacane kṛte svarasya sthāne vidhir bhavati, papatuḥ, āṭiṭat, jagmatuḥ, iyāya, nināya, ninayitha, lulāva, lulavitha, ninyatuḥ, cakratuḥ.
svaravidhir iti kim? asūṣupat, saparasvarāyāḥ saṃprasāraṇe paścād dvirvacanam.
svara iti kim? jeghrīyate.
dvirvacananimitta iti kim? dudyūṣati.
yena vinā yanna bhavati tattasya nimittam.
iṭo vidhinā sani dvirvacanam iti tena, aririṣatīti siddham.
katham iyeṣa, uvoṣa, na sthānivattvam, asavarṇa iti vacanāt.


yo 'nubandho 'prayogī. Kāt_3,8.31

anubadhyata ity anubandhaḥ, aprayuktir aprayogaḥ, anubandho yaḥ so 'prayogī, anuccāraṇīyo bhavati, iṅ, adhīte.
ḍakṛñ, kurute, evam anye 'pi.


śiḍ iti śādayaḥ. Kāt_3,8.32
