padyate, patsyate, apādi, pede vā, pādaḥ.
evaṃ rogaḥ, veśaḥ, sparśo nāma kṣayavyādhiś ca, okaḥ.


sṛ sthiravyādhyoḥ. Kāt_4,5.2

sarteḥ sthire vyādhau ca kartari ghañ bhavati, sarati kālāntaram iti sāraḥ, sthiro 'rthaḥ.
atīsāro vyādhiḥ, hrasvasya dīrghatā.
saranty aneneti sāro balam, visaranty aneneti visāro matsyaḥ, saṃjñāśabdāt karaṇa eva siddhaḥ.
yady evaṃ padyate 'neneti pādo bhaviṣyati, satyam, prapañcārthaṃ padigrahaṇam.


bhāve. Kāt_4,5.3

sarvasmād dhātor bhāve ghañ bhavati, pākaḥ, pākau, pākāḥ.
bhavatyarthaḥ kriyāsāmānya iha hi siddhatākhyaḥ sattvabhūta iti dvivacanabahuvacane staḥ.


akartari ca kārake saṃjñāyām. Kāt_4,5.4

kartṛvarjite kārake bhāve ca saṃjñāyāṃ gamyamānāyāṃ ghañ bhavati, prakurvanti tam iti prākāraḥ, prāsyata iti prāsaḥ, āharanti tam ity āhāraḥ, prasīdanty asmin nayanamanāṃsīti prāsādaḥ, dīryanta ebhir iti dārāḥ, jīryate 'neneti jāraḥ.
akartarīti kim? nadatīti nadaḥ śoṇaḥ.
asaṃjñāyām api, dāyo dattaḥ, lābho labdhaḥ.
kārakagrahaṇaṃ prasahya nañsamāsajñāpanārtham.


sarvasmāt parimāṇe. Kāt_4,5.5

parimeyatvāt parimāṇam, parimāṇaviṣaye vartamānāt sarvasmād dhātor ghañ bhavati, kartṛvarjite kārake bhāve ca saṃjñāyāṃ gamyamānāyām, saṃkhyāprasthādir vā parimāṇam, ekas taṇḍulaniścāyaḥ, dvau śūrpaniṣpāvau, prasthaniścāyaḥ, droṇāvakṣāyaḥ, alo bādhakatvāt sarvasmād bhaviṣyati, sarvasmād iti jñāpayati, dhātvāśritaḥ pratyayo ghañā bādhyate na tv arthāśrita iti, tena, ekā tilocchritiḥ, dve srutī tailasya, ktir eva.
ekaṃ sravaṇam, dve prasthāne, yuṭ siddhaḥ.
katham eko niścayaḥ, apyadhikārāt.


iṅābhyāṃ ca. Kāt_4,5.6

iṅa ākārāntāc ca dhātor ghañ bhavati, alo 'pavādaḥ, bhāve 'kartari ca kārake saṃjñāyām ity aviśeṣe 'dhikāro draṣṭavyaḥ.
adhyayanam adhīyate vā, adhyāyaḥ.
upetyādhīyate yasmāt, upādhyāyaḥ, upādhyāyā, upādhyāyī, iṅo ghañ nadādau vibhāṣayeti.
ākārāntāc ca, dāyaḥ, dhāyaḥ.


upasarge ruvaḥ. Kāt_4,5.7

upasarga upapade rauter ghañ bhavati, saṃrāvaḥ, uparāvaḥ.
upasarga iti kim? ravaḥ.
sāṃrāviṇam ity atra inuṇ bādhakaḥ.


sami duvaḥ. Kāt_4,5.8

samy upapade dunoter ghañ bhavati, saṃdāvaḥ.
samīti kim? davaḥ.


yudruvor udi ca. Kāt_4,5.9

udy upapade sami ca yudrubhyāṃ ghañ bhavati, udyāvaḥ, uddrāvaḥ.
saṃyāvaḥ, saṃdrāva eveti ke cit.
udi ceti kim? yavaḥ, dravaḥ.
apyadhikārād yāvaḥ, drāvaḥ.
dāva iti ca syāt.
tathā śāro vāyuḥ, śāraḥ śaralaḥ, nīśāraḥ prāvaraṇam, hrasvasya dīrghatā.


śrinībhūbhyo 'nupasarge. Kāt_4,5.10

ebhyo 'nupasarge ghañ bhavati, śrāyaḥ, nāyaḥ, bhāvaḥ.
anupasarga iti kim? praśrayaḥ, praṇayaḥ, prabhavaḥ.
kathaṃ prakṛṣṭo bhāvaḥ, prabhāvaḥ, anugato bhāvaḥ, anubhāvaḥ, vigato bhāvaḥ, vibhāvaḥ.
apyadhikārāt, naya iti ca.


kṣuśrubhyāṃ vau. Kāt_4,5.11

vāv upapada ābhyāṃ ghañ bhavati, vikṣāvaḥ, viśrāvaḥ.


straś ca prathane 'śabde. Kāt_4,5.12

prathanaṃ vistīrṇatā.
stṛṇāter vāv upapade ghañ bhavati prathane 'bhidheye, tac cet prathanaṃ śabdaviṣaye na syāt, paṭasya vistāraḥ.
aśabda iti kim? vākyasya vistaraḥ.
prathana iti kim? tṛṇasya vistaraḥ.


pre cāyajñe. Kāt_4,5.13

pre copapade stṛṇāter ghañ bhavati yajñād anyatra, prastāraḥ.
yajñe tu, barhiḥ prastaraḥ.


chandonāmni ca. Kāt_4,5.14

chandasāṃ saṃjñāviṣaye stṛṇāter ghañ bhavati, prastārapaṅktiḥ, viṣṭārapaṅktiḥ, āstārapaṅktiḥ.


pre drustuśruvaḥ. Kāt_4,5.15

pra upapada ebhyo ghañ bhavati, pradrāvaḥ, prastāvaḥ, praśrāvaḥ.
kathaṃ śrāvaḥ, apyadhikārāt.


niyo 'vodoḥ. Kāt_4,5.16

avodor upapadayor niyo ghañ bhavati, avanāyaḥ, unnāyaḥ.
katham udyato nayaḥ, unnayaḥ, apyadhikārād vā.


nirabhyoḥ pūlvoḥ. Kāt_4,5.17

nirabhyor upapadayor yathāsaṃkhyaṃ pūlvor ghañ bhavati, niṣpāvaḥ, abhilāvaḥ.


yajñe sami stuvaḥ. Kāt_4,5.18

samy upapade stauter ghañ yajñaviṣaye, sametya stuvanti yasmin, saṃstāvo deśaḥ, saṃstavo 'nyaḥ.


unnyor giraḥ. Kāt_4,5.19

unnyor upapadayor girater ghañ bhavati, udgāraḥ, nigāraḥ.
unnyor iti kim? garaḥ.


kiro dhānye. Kāt_4,5.20

unnyor upapadayor dhānyaviṣaye vartamānāt kirater ghañ bhavati, utkāro dhānyasya, nikāro dhānyasya.
dhānya iti kim? puṣpotkaraḥ, puṣpanikaraḥ.
kirater iti kim? kṛñ hiṃsāyām, dhānyanikaraḥ.


nau vṛñaḥ. Kāt_4,5.21

nāv upapade vṛño dhātor ghañ bhavati dhānye 'bhidheye, nīvārā vrīhayaḥ, hrasvasya dīrghatā.


udi śripuvoḥ. Kāt_4,5.22

udy upapade śripūṅbhyāṃ ghañ bhavati, ucchrāyaḥ, utpāvaḥ.
katham ucchrayaḥ, apyadhikārāt.


grahaś ca. Kāt_4,5.23

udy upapade graheś ca ghañ bhavati, udgrāhaḥ, bhāṣāyām apīti matam.


avanyor ākrośe. Kāt_4,5.24

avanyor upapadayor ākrośe gamyamāne graher ghañ bhavati, avagrāhas te vṛṣala, nigrāhas te vṛṣala.
ākrośa iti kim? avagrahaḥ padasya, nigrahaś caurasya.


pre lipsāyām. Kāt_4,5.25

pra upapade lipsāyāṃ graher ghañ bhavati, pātrapragrāheṇa carati bhikṣuḥ.
lipsāyām iti kim? pragrahaḥ.


sami muṣṭau. Kāt_4,5.26

samy upapade graher ghañ bhavati muṣṭāv arthe, saṃgrāho mallasya.
muṣṭāv iti kim? saṃgrahaḥ.
aṅgulīnāṃ vacanāviśeṣo muṣṭir iha gṛhyate, ekaḥ śākasaṃgrāhaḥ, sarvasmāt parimāṇe [Kāt_4,5.5] iti siddham.


parau yajñe. Kāt_4,5.27

parāv upapade yajñaviṣaye graher ghañ bhavati, uttaraparigrāhaḥ.
yajña iti kim? parigrahaḥ.


vāve varṣapratibandhe. Kāt_4,5.28

ava upapade graher ghañ bhavati vā varṣapratibandhe 'rthe, avagrāho varṣasya, avagraho vā.


pre raśmau. Kāt_4,5.29

pra upapade graher ghañ bhavati vā raśmāv arthe, pragrāhaḥ, pragraho vā.
raśmir iha rajjur ucyate.


vaṇijāṃ ca. Kāt_4,5.30

vaṇijāṃ ca saṃbandhini tulāsūtre 'rthe pra upapade graher ghañ bhavati vā, tulāpragrāheṇa carati, tulāpragraheṇa vā carati vaṇik.


vṛṇoter ācchādane. Kāt_4,5.31

pra upapade vṛṇoter ācchādane 'rthe ghañ bhavati vā, prāvāraḥ, prāvaraḥ, āṅpūrvo 'yam.


āṅi rupluvoḥ. Kāt_4,5.32

āṅy upapade rauteḥ plavateś ca ghañ bhavati vā, ārāvaḥ, āravaḥ, āplāvaḥ, āplavaḥ.


parau bhuvo 'vajñāne. Kāt_4,5.33

parāv upapade bhavater ghañ bhavati vā, avajñāne 'rthe, paribhāvaḥ, paribhavaḥ.
avajñāna iti kim? sarvato bhavanaṃ paribhavaḥ.


ces tu hastādāne. Kāt_4,5.34

hastādānaviṣaye cinoter ghañ bhavati, puṣpapracāyaḥ.
hastādānagrahaṇaṃ pratyāsannopalakṣaṇam, tena vṛkṣāgre phalapracayaṃ karoti.
apyadhikārāt steye na syāt, hastena phalapracayaṃ karoti cauraḥ.


śarīranivāsayoḥ kaś cādeḥ. Kāt_4,5.35

cinoteḥ śarīranivāse cārthe ghañ bhavati, ādeś ca ko bhavati, cīyate 'sau, kāyaḥ śarīram, nicīyate 'sminn iti nikāyo nivāsaḥ.
apyadhikārāc citirāśyor api, ācīyate 'sau, ākāyaś citiḥ, gomayanikāyaḥ.
kathaṃ kāṣṭhanicayaḥ, bahutvamātravivakṣayeti.


saṃghe cānauttarādharye. Kāt_4,5.36

prāṇināṃ samūhaḥ saṃgha ucyate.
anauttarādharye saṃghe cārtha cinoter ghañ bhavati, kaś cādeḥ, vaiyākaraṇanikāyaḥ.
anauttarādharya iti kim? śūkaranicayaḥ.


parinyor nīṇor dyūtābhreṣayoḥ. Kāt_4,5.37

parinyor upapadayor yathāsaṃkhyaṃ nī-iṇbhyāṃ ghaṇ bhavati dyūtaviṣaye 'bhreṣe cārthe, abhreṣo 'calanam, yathāprāptakaraṇam ity arthaḥ, pariṇāyena śārīn hanti, sarvato nayanenety arthaḥ, eṣo 'tra nyāyaḥ.


vyupayoḥ śeteḥ paryāye. Kāt_4,5.38

vyupayor upapadayoḥ paryāyaviṣaye vartamānāc cheter ghañ bhavati, tava rājaviśāyaḥ, tava rājopaśāyaḥ, tava rājani śayituṃ paryāya ity arthaḥ.
asmād eva jñāpakāt paripūrvādiṇaḥ krame 'rthe ghañ bhavati.


abhividhau bhāva inuṇ. Kāt_4,5.39

abhividhau gamyamāne dhātor inuṇ bhavati, sāṃkoṭinaṃ sāṃrāviṇaṃ vartate, kriyayaivābhivyāptiḥ, inuṇantāt svarthe 'ṇ, yuḍ api dṛśyate, saṃkuṭanaṃ vartate.


karmavyatīhāre ṇac striyām. Kāt_4,5.40

kriyāvinimaye gamyamāne dhātor ṇaj bhavati striyāṃ bhāve, vyāvakrośī, vyāvabhāṣī, ṇajantāt svārthe 'ṇ.
kva cid adhikārāt tatra kriyāvyatīhāreṇa vṛddhir āgamaḥ.
kathaṃ vyatīkṣā, vyavakruṣṭir iti, astryadhikārād vāsarūpatā.


svaravṛdṛgamigrahām al. Kāt_4,5.41

svarāntād vṛdṛgamigrahibhyaś cāl bhavati, ghaño 'pavādaḥ, kṣayaḥ, krayaḥ, bhavaḥ, lavaḥ.
vṛṅ vṛñ vā, varaḥ.
dṛṅ, daraḥ.
gamaḥ, grahaḥ.
vṛdror eveti niyamād anyebhya ṛkārāntebhyo ghañ eva, kāraḥ, hāraḥ.
dīrghād al eva, kṝ karaḥ, gṝ garaḥ.
bhītir bhayam ity al eva.
na yuḍādayo 'pīti, vaśaḥ, raṇa iti rūḍhitvād al.


upasarge 'deḥ. Kāt_4,5.42

upasarga upapade 'der al bhavati, praghasaḥ, vighasaḥ.
ghañalor ghamḷḥ.
upasarga iti kim? ghāsaḥ.


nau ṇa ca. Kāt_4,5.43

nāv upapade 'der al bhavati ṇa ca, nighasaḥ, nyādaḥ.


madeḥ prasamor harṣe. Kāt_4,5.44

prasamor upapadayor mader al bhavati harṣe 'rthe, pramadaḥ kanyānām, saṃmadaḥ kokilānām.


vyadhajapoś cānupasarge. Kāt_4,5.45

anupasarge vyadhijapibhyāṃ madeś cāl bhavati, vyadhaḥ, japaḥ, madaḥ.
anupasarga iti kim? āvyādhaḥ, upajāpaḥ, pramādaḥ.


svanahasor vā. Kāt_4,5.46

anupasarga ābhyām al bhavati vā, svanaḥ, svānaḥ, hasaḥ, hāsaḥ.
anupasarga iti kim? prasvānaḥ, prahāsaḥ.


yamaḥ saṃnyupaviṣu ca. Kāt_4,5.47

anupasarge saṃnyupaviṣu ca yamer al bhavati vā, yamaḥ, yāmaḥ, saṃyamaḥ, saṃyāmaḥ, niyamaḥ, niyāmaḥ, upayamaḥ, upayāmaḥ, viyamaḥ, viyāmaḥ.


nau gadanadapaṭhasvanām. Kāt_4,5.48

nāv upapada ebhyo 'l bhavati vā, nigadaḥ, nigādaḥ, ninadaḥ, ninādaḥ, nipaṭhaḥ, nipāṭhaḥ, nisvanaḥ, nisvānaḥ.
svanahasor vā [Kāt_4,5.46] iti vacanād anupasarga iha na vartate.


kvaṇo vīṇāyāṃ ca. Kāt_4,5.49

nāv upapade 'nupasarge ca vīṇāviṣaye kvaṇater al bhavati vā, kvaṇaḥ, kvāṇaḥ, nikvaṇaḥ, nikvāṇaḥ.
cakāre sati vīṇāgrahaṇaṃ sopasargārtham, prakvaṇo vīṇāyāḥ, prakvāṇaḥ.


paṇaḥ parimāṇe nityam. Kāt_4,5.50

paṇater al bhavati nityaṃ parimāṇe 'rthe, paṇaḥ, śākādīnām api parimitā muṣṭiḥ paṇa ucyate.
parimāna iti kim? dāsyāḥ pāṇaḥ.


samudor ajaḥ paśuṣu. Kāt_4,5.51

samudor upapadayoḥ paśuṣu vartamānād ajer al bhavati, samajaḥ paśunām, samūha ity arthaḥ.
udajaḥ paśūnām, preraṇam ity arthaḥ.
paśuṣv iti kim? samājaś chāttrāṇām, udājaḥ khagānām.


glaho 'kṣeṣu. Kāt_4,5.52

akṣaviṣaye vartamānād graher ali latvaṃ nipātyate, akṣāṇāṃ glahaḥ, glahiḥ prakṛtyantaram ity eke, tadā praglāha iti ghañi pratyudāharaṇam.


sarteḥ prajane. Kāt_4,5.53

prajane garbhagrahaṇe vartamānāt sarter al bhavati, gavām upasaraḥ, upasāro 'nyaḥ.


hvo huś cābhyupaniviṣu ca. Kāt_4,5.54

eṣūpapadeṣu hvayater al bhavati hur ādeśaś ca, abhihavaḥ, upahavaḥ, nihavaḥ, vihavaḥ.


āṅi yuddhe. Kāt_4,5.55

āṅy upapade hvayater al bhavati yuddhe 'rthe hur ādeśaś ca, āhūyante yasmin yoddhāraḥ sa āhavaḥ.
katham āhūyante pānāya gāvo yasmin sa āhāvo jalādhāraḥ, anyatrāpīti ghañi ca hur ādeśaḥ.


bhāve 'nupasargasya. Kāt_4,5.56

anupasargasya hvayater al bhavati bhāve hur ādeśaś ca, havaḥ.
anupasargasyeti kim? prahvāyaḥ.


hanter vadhiś ca. Kāt_4,5.57

anupasargasya hanter al bhavati bhāve vadhir ādeśaś ca, hananaṃ vadhaḥ.
apyadhikārāc ca ghātaḥ.
anupasargasyeti kim? vighātaḥ.


mūrtau ghaniś ca. Kāt_4,5.58

mūrtiḥ kāṭhinyam, mūrtāv arthe hanter al bhavati ghanir ādeśaś ca, dadhno ghanaḥ, ghanaṃ dadhīty abhedāt.


prād gṛhaikadeśe ghañ ca. Kāt_4,5.59

prād hanter al bhavati ghañ ca ghanir ādeśaś ca gṛhaikadeśe 'rthe, praghaṇaḥ, praghāṇaḥ, gṛhasya dvidhākṛtasya dvāraprakoṣṭhābhyāṃ yo vahir bhūtaḥ, tatrāpīti vacanāṇ ṇatvam.


antarghanodghanau deśātyādhānayoḥ. Kāt_4,5.60

etāv alantau nipātyete deśātyādhānayor yathāsaṃkhyam, antarhanyate yasmin so 'ntarghano deśaḥ, ūrdhvaṃ hanyate yasmin sa udghanaḥ, yasyopari kāṣṭhāni hanyante tad atyādhānam.


karaṇe 'yovidruṣu. Kāt_4,5.61

eṣūpapadeṣu hanter al bhavati karaṇe ghanir ādeśaś ca, ayo hanyate 'neneti, ayoghanaḥ, vihanyate 'neneti vighanaḥ, evaṃ drughaṇaḥ, saṃjñāyāṃ ṇatvam.


parau ḍaḥ. Kāt_4,5.62

parāv upapade hanter ḍo bhavati karaṇe ghanir ādeśaś ca, parihanyate 'neneti parighaḥ.
latve palighaḥ.


nau nimite. Kāt_4,5.63

nāv upapade hanter ḍo bhavati ghanir ādeśaś ca nimite vastuni, nirviśeṣeṇa hanyante jñāyante vā, nighā vṛkṣāḥ, nighāḥ śālayaḥ.
sarvato nimitā ārohataḥ pariṇāhataś ca.
nimita iti kim? nighātaḥ.


samudor gaṇapraśaṃsayoḥ. Kāt_4,5.64

samudor upapadayor hanter ḍo bhavati ghanir ādeśaś ca gaṇe praśaṃsāyām, saṃhananaṃ saṃhanyate yasminn avayavo vā, saṃghaḥ.
utkṛṣṭaṃ hanyate jñāyata iti, udgho manuṣyaḥ, praśasta ity arthaḥ.


upāt ka āśraye. Kāt_4,5.65

upād hanteḥ ko bhavati, āśraye gamyamāne, ghanir ādeśaś ca, kuḍyopaghnaṃ vasati.


stambe 'c ca. Kāt_4,5.66

stamba upapade hanter aj bhavati kapratyayo ghanir ādeśaś ca, stambo hanyate 'neneti stambaghnaḥ, stambaghno daṇḍaḥ, stambaghno yaṣṭiḥ, puṃstvam eva, ke cit striyām ādā, stambaghnā yaṣṭir iti.
apyadhikārāt sthāsnāpibativyadhihanibhyaḥ kaḥ syāt, ākhūtthaṃ vartate, prasnāty asminn iti prasnaḥ, prapibanty asyām iti prapā, āvidhyate 'nenety āvidhaḥ, vihanyate 'neneti vighnaḥ, āyudhyate 'nenety āyudhaṃ śastraṃ, jñāpakād eva.


ṭvanubandhād athuḥ. Kāt_4,5.67

ṭvanubandhād dhātor athur bhavati bhāva eva, ṭuvepṛ, vepathuḥ.
ṭu-ośvi, śvayathuḥ.
ṭudu, davathuḥ.
ṭuvama, vamathuḥ.
vepadava iti vāsarūpatvāt.


ḍvanubandhāt trimak tena nirvṛtte. Kāt_4,5.68

ḍvanubandhād dhātos trimag bhavati, tena dhātvarthena nirvṛtte 'rthe.
ḍupacaṣ, pākena nirvṛttam, paktrimam.
ḍukṛñ, karaṇena nirvṛttam, kṛtrimam.
nirvṛttam iti kartari karmaṇi vā, teneti yathāyogaṃ tṛtīyā.


yācivichiprachiyajisvapirakṣiyatāṃ naṅ. Kāt_4,5.69

ebhyo naṅ bhavati, yācñā, viśnaḥ, praśnaḥ, yajñaḥ, svapnaḥ, rakṣṇaḥ, yatnaḥ.


upasarge daḥ kiḥ. Kāt_4,5.70

upasarga upapade dāsaṃjñakāt kir bhavati, ādiḥ, nidhiḥ.
apyadhikārād antardhiḥ.


karmaṇy adhikaraṇe ca. Kāt_4,5.71

karmaṇy upapade dāsaṃjñakād adhikaraṇe ca kir bhavati, vāladhiḥ, jaladhiḥ.
upasargair avyavadhānataiva, payonidhiḥ.


striyāṃ ktiḥ. Kāt_4,5.72

strīliṅge bhāve 'kartari ca kārake saṃjñāyāṃ ktir bhavati, kṛtiḥ, buddhiḥ, ijyate 'nayeti, iṣṭiḥ, evaṃ śrutiḥ, stutiḥ, karaṇe 'pi.


sātihetiyūtijūtayaś ca. Kāt_4,5.73

ete ktipratyayā nipātyante striyām, sinoteḥ sanoter vā sātiḥ, hinoter hetiḥ, yauter yūtiḥ, javater jūtiḥ.


bhāve pacigāpāsthābhyaḥ. Kāt_4,5.74

ebhyo bhāve striyāṃ ktir bhavati, paceḥ ṣānubandhatvād aṅi prāpte, paktiḥ.
tathā, ātaś copasarge [Kāt_4,5.84] saṃgītiḥ, prapītiḥ, saṃsthitiḥ.
apyadhikārāt saṃsthā, vyavasthā.


vrajyajoḥ kyap. Kāt_4,5.75

bhāve striyām ābhyāṃ kyab bhavati, vrajyā, ijyā, iṣṭir ity api bhāve.


samajāsanisadanipatiśīṅsuvidyaṭicarimanibhṛñiṇāṃ saṃjñāyām. Kāt_4,5.76

ebhyaḥ saṃjñāyāṃ bhāve kyab bhavati striyām, samajyā, āsyā, niṣīdanty asyām iti niṣadyā, nipatanty asyām iti nipatyā, śerate 'syām iti śayyā, adhikaraṇe 'pi, savanaṃ sutyā, 
vidyā, karaṇe 'pi, aṭeś cekrīyitāntād evābhidhānād aṭāṭyā, paripūrvād eva careḥ paricaryā, manyā, bhṛtyā, ityā.
apyadhikārāt, āsutiḥ, bhṛtiḥ, samitiḥ.
bhāva iti kim? bhāryā.
saṃjñāyām iti kim? saṃvittiḥ.


kṛñaḥ śa ca. Kāt_4,5.77

kṛñaḥ śo bhavati ktiḥ kyap ca, kriyata iti kriyā, bhāve ca, kṛtiḥ, kṛtyā.


sarter yaś ca. Kāt_4,5.78

abhidhānāt paripūrvāt sarter yo bhavati, parisaryā.
cakārāj jāgarteś ca, jāgaryā.


icchā. Kāt_4,5.79

iṣer iccheti nipātyate, icchā.


śaṃsipratyayād aḥ. Kāt_4,5.80

śansur niṣṭhāyām aniḍ iti vacanam, śanseḥ pratyayāntāc ca dhātor apratyayo bhavati striyām, praśaṃsā, pipatiṣā.
dṛśado yin, dṛśadā, aṭāṭā, kaṇḍūyā, kaṇḍūtir apīty eke.


guroś ca niṣṭhāseṭaḥ. Kāt_4,5.81

gurumato dhātor niṣṭhāyāṃ seṭo 'pratyayo bhavati, īhā, īkṣā, jāgarā.
guror iti kim? nigṛhītiḥ.
niṣṭhāseṭa iti kim? nītiḥ, rāddhiḥ.


ṣānubandhabhidādibhyas tv aṅ. Kāt_4,5.82

ṣānubandhebhyo bhidādibhyas tv aṅ bhavati, jṝṣ, jarā.
ḍupacaṣ, pacā.
kṣiṣa, kṣiyā.
ghaṭādayaḥ ṣānubandhāḥ, ghaṭā, vyathā.
kṛpa kṛpāyām iti nirdeśāt kṛpā, upalabdhir iti jñāpakāt, kṣāntir ity api syāt.
bhidādibhyo nāma gaṇanirdiṣṭebhya iti bhidā vidāraṇe, bhittir anyā.
chidā dvidhākaraṇe, chittir anyā.
guhā parvataikadeśe, gūḍhir anyā.
āṅpūrvād arteḥ, ārā śastrī, artir anyā.
dhṛṅ prapāte, dhārā, dhṛtir anyā.
vida, vidā.
kṣipa, kṣipā.
gudha, godhā.
hṛñ, hārā.
kṛñ, kārā.
likha, lekhā, ratvaṃ vādeḥ, rekhā.
ūnacudapīḍamṛgayatibhya inantebhyo yau prāpte vacanam, ūnā, cūḍā, dīrghatvaṃ ḍatvaṃ ca syāt, pīḍā, mṛgayā.
vaśā, rujā, mṛjā, guṇavṛddhyādikam arthaviṣeṣaś ca gaṇapāṭhasāmarthyāt.


bhīṣicintipūjikathikumbicarcispṛhitolidolibhyaś ca. Kāt_4,5.83

ebhya inantebhyo 'ṅ bhavati, bhiyo hetubhaye ṣāntaḥ, bhīṣaṇaṃ bhīṣā.
citi smṛtyām, cintā, pūja pūjāyām, pūjā.
katha vākyaprabandhe, kathā.
kubi cchādane, kumbā.
carca adhyayane, carcā.
spṛha īpsāyām, spṛhā.
tula unmādane, tolā.
dula utkṣepe, dolā.
kathaṃ tulā, tulayā saṃmita iti nirdeśāt.


ātaś copasarge. Kāt_4,5.84

upasarga upapada ākārāntād dhātor aṅ bhavati, saṃsthā, upadā, upadhā.
antaḥpūrvāc ca vaktavyam, antardhā.
kathaṃ śraddhā, ā śraddhā [Kāt_2,1.10] iti nirdeśāt.
apyadhikārāt pramitiḥ.


īṣiśranthyāsivandividikāritāntebhyo yuḥ. Kāt_4,5.85

ebhyo yur bhavati.
īṣa gatihiṃsādāneṣu, īṣaṇā.
śranthanā, upāsanā, vandanā.
āsisahacarito vettiḥ, vedanā.
kāraṇā.
curādau ghaṭṭa calane, ghaṭṭanā, bhauvādikasya kter anabhidhānāt.


kīrtīṣoḥ ktiś ca. Kāt_4,5.86

kīrtayater iṣeś ca ktir yuś ca bhavati, kīrttiḥ, saṃkīrtanā.
iṣa gatau, iṣa ābhīkṣṇye vā, anviṣṭiḥ, parīṣṭiḥ, anveṣaṇā, paryeṣaṇā.
iṣu icchāyām iti sānubandhaḥ, iṣṭiḥ.


rogākhyāyāṃ vuñ. Kāt_4,5.87

vyādher ākhyāyāṃ dhātor vuñ bhavati, pravāhikā, pracchardikā, vicarcikā.
apyadhikārāt, śiro'rdanam, śiro'rttiḥ.


saṃjñāyāṃ ca. Kāt_4,5.88

saṃjñāyāṃ ca viṣaye dhātor vuñ bhavati, udyānapuṣpāṇi bhajyante yasyāṃ krīḍāyāṃ sā, udyānapuṣpabhañjikā krīḍā, krīḍāyāṃ nityasamāsa eva, puṣpabhañjikā krīḍety evārthavatī saṃjñā, evaṃ vāraṇapūṣpapracāyikā.


paryāyārharṇeṣu ca. Kāt_4,5.89

eṣu vartamānād dhātor vuñ bhavati, adyabhavataḥ śāyikā.
arhati bhavān ikṣubhakṣikām.
ṛṇe, pāyasabhojikāṃ me dhārayasi.
cakārād utpattau ca, ikṣubhakṣikā ma udapādi na ca bhavati, cikīrṣā jihīrṣā ma utpadyate.
bhāvamātre ca dṛśyate, kā nāma śāyikā, anyeṣv adhīyamāneṣu, kā nāmāsikā, anyeṣu gacchas tv iti. 


praśnākhyānayor iñ ca vā. Kāt_4,5.90

praśna ākhyāne ca gamyamāne dhātor iñ vuñ ca bhavati, vāgrahaṇād yathāprāptam, kāṃ tvaṃ kārim akārṣīḥ kāṃ kārikāṃ kāṃ kṛtiṃ kāṃ kriyāṃ kāṃ kṛtyām, sarvāṃ kārim akārṣaṃ sarvāṃ kārikāṃ sarvāṃ kṛtiṃ sarvāṃ kriyāṃ sarvāṃ kṛtyām.


nañy any ākrośe. Kāt_4,5.91

nañy upapada ākrośe gamyamāne dhātor anir bhavati, akaraṇis te vṛṣala bhūyāt, evam ajīvaniḥ.
nañīti kim? mṛtis te vṛṣala bhūyāt.
saṃpadādibhyaḥ kvib bhāve kārake cānyatrāpīti bahulatvāt, sa eva saṃpat, pratipat, vipat, saṃpattir ity api syāt, saṃpadādir ākṛtigaṇo 'yam.
ikiśtipo dhātoḥ svarūpe 'rthe jñāpakād eva siddhāḥ.
akāraḥ kakāra ity uṇādiṣu kāraśabdena vā samāsaḥ, yathā, evaṃkāraḥ, oṃkāraḥ, cītkāraḥ, śītkāraḥ, sphītkāraḥ, sphutkāraḥ, vaṣaṭkāraḥ, svāhākāra ity ādi.
rādiphaḥ, repha ity auṇādikaḥ.


kṛtyayuṭo 'nyatrāpi ca. Kāt_4,5.92

kṛtyā yuṭ ca yasminn arthe vihitās tato 'nyatrāpi ca bhavanti lakṣyataḥ, snānīyaṃ cūrṇam, dānīyo brāhmaṇaḥ, samāvartanīyo guruḥ, pravacanīya upādhyāyaḥ, karaṇādiṣu bhavanty amī, bhavyageyapravacanīyopasthānīyajanyāplāvyāpātyāḥ kartary api bhavanti, āṅpūrvayoḥ pluṅpatyor yaṇ iti.
rājabhir bhujyante, rājabhojanāḥ śālayaḥ, rājācchādanāni vāsāṃsi, avasecanam, avaśravaṇam, dānam, ete karmaṇi.
praskandanam, prapatanam ity apādāne.
apiśabdo 'tra bahulārtha iti.
ṣṭhivuṣivvor dīrghaś ca vā, niṣṭhīvanaṃ niṣṭhevanam, niṣīvaṇaṃ niṣevaṇam.
karotīti kāraṇam.


napuṃsake bhāve ktaḥ. Kāt_4,5.93

napuṃsake bhāve 'rthe kto bhavati, śayitam, sthitam, bhavatā kṛtam, prāptam anenety avivakṣitakarmatvāt, yuṭā bādhito napuṃsake kto yathā syād iti vacanam, vāsarūpatvāc ced ghañādayo 'pi syur iti.


yuṭ ca. Kāt_4,5.94

napuṃsake bhāve yuṭ ca bhavati, sthānam, gamanam.


karaṇādhikaraṇayoś ca. Kāt_4,5.95

karaṇe 'dhikaraṇe ca yuḍ bhavati napuṃsake, idhmavraścanam, palāśaśātanam.
adhikaraṇe ca, godohanī ghaṭī, śaktudhānī sthālī.


puṃsi saṃjñāyāṃ ghaḥ. Kāt_4,5.96

karaṇādhikaraṇayoḥ puṃsi saṃjñāyāṃ gho bhavati svarāntāt, uraś chādyate 'neneti, uraśchadaḥ.
kurvanty aneneti karaḥ, śṛṇanty aneneti śaraḥ.
adhikaraṇe 'pi, līyante 'sminn iti layaḥ, nilīyante 'sminn iti nilayaḥ, viṣiṇvanty asminn iti viṣayaḥ.


gocarasaṃcaravahavrajavyajakramāpaṇanigamāś ca. Kāt_4,5.97

ete ghapratyayāntā nipātyante, gāvaś caranty asminn iti gocaraḥ, pratyāsattir upalakṣyate.
evaṃ saṃcaraḥ, vahanty aneneti vaho vṛṣabhasya, vrajanty asminn iti vrajaḥ.
vipūrvo 'ja, vyajanty aneneti vyajaḥ, krāmanty aneneti kramaḥ.
āpaṇāyante 'neneti, āpaṇaḥ.
nigacchanty aneneti nigamaḥ.
cakārāt, bhajanty asminn iti bhagaḥ, nikaṣanty aneneti nikaṣaḥ.


ave tṝstror ghañ. Kāt_4,5.98

ava upapade tṝstṝbhyāṃ ghañ bhavati, ghāpavādaḥ.
avataranty aneneti, asminn iti vā, avatāraḥ.
avastṛṇanty aneneti, asminn iti vā, avastāraḥ.


vyañjanāc ca. Kāt_4,5.99

vyañjanāntāc ca ghāpavādo ghañ bhavati, likhyanty aneneti lekhaḥ, vidanty aneneti vedaḥ.
apamṛjanty aneneti, apāmārgaḥ, hrasvasya dīrghatā.
ācaranty aneneti, ācāraḥ.
evam āvāsaḥ.
cakārāt, adhyāyaḥ, nyāyaḥ, udyāvaḥ, saṃhāraḥ, ādhāraḥ, ādhāya iti ca.


udaṅko 'nudake. Kāt_4,5.100

udañcater ghañy udaṅka iti nipātyate 'nudakaviṣaye, ūrdhvam añcanty aneneti, udaṅkaḥ, ghṛtodaṅkaḥ.
anudaka iti kim? udakodañcanaḥ, ghe tv aviśeṣād yuṭ.


jālam ānāyaḥ. Kāt_4,5.101

ānāya iti nipātyate jālaṃ cet, ānīyante 'neneti, ānāyo matsyānām.

ākhanyate 'neneti, ākhanaḥ, gho 'pi dṛśyate, ākhānaḥ, ghañ api.
ākha ity anyato 'pi ceti ḍaḥ, karaṇe 'pi, ākharaḥ, ākhanikaḥ, ākhanikavaka iti ḍara-ika-ikavakā auṇādikā iti.


īṣadduḥsuṣu kṛcchrākṛcchrārtheṣu khal. Kāt_4,5.102

kṛcchraṃ duḥkhaṃ duso 'rthaḥ, akṛcchraṃ sukham itarayor arthaḥ, eṣūpapadeṣu kṛcchrākṛcchrārtheṣu dhātoḥ khal bhavati bhāve karmaṇi ca.
īṣad anāyāsena kriyate, īṣatkaraḥ kaṭo bhavatā.
duḥkhenāyāsena kriyate, duṣkaraḥ.
sukhenānāyāsena kriyate, sukaraḥ.
kṛcchrākṛcchrārtheṣv iti kim? īṣallabhyaṃ dhanam, kṛpaṇān manāg ity arthaḥ.


kartṛkarmaṇoś ca bhūkṛñoḥ. Kāt_4,5.103

īṣadādiṣūpapadeṣu kṛcchrākṛcchārtheṣu kartṛkarmaṇoś ca bhūkṛñoḥ khal bhavati, khānubandhabalāt kartṛkarmanor evānantaryam.
īṣadāḍhyena bhūyate, īṣadāḍhyaṃbhavaṃ bhavatā, durāḍhyaṃbhavam, svāḍhyaṃbhavam. 
īṣadāḍhyaḥ kriyate, īṣadāḍhyaṃkaro bhavān, durāḍhyaṃkaraḥ, svāḍhyaṃkaraḥ.
yadeṣadāḍhya eva san kiṃ cit kriyate tadā na bhavati, karoter ihābhūtaprādurbhāvārthatvāt.
yathāsaṃkhyād īṣadāḍhyo 'nubhūyata ity atra na bhavati.


ādbhyo yv adaridrāteḥ. Kāt_4,5.104

īṣadādiṣu kṛcchrākṛcchrārtheṣūpapadeṣvākārāntebhyo yur bhavati, adaridrāteḥ, īṣatpānaḥ, supānaḥ, duṣpānaḥ.
adaridrāter iti kim? īṣaddaridraḥ.


śāsuyudhidṛśidhṛṣimṛṣāṃ vā. Kāt_4,5.105

īṣadādiṣūpapadeṣu kṛcchrākṛcchrārtheṣv eṣāṃ yur bhavati vā, īṣacchāsanaḥ, īṣacchāsaḥ.
duḥśāsanaḥ, duḥśāsaḥ.
suśāsanaḥ, suśāsaḥ.
īṣadyodhanaḥ, īṣadyodhaḥ.
duryodhanaḥ, duryodhaḥ.
suyodhanaḥ, suyodhaḥ.
īṣaddarśanaḥ, īṣaddarśaḥ.
durdarśaṇaḥ, durdarśaḥ.
sudarśaṇaḥ, sudarśaḥ.
īṣaddharṣanaḥ, īṣaddharṣaḥ.
durdharṣaṇaḥ, durdharṣaḥ.
sudharṣaṇaḥ, sudharṣaḥ.
īṣanmarṣaṇaḥ, īṣanmarṣaḥ.
durmarṣaṇaḥ, durmarṣaḥ.
sumarṣaṇaḥ, sumarṣaḥ.
vāgrahaṇāt stryadhikārāt pareṣu na vāsarūpavidhir iti.


icchārtheṣv ekakartṛkeṣu tum. Kāt_4,5.106

icchārtheṣu dhātuṣv ekakartṛkeṣūpapadeṣu dhātos tum eva bhavati, na tu vuṇtumau kriyāyāṃ kriyārthāyām iti [Kāt_4,4.69] , icchati bhoktum, bhoktuṃ kāmayate.
ekakart(←v)ṛkeṣv iti kim? bhinnakartṛkeṣu vidhir mā bhūt, rājño bhojanam icchati, icchan karotīty api syāt.
icchārtheṣv iti kim? pācako vrajati.


kālasamayavelāśaktyartheṣu ca. Kāt_4,5.107

eṣūpoccāriṣūpapadeṣu dhātos tum eva bhavati.
kālo bhoktum, bhoktuṃ kālaḥ, samayo bhoktum, velā bhoktum, samartho bhoktum, bhoktuṃ śaktaḥ, prabhur bhoktum, paryāpto bhoktum, alaṃ bhoktum.
bhavater vṛter vā tādarthyasya pratīyamānatvāt, yathā bhoktuṃ manaḥ, gantuṃ kāmaḥ, śrotuṃ śrotram, draṣṭuṃ cakṣuḥ, yoddhuṃ dhanuḥ, vaktuṃ jaḍaḥ.
uccāraṇaṃ tu vaktur āyattam iti.
tathā śaktyarthāt, śaknoti bhoktum, pārayati bhoktum, dhṛṣṇoti bhoktum, jānāti bhoktum, glāyati bhoktum, ghaṭate bhoktum, ārabhate bhoktum, ālabhate bhoktum, prakramate bhoktum, utsahate bhoktum, arhati bhoktum, asti bhoktum, vidyate bhoktum, kriyāyāṃ kriyārthāyām iti tum siddha eva, vuṇ apy abhidhānād draṣṭavyaḥ.


arhatau tṛc. Kāt_4,5.108

arhatyarthaviśiṣṭād dhātos tṛj bhavati, kanyāyāḥ khalu bhavān voḍhā.
adhyetā khalu bhavāñ śāstrasya, prayogataś ceti.
arhe śaktau ca saptamī sā bādhikā yathā syād iti vacanam, bhavān khalu kanyām udvaheta, arhaḥ śakta ity arthaḥ.


śaki ca kṛtyāḥ. Kāt_4,5.109

śakanaṃ śak, śaktyarthaviśiṣṭād arhatyarthaviśiṣṭāc ca dhātoḥ kṛtyā bhavanti, bhavatā khalu kanyā voḍhavyā, vahanīyā, vāhyā, uhyeteti ca. 


praiṣyātisargaprāptakāleṣu. Kāt_4,5.110

praiṣyādiṣu gamyamāneṣu dhātoḥ kṛtyā bhavanti, preṣitas tvaṃ bhavatā grāmo gantavyaḥ, gamanīyaḥ, gamyaḥ.
atisargo 'numatiḥ, guruṇānujñātas tvaṃ bhavatā kaṭaḥ kartavyaḥ, karaṇīyaḥ, kāryaḥ, kṛtyaḥ.
prāptas te kālaḥ kaṭakaraṇe kartavyaḥ, karaṇīyaḥ, kṛtyaḥ, kāryaḥ kaṭo bhavatā.
ūrdhvaṃ muhūrtāt kaṭaḥ kartavya ity api vaktavyam.
praiṣyādiṣu pañcamīsaptamyuktā sā bādhikā syād iti vacanam.


āvaśyakādhamarṇayor ṇin. Kāt_4,5.111

avaśyaṃ bhāve gamyamāne 'dhamarṇe ca kartari dhātor ṇin bhavati, avaśyaṃ dāyī, avaśyaṃ kārī.
adhamarṇe ca, śataṃ dāyī, sahasraṃ dāyī, dāyī me śataṃ bhavān.


tikkṛtau saṃjñāyām āśiṣi. Kāt_4,5.112

āśīrviṣaye saṃjñāyāṃ gamyamānāyāṃ dhātos tikkṛtau bhavataḥ, tanutāt, tantiḥ. 
devāyainaṃ deyāt, devadattaḥ, evaṃ yajñadattaḥ.
vīro bhūyād iti vīrabhūtiḥ, mitrabhūtiḥ, agnir asya bhūyād ity agnibhūtiḥ.
saṃjñāśabdā yathākathaṃcid vyutpādyāḥ.


dhātusaṃbandhe pratyayāḥ. Kāt_4,5.113

dhātvarthānāṃ saṃbandhe viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvalakṣaṇe svaṃ kālaṃ tyaktvā viśeṣyasya dhātvarthasya kāle kṛtsaṃjñakāḥ pratyayāḥ sādhavo bhavanti na tu tyādayaḥ sādhyavihitatvāt.
sūtraṃ tv idaṃ sukhārtham eva.
agniṣṭomayājī putro 'sya janitā, agniṣṭomayājīti bhūte ṇiniḥ, janitety anena saṃbandhe bhaviṣyati sādhur bhavati, evaṃ kṛtaḥ kaṭaḥ śvo bhavitā, bhāvi kṛtyam āsīt, bhaviṣyati vihito ṇinir bhūte siddhaḥ.
prakaraṇāt kṛto labdhāḥ, pratyayagrahaṇaṃ sāmānyārtham.
gomān āsīt, gomān bhaviteti, gomān iti vartamāne mantuḥ, āsīd ity anena saṃbandhe 'tīte siddhaḥ, bhavitety anena bhaviṣyatīti.


iti daurgasiṃhyāṃ vṛttau kṛtsu pañcamaḥ pādaḥ samāptaḥ.



alaṃkhalvoḥ pratiṣedhayoḥ ktvā vā. Kāt_4,6.1

alaṃkhaluśabdayoḥ pratiṣedhārthayor upapadayor dhātoḥ ktvā bhavati vā, alaṃ kṛtvā, khalu kṛtvā.
alaṃ bhojanena, khalu bhojanena.
alaṃkhalvor iti kim? mā kārṣīḥ.
pratiṣedhārthayor iti kim? alaṃkāro niṣkasya, khaludānaṃ kanyāyāḥ, niścaye 'tra khaluśabdaḥ.


meṅaḥ. Kāt_4,6.2

mayateḥ ktvā bhavati vā, apūrvakālārthaṃ vaktavyam, apamāya, apamitya yācate, yapītvaṃ neṣyate, na yāceḥ ktvā, abhidhānāc ca, apamātuṃ yācate, yācitvāpamayate.


ekakartṛkayoḥ pūrvakāle. Kāt_4,6.3

ekakartṛkayor dhātvarthayor madhye yaḥ pūrvakriyākālas tasmin vartamānād dhātoḥ ktvā bhavati, śaktiśaktimator abhedavivakṣayaikakartṛkatā, bhuktvā vrajati, dvivacanasyātantratvāt parāpekṣayā vā, bhuktvā pītvā vrajati, ekakartṛkayor iti kim? bhuktavati gurau śiṣyo vrajati.
pūrvakāla iti kim? pacati ca paṭhati ca.
katham akṣiṇī nimīlya hasati, mukhaṃ vyādāya svapiti, muhūrtādikālasya vivakṣitatvāt.
kathaṃ mṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā duḥkhaṃ bhavati, priyaṃ dṛṣṭvā sukhaṃ syāt, bhinnakartṛkatvāc cintyam etat.


parāvarayoge ca. Kāt_4,6.4

parasyāvareṇa yoge 'varasya ca pareṇa yoge sati dhatoḥ ktvā bhavati, aprāpya nadīṃ parvataḥ, paranadīyogenāvaradeśasthaḥ parvato viśiṣyate.
atikramya parvataṃ nadī, avaraparvatayogena paradeśasthā nadī viśiṣyate.
bhavateḥ sarvatra saṃbhavād ekakartṛkatā pūrvakālatā ca duḥkhapratipattigamyeti vacanam.


ṇam cābhīkṣṇye dviś ca padam. Kāt_4,6.5

ekakartṛkayor dhātvarthayoḥ pūrvakāle vartamānād dhātor ṇam bhavati ktvā cābhīkṣṇye padaṃ ca dvir bhavati, bhojaṃ bhojaṃ vrajati, bhuktvā bhuktvā vrajati.
dviś ca padam iti sukhārtham evedam.
lunīhi lunīhīti lokato darśanāt.
yad ayaṃ bhuṅkte tato vrajati, yacchabdaprayoge tataḥśabdena kramasyābhidhānāt ktvā na bhavati, ābhīkṣṇyābhāvāc ca ṇam na syāt.
yad ayaṃ punaḥ punar bhuṅkte tato vrajati, punaḥpunaḥśabdenābhīkṣṇyasyābhidhānāt.
yad ayaṃ bhuṅktvā gacchati tato 'dhīta iti bhojanagamanayoḥ krame ktvā, gamanādhyayanayos tu kramasya tataḥśabdenābhidhānāt.


vibhāṣāgreprathamapūrveṣu. Kāt_4,6.6

eṣūpapadeṣu vibhāṣā dhātor ṇam bhavati, agre bhojaṃ vrajati, agre bhuktvā vrajati, prathamaṃ bhojaṃ vrajati, prathamaṃ bhuktvā vrajati, pūrvaṃ bhojaṃ vrajati, pūrvaṃ bhuktvā vrajati.
pūrvaṃ bhuṅkte tato vrajatīti tataḥśabdena kramasyābhidhānāt.


karmaṇy ākrośe kṛñaḥ khamiñ. Kāt_4,6.7

karmaṇy upapade kṛñaḥ khamiñ bhavati, ākrośe gamyamāne, cauraṃkāram ākrośati, karotir ihoccāraṇe, ākrośena kriyayaiva karma.
ākrośa iti kim? sādhu kṛtvā stauti.
khānubandho māgamārthaḥ.


svādau ca. Kāt_4,6.8

svādvarthe svāduḥ, tasminn upapade kṛñaḥ khamiñ bhavati, svāduṃkāraṃ bhuṅkte, saṃpannaṃkāraṃ bhuṅkte, lavaṇaṃkāraṃ bhuṅkte.
svādāv iti kim? rūpam idam adīrghāntatāṃ gamayati, tena svādūkṛtya svādvīṃ kṛtvā bhuṅkte yavāgūm.


anyathaivaṃkathamitthaṃsu siddhāprayogaś cet. Kāt_4,6.9

eṣūpapadeṣu kṛñaḥ khamiñ bhavati siddhāprayogaś cet karotir vartate, yasmād anyathādayaḥ śabdāḥ prakāram ācakṣate, ukteṣv api prayogāvirbhāvāyeti karotiḥ prayujyate, anyathākāraṃ bhuṅkte, evaṃkāraṃ bhuṅkte, kathaṃkāraṃ bhuṅkte, itthaṃkāraṃ bhuṅkte.
siddhāprayogaś ced iti kim? anyathā kṛtvā śiro bhuṅkte.


yathātathayor asūyāprativacane. Kāt_4,6.10

osyetvaṃ sūtratvāt [Ā_2,1.20] , asūyā 'kṣamā tadarthaṃ prativacanam, yathātathayoḥ kṛñaḥ khamiñ bhavati, asūyāprativacane gamyamāne, siddhāprayogaś cet karotir bhavati, yathākāram ahaṃ bhokṣye tathākāram ahaṃ bhokṣye kiṃ tavānena.
asūyāprativacana iti kim? yathā kṛtvāhaṃ bhokṣye, tathā kṛtvāhaṃ śiro bhokṣye kiṃ tavānena.


dṛśo ṇam sākalye. Kāt_4,6.11

sākalyaviśiṣṭe karmaṇy upapade dṛśo ṇam bhavati, kanyādarśaṃ varayati, yāṃ yāṃ kanyāṃ paśyati tāṃ sarvāṃ varayatīty arthaḥ.
vider vaktavyam, brāhmaṇavedaṃ bhojayati, yaṃ yaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jānāti labhate vicārayati taṃ sarvaṃ bhojayatīty arthaḥ.
sākalya iti kim? kaṃ cid brāhmaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhojayati.


yāvati vindajīvoḥ. Kāt_4,6.12

yāvad ity anirdiṣṭārthavācī, yāvad ity upapade vindater jīvateś ca ṇam bhavati, yāvadvedaṃ bhuṅkte, yāvad yāvantaṃ vā labhate tāvat tāvantaṃ vā bhuṅkta ity arthaḥ. yāvajjīvam adhīte, yāvaj jīvati tāvad adhīta ity arthaḥ.


carmodarayoḥ pūreḥ. Kāt_4,6.13

pūrir inanta eva sakarmakaḥ, carmodarayoḥ karmaṇor upapadayoḥ pūrayater ṇam bhavati, carmapūraṃ dadāti, udarapūraṃ bhuṅkte.


varṣapramāṇa ūlopaś ca vā. Kāt_4,6.14

karmaṇy upapade pūrayater ṇam bhavati varṣapramāṇe gamyamāne, pūrayater ūlopaś ca vā, goṣpadapūraṃ vṛṣṭo devaḥ, goṣpadapraṃ vṛṣṭo devaḥ.


celārthe knopeḥ. Kāt_4,6.15

celārthe karmaṇy upapade knopayater ṇam bhavati, varṣapramāṇe gamyamāne, celaknopaṃ vṛṣṭo devaḥ, vastraknopaṃ vṛṣṭo devaḥ, vasanaknopaṃ vṛṣṭo devaḥ.


nimūlasamūlayoḥ kaṣaḥ. Kāt_4,6.16

nimūlasamūlayoḥ karmaṇor upapadayoḥ kaṣater ṇam bhavati, nimūlakāṣaṃ kaṣati, samūlakāṣaṃ kaṣati, nimūlaṃ samūlaṃ kaṣatīty arthaḥ.


śuṣkacūrṇarukṣeṣu piṣaḥ. Kāt_4,6.17

eṣu karmasūpapadeṣu piṣor ṇam bhavati, śuṣkapeṣaṃ pinaṣṭi, cūrṇapeṣaṃ pinaṣṭi, rukṣapeṣaṃ pinaṣṭi, śuṣkaṃ pinaṣṭīty arthaḥ.


jīve grahaḥ. Kāt_4,6.18

jīve karmaṇy upapade graher ṇam bhavati, jīvagrāhaṃ gṛhṇāti, jīvaṃ gṛhṇātīty arthaḥ.


akṛte kṛñaḥ. Kāt_4,6.19

akṛte karmaṇy upapade kṛño ṇam bhavati, akṛtakāraṃ karoti, akṛtaṃ karotīty arthaḥ.


samūle hanteḥ. Kāt_4,6.20

samūle karmaṇy upapade hanter ṇam bhavati, samūlaghātaṃ hanti, samūlaṃ hantīty arthaḥ.


karaṇe. Kāt_4,6.21

karaṇavāciny upapade hanter ṇam bhavati, pādaghātaṃ bhūmiṃ hanti, pādena hantīty arthaḥ.
muṣṭighātaṃ cauraṃ hanti, muṣṭinā cauraṃ hantīty arthaḥ.
param api hiṃsārthāc caikakarmakād iti vacanaṃ bādhate karaṇasya vyaktitvāt.


hastārthe grahavartivṛtām. Kāt_4,6.22

hastārthe karaṇa upapada eṣāṃ ṇam bhavati, hastena gṛhṇāti, hastagrāhaṃ gṛhṇāti.
evaṃ karagrāhaṃ gṛhṇāti.
hastena vartayati, hastavartaṃ vartayati.
hastena vartate, hastavartaṃ vartate.


svārthe puṣaḥ. Kāt_4,6.23

svāny ātmātmīyajñātivittāni, svābhidheyeṣu karaṇeṣūpapadeṣu puṣo ṇam bhavati, svena poṣati puṣyati puṣṇāti vā, svapoṣaṃ poṣati, evam ātmapoṣam, ātmīyapoṣam, gopoṣam, mahiṣīpoṣam, pitṛpoṣam, mātṛpoṣam, vittapoṣam, raipoṣam.


snehane piṣaḥ. Kāt_4,6.24

snihyate sicyate 'neneti snehanam udakādi, snehavācini karaṇa upapade piṣo ṇam bhavati, udakena pinaṣṭi, udapeṣaṃ pinaṣṭi, evaṃ tailapeṣam, ghṛtapeṣam.
udakasyodaḥ peṣavāsavāhanadhiṣu ca nipātyate.


bandho 'dhikaraṇe. Kāt_4,6.25

adhikaraṇe nāmny upapade badhnāter ṇam bhavati, cakre baddhaḥ, cakrabandhaṃ baddhaḥ, guptibandhaṃ baddhaḥ, hastabandhaṃ baddhaḥ.


saṃjñāyāṃ ca. Kāt_4,6.26

adhikaraṇe 'nadhikaraṇe copapade badhnāter ṇam bhavati saṃjñāyāṃ gamyamānāyām, krauñce krauñcena vā baddhaḥ, krauñcabandhaṃ baddhaḥ.
evaṃ mayūrikābandham, aṭṭālikābandham.
bandhaviśeṣāṇām iyaṃ saṃjñā.


kartror jīvapuruṣayor naśivahibhyām. Kāt_4,6.27

jīvapuruṣayoḥ kartror upapadayor naśivahibhyāṃ ṇam bhavati yathāsaṃkhyaṃ, jīvanāśaṃ naṣṭaḥ, jīvo naṣṭa ity arthaḥ. puruṣavāhaṃ vahati, puruṣo vahatīty arthaḥ.
kartror iti kim? jīvena naṣṭaḥ, puruṣeṇoḍhaḥ.


ūrdhve śuṣipūroḥ. Kāt_4,6.28

ūrdhve kartṛvāciny upapade śuṣeḥ pūreś ca ṇam bhavati, ūrdhvaśoṣaṃ śuṣkaḥ, ūrdhvapūraṃ pūrṇaḥ, ūrdhvaḥ sann ity arthaḥ.

anyathākāraṃ bhuṅkta ity ādiṣu kim arthaṃ ṇamo vidhānam, vyāpyatvād dvitīyā bhaviṣyati, yathā, odanapākaṃ śete.
graher na ghañ iti kartavyam eva.
goṣpadaṃ prātīti goṣpadapram iti kriyāviśeṣaṇatvāt, tad ayuktam, tarāṃ tamāṃ ceṣyate 'vyayatvāt pūrvakālo 'pi yathābhidhānaṃ pratipādya eva, tathā ca vikalpādhikāre kvāpi dṛśyate, anyathākāraṃ bhujyata odana iti dvitīyā na syāt, yathā, odanaḥ paktvā bhujyate, kṛdavyayo hi bhāve 'bhidhānāt pradhānaśaktyabhidhāne guṇaśaktir avihitavat prakāśate.


karmaṇi copamāne. Kāt_4,6.29

kartari karmaṇi copamānavāciny upapade dhātor ṇam bhavati, cūḍaka iva naṣṭaḥ, cūḍakanāśaṃ naṣṭaḥ.
karmaṇi ca, suvarṇam iva nihitam, suvarṇanidhāyaṃ nihitam, odanapācaṃ pakvaḥ.
upamāna iti kim? cūḍako naṣṭaḥ, suvarṇaṃ nihitam.


kaṣādiṣu tair evānuprayogaḥ. Kāt_4,6.30

kaṣādiṣu ṇamo viṣayabhūteṣu tair eva kaṣādibhir anuprayogaḥ kartavyo nānyair iti, anuprayogaś ca pūrvakālatām abhidadhāty eva, nimūlakāṣaṃ kaṣati.
kaṣādiṣv iti kim? celaknopaṃ vṛṣṭo devaḥ.


tṛtīyāyām upadaṃśeḥ. Kāt_4,6.31

tṛtīyānta upapada upapūrvād danśer ṇam bhavati, mūlakenopadaṃśaṃ bhuṅkte, mūlakādikaraṇatayā bhujinā yuktam apy upadaṃśinā vyāptam ity upapadaṃ syāt, vādhikārād mūlakenopadaśya bhuṅkte.
tṛtīyāyām iti kim? mūlakam upadaśya bhuṅkte.


hiṃsārthāc caikakarmakāt. Kāt_4,6.32

tṛtīyānta upapade hiṃsārthād dhātor anuprayogeṇa samānakarmakāṇ ṇam bhavati, daṇḍenopaghātaṃ daṇḍopaghātaṃ gāḥ kalayati.
ekakarmakād iti kim? daṇḍenāhatya bhūmiṃ gopālako gāḥ sādayati.


saptamyāṃ ca pramāṇāsattyoḥ. Kāt_4,6.33

tṛtīyānte saptamyante copapade dhātor ṇam bhavati pramāṇe gamyamāne pratyāsattau ca, saṃbandhāvivakṣāyāṃ na yathāsaṃkhyam, dvyaṅgulenotkarṣam, dvyaṅgula utkarṣam, dvyaṅgulotkarṣaṃ gaṇḍikāṃ chinatti.
keśair grāham, keśeṣu grāham, keśagrāhaṃ yudhyante.


upapīḍarudhakarṣaś ca. Kāt_4,6.34

tṛtīyānte saptamyante copapada upapūrvebhya ebhyo ṇam bhavati, pārśvābhyām upapīḍaṃ, pārśvayor upapīḍaṃ, pārśvopapīḍaṃ śete.
vrajenoparodhaṃ, vraja uparodhaṃ, vrajoparodhaṃ gāḥ sādayati.
pāṇinopakarṣaṃ, pāṇāv upakarṣaṃ, pānyupakarṣaṃ dhānā bhakṣayati.


apādāne parīpsāyām. Kāt_4,6.35

pari samantād āptum icchā parīpsā tvarety arthaḥ, apādāna upapade dhātor ṇam bhavati parīpsāyāṃ gamyamānāyām, śayyāyā utthāyaṃ, śayyotthāyaṃ dhāvati.
randhrād upakarṣaṃ, randhropakarṣaṃ payaḥ pibati.
parīpsāyām iti kim? āsanād utthāya gacchati.


dvitīyāyāṃ ca. Kāt_4,6.36

dvitīyānte copapade dhātor ṇam bhavati parīpsāyāṃ gamyamānāyām, loṣṭaṃ grāhaṃ, loṣṭagrāhaṃ yudhyante, evaṃ nāma tvarante yenāyudham api nādriyante.


svāṅge 'dhruve. Kāt_4,6.37

svam aṅgaṃ svāṅgam, svāṅgasaṃjñake 'dhruve dvitīyānta upapade dhātor ṇam bhavati, bhruvau vikṣepaṃ, bhrūvikṣepaṃ jalpati.
akṣiṇī kāṇaṃ, akṣikāṇaṃ hasati.
adhruva iti kim? utkṣipya śiraḥ kathayati.
yasminn aṅge chinne prāṇī na mriyate tad adhruvam.


parikliśyamāne ca. Kāt_4,6.38

pari samantāt kliśyamāne svāṅge ca dvitīyānta upapade dhātor ṇam bhavati, urāṃsi pratipeṣaṃ, uraḥpratipeṣaṃ yudhyante, kṛtsnam uraḥ pīḍayitvā yudhyanta ity arthaḥ.


viśipatipadiskandāṃ vyāpyamānāsevyamānayoḥ. Kāt_4,6.39

vyāpyamāna āsevyamāne ca dvitīyānta upapada ebhyo dhātubhyo ṇam bhavati.
śrutatvād viśyādikriyābhiḥ sākalyena dravyāṇām eva saṃbandho vyāptir īpsāṃ, ato dravyasya dvirvacanam.
āsevā tātparyam ābhīkṣṇyaṃ tac ca kriyāyā eveti.
viśyādīnāṃ ṇamantānāṃ dvirvacanaṃ bhavati, gehaṃ geham anupraveśam āste, geham anupraveśam anupraveśam āste.
gehaṃ geham anuprapātam āste, geham anuprapātam anuprapātam āste.
gehaṃ geham anuprapādam āste, geham anuprapādam anuprapādam āste.
gehaṃ geham avaskandam āste, geham avaskandam avaskandam āste.
samāsa eva vīpsābhīkṣṇyārtham abhidhatte śabdaśaktitvāt, gehānupraveśam, gehānuprapātam, gehānuprapādam, gehāvaskandam āsta iti.
vyāpyamānāsevyamānayor iti kim? geham anupraviśya bhuṅkte.
ābhīkṣṇye ṇam siddha eva, upapadasamāsavibhāṣārtham idam.


tṛṣyasvoḥ kriyāntare kāleṣu. Kāt_4,6.40

kāleṣu dvitīyānteṣūpapadeṣu kriyāntare gamyamāne tṛṣyasvor ṇam bhavati, dvyahaṃ tarṣaṃ, dvyahatarṣaṃ gāḥ pāyayati.
dvyaham abhyāsaṃ, dvyahābhyāsaṃ gāḥ pāyayati, adya yat pānaṃ yac ca dvyahe 'tīte bhaviṣyati tanmadhyapātinā tarṣaṇenābhyasanena ca gavāṃ pānakriyā vyavadhīyate.
tṛṣyasvor iti kim? dvyaham upoṣya bhuṅkte.
kriyāntara iti kim? ahar abhyasyeṣūn gataḥ, abhyasaneneṣavaḥ kālāś ca vyāpyante na gatir vyavadhīyate.
kāleṣv iti kim? yojanam abhyasya gāḥ pāyayati.
kriyāgrahaṇaṃ sukhārtham.


nāmny ādiśigrahoḥ. Kāt_4,6.41

nāmni svarūpe dvitīyānta upapada ādiśer grahaś ca ṇam bhavati, nāmāny ādeśaṃ, nāmādeśaṃ dadāti.
nāmāni grāham, nāmagrāham āhvayati.


kṛño 'vyaye 'yatheṣṭākhyāne ktvā ca. Kāt_4,6.42

yatheṣṭam iti vīpsāyām avyayībhāvaḥ, avyaya upapade kṛño ṇam bhavati ktvā ca, ayatheṣṭākhyāne gamyamāne, brāhmaṇa putras te jātaḥ, nīcaiḥkāram, nīcaiḥkṛtya, nīcaiḥ kṛtvācaṣṭe, uccair nāma priyam ākhyeyam.
brāhmaṇa kanyā te garbhiṇī, kiṃ tarhi vṛṣaly uccaiḥkāram, uccaiḥkṛtya, uccaiḥ kṛtvācaṣṭe, nīcair nāmāpriyam ākhyeyam.
ayatheṣṭākhyāna iti kim? brāhmaṇa putras te jātaḥ, uccaiḥ kṛtvācaṣṭe.
samāsavikalpārthaṃ ktvāgrahaṇam.


tiryacy apavarge. Kāt_4,6.43

tiryakśabda upapade kṛño ṇam bhavati ktvā ca, apavarge(←ºga) gamyamāne, tiryakkāraṃ, tiryakkṛtya, tiryak(←ºtiyak) kṛtvā gataḥ, parisamāpya gata ity arthaḥ.
apavarga iti kim? tiryakkṛtvā kāṣṭhaṃ gataḥ.


svāṅge tasi. Kāt_4,6.44

svāṅgasaṃjñake taspratyayānta upapade kṛño ṇam bhavati, mukhataḥkāram(←sukhaº), mukhataḥkṛtya(←sukhaº), mukhataḥ(←sukhaº) kṛtvāste.
svāṅga iti kim? sarvataḥ kṛtvā gataḥ, avyayādhikārān mukhe tasyatīti mukhataḥ kṛtvā gata iti.


bhuvas tūṣṇīmi ca. Kāt_4,6.45

svāṅge taspratyayānte tūṣṇīmśabde copapade bhuvo dhātor ṇam bhavati ktvā ca.
mukhatobhāvam, mukhatobhūya, mukhato bhūtvāste.
tūṣṇīṃbhāvam, tūṣṇīṃbhūya, tūṣṇīṃ bhūtvāste.
kathaṃ nānākāraṃ, nānākṛtya, nānā kṛtvā bhuṅkte.
vinākāraṃ, vinākṛtya, vinā kṛtvā gata iti kriyāviśeṣaṇam eva, nāmnāṃ yuktārthatvād vā samāsaḥ, nānā kṛtvā kāṣṭhāni gata iti sāpekṣatvān na samāsaḥ, evaṃ nānābhāvam, nānābhūya, nānā bhūtvāste.
vinābhāvaṃ, vinābhūya, vinā bhūtvā gata iti.
tathā, anvagbhāvam, anvagbhūya, anvag bhūtvāste, ānukūlya eva samāso 'bhidhānāt, tenānvag bhūtvā tiṣṭhati śatruḥ.


kartari kṛtaḥ. Kāt_4,6.46

kṛtsaṃjñakāḥ pratyayāḥ kartari veditavyāḥ, karotīti kartā kārakaḥ, pacaḥ, nandanaḥ.
nirākāṅkṣeṣu vākyeṣu paribhāṣeyaṃ śeṣabhūtā vā, khyuṭkaraṇenāghrātatvād na pākṣikī vṛttiḥ.


bhāvakarmaṇoḥ kṛtyaktakhalarthāḥ. Kāt_4,6.47

pūrvasyāpavādo 'yam, bhāve karmaṇi ca kṛtyāḥ ktaḥ khalarthāś ca veditavyāḥ, śayitavyaṃ bhavatā, bhoktavya odano bhavatā, āsitaṃ bhavatā, kṛtaḥ kaṭo bhavatā, īṣadāḍhyaṃbhavaṃ bhavatā, īṣatkaraḥ kaṭo bhavatā, īṣatpānaṃ bhavatā, īṣatpānaḥ somo bhavatā.
arthād akarmakebhyo bhāve sakarmakebhyaś ca karmaṇīti.


ādikarmaṇi ktaḥ kartari ca. Kāt_4,6.48

ādikriyāyāṃ yaḥ kto vihitaḥ sa kartari kārake veditavyo yathāprāptaṃ ca, prakṛtaḥ kaṭaṃ bhavān, prakṛtaḥ kaṭo bhavatā, prasupto bhavān, prasuptaṃ bhavatā, praśabda ādikriyādyotakaḥ, bahūnāṃ kriyākṣaṇānām ādikriyākṣaṇo 'tīta eva, bhaviṣyati kaṭe kaṭaśabdas tādarthyāt.


gatyarthākarmakaśliṣaśīṅsthāsavasajanaruhajīryatibhyaś ca. Kāt_4,6.49

gatyarthebhyo 'karmakebhyaḥ śliṣādibhyaś ca kartari kto veditavyaḥ, cakārād yathāprāptaṃ ca.
gato grāmaṃ bhavān, prāpto grāmaṃ bhavān, gato grāmo bhavatā, prāpto grāmo bhavatā, gatam anena, prāptam anena.
akarmakebhyaḥ, śayito bhavān, śayitaṃ bhavatā.
śliṣādayaḥ sopasargāḥ sakarmakāḥ, śliṣa āliṅganārthaḥ, āśliṣṭo guruṃ bhavān, āśliṣṭo gurur bhavatā.
adhiśayitaḥ khaṭvāṃ bhavān, adhiśayitā khaṭvā bhavatā.
upasthito guruṃ bhavān, upasthito gurur bhavatā.
upāsito guruṃ bhavān, upāsito gurur bhavatā.
vasa nivāsārtha eva, anūṣito guruṃ bhavān, anūṣito gurur bhavatā.
anujāto māṇavako māṇavikām, anujātā māṇavikā māṇavakena.
ārūḍho vṛkṣaṃ bhavān, ārūḍho vṛkṣo bhavatā.
anujīrṇo vṛṣalīṃ bhavān, anujīrṇā vṛṣalī bhavatā.


dāśagoghnau saṃpradāne. Kāt_4,6.50

etau saṃpradāne nipātyete.
dāśṛ dāne, dāśante yasmai sa dāśaḥ, gāṃ hanti yasmā āgatāya sa goghno 'tithiḥ, nipātanād acṭakau.
arghyārhā ṛtvigādaya eva tadyogyatayāpy ucyante.


bhīmādayo 'pādāne. Kāt_4,6.51 

ete nipātyante 'pādāne, bibhety asmād iti bhīmaḥ, evaṃ bhīṣmaḥ.
caruḥ, praskandanaḥ, prapatanaḥ, samudraḥ, sruvaḥ.
eta auṇādikā vyutpattiś ca yathākathaṃcit.


tābhyām anyatroṇādayaḥ. Kāt_4,6.52

tābhyāṃ saṃpradānāpādānābhyām anyatra kāraka uṇādayo bhavanti, kṛttvād uṇādayaḥ kartari prāptāḥ karmādiṣv api kathyante.
karotīti kāruḥ, vātīti vāyuḥ, kṛṣyata iti kṛṣiḥ, tanyata iti tantuḥ.


kto 'dhikaraṇe dhrauvyagatipratyavasānārthebhyaḥ. Kāt_4,6.53

dhruvo niścalaḥ sa ca kriyāviśeṣaṇam, tasya bhāvo dhrauvyam, acalātmakakriyātmakatvād dhrauvyārthā akarmakā ucyante, pratyavasānaṃ bhojanam.
dhrauvyārthebhyo gatyarthebhyaḥ pratyavasānārthebhyaś ca kto 'dhikaraṇe veditavyo yathāprāptaṃ ca, idam eṣām āsitam, āsitam ebhiḥ, āsito bhavān.
idam eṣāṃ yātam, iha tair yātam, grāmas tair yātaḥ, grāmaṃ te yātāḥ.
adhikaraṇaṃ karmakartā ca noktam iti liṅgārthamātre prathamaiva.
idam eṣāṃ bhuktaṃ pītam, iha tair bhukta odanaḥ pītaṃ payaḥ, bhojanārthāt kartary api syād iti vyavahitaḥ pāṭhaḥ, kathaṃ bhuktvā viprāḥ pītā gāva iti, anyatrāpīti vacanāt, tadyogād arśa-āditvād vā, devaś ced vṛṣṭaḥ saṃpannāḥ śālaya iti śālihetavaḥ saṃpannā ity atītatā.


yuvujhām anākāntāḥ. Kāt_4,6.54

eṣāṃ sthāne 'na aka anta ity eta ādeśā bhavanti yathāsaṃkhyam, nandanaḥ, pācakaḥ, gaṇḍayantaḥ, maṇḍayantaḥ, gaṇḍimaṇḍijinandibhyo jhac.
kathaṃ bhujyuḥ, mṛtyuḥ, bhujimṛṅbhyāṃ yuktyukāv auṇādikasya bahulatvāt kṛdadhikārāc ca.
ūrṇāḥ santyasya, ūrṇāyuḥ.


samāse bhāviny anañaḥ ktvo yap. Kāt_4,6.55

naño 'nyasyāvyayasya ktvāntenaiva samāse bhāvini ktvāpratyayasya yab ādeśo bhavati, praṇamya, pradīvya, āpṛcchya, adhītya, upetya.
bhāvigrahaṇam upadeśayabartham iti tena pañcamopadhāprabhṛtīnāṃ dīrghādikaṃ na syāt to 'ntaś ca syāt, khāṭkṛtya, kanyām alaṃkṛtya, satkṛtya, asatkṛtya, antarhatya, kaṇehatya payaḥ pibati, manohatya payaḥ pibati, tāvat pibati yāvat tṛpta ity arthaḥ.
puraskṛtya, astaṃkṛtya, acchagatya, acchavrajya, acchodya, adaḥkṛtya cintayati, tirobhūya, tiraskṛtya, upājekṛtya, anvājekṛtya, sākṣātkṛtya, madhyekṛtya, padekṛtya, nivacanekṛtya, urasikṛtya, manasikṛtya, hastekṛtya, pāṇaukṛtya, prādhvaṃkṛtya, upaniṣatkṛtya, jīvikākṛtya.
anukaraṇaṃ ca kṛtā bhūṣaṇādarānādareṣv alaṃ sad asat, agrahaṇe 'ntar, tṛptau ca kaṇemanasī, puro 'staṃ ca, accha ca gatyarthavadibhiḥ, anupadeśe 'das, tiro 'ntardhau sa tiras, upāje 'nvāje, sākṣātprabhṛtīni ca kṛñā vā, madhye pade nivacane, anatyādhāna urasimanasī, nityaṃ haste pāṇāv udvāhe, bandhane prādhvam, upaniṣadaupamye jīvikā ca, pūrve samastāś ca.
samāsa iti kim? tiraḥ kṛtvā, upāje kṛtvā.
anaña iti kim? akṛtvā.
paryudāso 'yam, tena sasaṃkhyān na syāt, paramakṛtvā.


cajoḥ kagau dhuḍghānubandhayoḥ. Kāt_4,6.56

cajoḥ kagau bhavataḥ, dhuṭi ghānubandhe ca pratyaye pare, nimittena tu saṃbandhasyāvivakṣitatvān na yathāsaṃkhyam, paktā, bhoktā, pākaḥ, bhogaḥ.
rugnaḥ, bhugna iti nityam api natvaṃ bādhitvā 'ntaraṅgatvāc cavargasya kir asti.
aghānubandhe kṛti vyāvṛttiḥ syād iti dhuḍgrahaṇam.


nyaṅkvādīnāṃ haś ca ghaḥ. Kāt_4,6.57

nyaṅku, ity evam ādīnāṃ cajoḥ kagau bhavataḥ, haś ca gho bhavati.
nāv añcer uḥ, nyaṅkuḥ.
bhṛmṛtṝcaritsaritanimasjiśīṅbhya uḥ, madguḥ.
prathimradibhrasjāṃ saṃprasāraṇaṃ salopaś ca, bhṛguḥ.
sphāyitancivancīty āde rak, takram, vakram.
asun, ucyate 'sminn iti, okaḥ. 
vyatiṣaṅgaḥ, avasargaḥ, sanjeḥ sṛjeś ca.
pacād yac, śvapākaḥ, māṃsapākaḥ, kapotapākaḥ, ulūkapākaḥ, karmaṇy an, dūre pacyate svayam eva, phale pacyate svayam eva, pacād yac, gaṇanipātanād upadhāyā dīrghatvaṃ saptamyāś cāluk, dūrepākaḥ, phalepākaḥ, kṣaṇepāka iti ke cit, mehatīty ac, megho jalada eva.
avadāghaḥ, nidāghaḥ.
arhateḥ, arghaḥ.
ghañi saṃjñāyām, anyatrāvadāhaḥ, nidāhaḥ, arhaḥ.


na kavargādivrajyajām. Kāt_4,6.58

kavargāder vrajer ajeś ca cajoḥ kagau na bhavataḥ, kūjaḥ, kharjaḥ, garjaḥ, parivrājaḥ, udājaḥ, ājyaṃ ghṛtam.

vancer gatāv iti vaktavyam, vacyata iti vañcyaṃ gatā vaṇijaḥ, gantavyaṃ gatā ity arthaḥ.
gatāv iti kim? vaṅkyaṃ kāṣṭham, vancir atra kauṭilye.


ghyaṇy āvaśyake. Kāt_4,6.59

avaśyaṃbhāve gamyamāne ghyaṇi cajoḥ kagau na bhavataḥ, avaśyapācyam, avaśyabhojyam.
āvaśyaka iti kim? pākya odanaḥ.


pravacarciruciyācityajām. Kāt_4,6.60

anāvaśyakārthaṃ vacanam, eṣāṃ cajoḥ kagau na bhavataḥ, ghyaṇi pare, pravācyaḥ pāṭhaviśeṣaḥ, tadvān grantho 'py ucyata iti śabdaviṣayatā. ṛca stutau, arcyaḥ.
rocyaḥ, yācyaḥ, tyājyaḥ.
kathaṃ śocyaḥ, hetvinantatvāt.


vaco 'śabde. Kāt_4,6.61

vacer ghyaṇi ko na bhavati, aśabdaviṣaye, vācyam. 
aśabda iti kim? vākyaṃ padasamudāyaḥ.
vakravākyaracanāramaṇīya ity api syāt.


niprābhyāṃ yujaḥ śakye. Kāt_4,6.62

niprābhyāṃ parasya yujaḥ śakye 'rthe ghyaṇi go na bhavati, niyoktuṃ śakyaḥ, niyojyo bhṛtyaḥ, evaṃ prayojyaḥ.
śakya iti kim? niyoktum arhati, niyogyaḥ, prayogyaḥ prabhuḥ.


bhujo 'nne. Kāt_4,6.63

bhujo bhakṣe 'rthe ghyaṇi go na bhavati, bhojyam annam, bhojyaṃ payaḥ.
anna iti kim? bhogyaḥ kambalaḥ, bhogyā bhūḥ.


bhujanyubjau pāṇirogayoḥ. Kāt_4,6.64

bhujanyubjau ghañantau pāṇirogayor arthayor yathāsaṃkhyaṃ nipātyete, bhujyate 'neneti bhujaḥ pāṇiḥ, nyubjitaḥ śete 'sminn iti nyubjo rogaviśeṣaḥ, vyañjanāc ca [Kāt_4,5.99] iti ghañ.
pāṇirogayor iti kim? bhogaḥ, nyudgaḥ, gatve dopadha iṣyate.


dṛgdṛśadṛkṣeṣu samānasya saḥ. Kāt_4,6.65

samānasya dṛgādiṣu so bhavati, vacanāt kvipṭakśakaḥ.
sadṛk, sadṛśaḥ, sadṛkṣaḥ.
yogavibhāgāt pakṣādiṣu ca, sapakṣaḥ, sajyotiḥ, ity ādi yatheṣṭaṃ samāsaḥ, pakṣa, jyotiḥ, janapada, rātri, nābhi, bandhu, patnī.
rūpādau vā, samāno rūpaḥ, sarūpaḥ, rūpa, nāma, gotra, sthāna, varṇa, vayaḥ, dharma, jātīya, udara, udarya.
sabrahmacārīti nityam.


idam ī. Kāt_4,6.66

idam dṛgādiṣv īr bhavati, īḍṛk, īdṛśaḥ, īdṛkṣaḥ, abhedabalāt sarvasya.


kim kī. Kāt_4,6.67

kim dṛgādiṣu kīr bhavati, kīdṛk, kīdṛśaḥ, kīdṛkṣaḥ.
idaṃ kiṃ parimāṇam asya, iyān, kiyān, sadya-ādyatvāt.


ado 'mūḥ. Kāt_4,6.68

ado dṛgādiṣv amūr bhavati, amūdṛk, amūdṛśaḥ, amūdṛkṣaḥ.
ke cid amūkādṛk, amūkādṛśaḥ, amūkādṛkṣa iti tadāyatna eva.


ā sarvanāmnaḥ. Kāt_4,6.69

sarvanāmno dṛgādiṣv ā bhavati, tādṛk, tādṛśaḥ, tādṛkṣaḥ.
bhavādṛg ity antaraṅgatvān nalopaḥ.
anyādṛg iti sarvanāmna iti vacanād anyaśabdād api dṛśaḥ kvipṭakśag iti.
yattadetat parimāṇam asya, yāvān, tāvān, etāvān, iti sadya-ādyatvāt, parimāṇe vantub ātvaṃ ceti.


viṣvagdevayoś cāntyasvarāder adry añcatau kvau. Kāt_4,6.70

viṣvagdevayoḥ sarvanāmnaś cāntyasvarāder avayavaś cāñcatau kvibante pare 'drir ādeśo bhavati, viṣvag añcatīti viṣvadryaṅ, devadryaṅ.
yadryaṅ, tadryaṅ, sarvadryaṅ, adryaṅ, amudryaṅ.


sahasaṃtirasāṃ sadhrisamitirayaḥ. Kāt_4,6.71

eṣāṃ sadhri sami tiri, ity eta ādeśā yathāsaṃkhyaṃ bhavanti, añcatau kvibante, sahāñcatīti sadhryaṅ, samañcatīti samyaṅ, tiro 'ñcatīti tiryaṅ.


ruher dho vā. Kāt_4,6.72

ruher dho bhavati vā kvau pare, virohatīti vīrut, vīrudhau, vīruṭ, vīruhau, ver hrasvasya dīrghatā.
vyavasthitavibhāṣayā vipūrvasyaiva, tena bhūruṭ, bhūruhau.


mo no dhātoḥ. Kāt_4,6.73

dhātor makārasya nakāro bhavati kvau pare, śamu, praśān.
tamu, pratān.
no 'danta ity asya ca lopaḥ, kvau sthānivadbhāvāl liṅgāntanakārasya nalopo na syāt.
dhātugrahaṇaṃ vānivṛttyartham.


vamoś ca. Kāt_4,6.74

vamoś ca parayor dhātor mo no bhavati, jaganvān, ganmā, sarvadhātubhyo man.


svare dhātur anāt. Kāt_4,6.75

nakārāntaḥ svare pare dhātur eva bhavati, anāt, ākāro na nivartata ity arthaḥ, praśāmau, pratāmau, jagmuṣaḥ, jagmuṣī.
tadāśrita eva svare, tena praśān atreti.
svara iti kim? praśānbhyām.
ye ceṣyate, praśāmam icchati, praśāmyati, praśāme hitam, praśāmyam.


artīṇghasaikasvarātām iḍ vansau. Kāt_4,6.76

artīṇghasaikasvarādantānām eva vansāv iḍ bhavaty ādiḥ.
srādiniyamena parokṣāvadbhāvād iṭ siddho niyamyate [Kāt_3,7.35].
ārivān, īyivān, jakṣivān, ādivān, pecivān, dadivān, papivān.
daridrāṃ cakṛvān ity āmā bhāvyam.
ārtyādigrahaṇād eva vansau dvirvacane saty ekasvarā grahītavyā naikatvaṃ vacanād iṇaḥ.
eṣām iti kim? babhajvān, jajāgarvān.


gamahanavidaviśadṛśāṃ vā. Kāt_4,6.77

aprāpte vibhāṣeyam, eṣāṃ vansāv iḍ vā bhavati, jagmivān, jaganvān, jaghnivān, jaghanvān, vividivān, vividvān, bahubhiḥ savikaraṇaiḥ sāhacaryāl lābhārthasya vider grahaṇam.
viviśivān.
viviśvān, dadṛśivān, dadṛśvān.


dāśvān sāhvān mīḍhvāṃś ca. Kāt_4,6.78

ete nipātyante,

dvirvacanam aniṭtvaṃ ca saher dīrgho miher api,
ḍhatvaṃ ca khalu tantratvāt sarvāṇi vacanāni ca.


na śryuvarṇavṝtāṃ kānubandhe. Kāt_4,6.79

śrayater uvarṇāntasya vṛñvṛṅor ṛkārāntasya ca kānubandhe sārvadhātuke neḍ bhavati, śritaḥ, śritavān, śritvā.
yutaḥ, yutavān, yutvā.
rutaḥ, rutavān, rutvā.
lūnaḥ, lūnavān, lūtvā.
vṛtaḥ, vṛtavān, vṛtvā.
kīrṇaḥ, kīrṇavān, kīrttvā.
vacanād vikṛte 'pi syāt, śeśriyitaḥ, loluvita iti siddhaye.
ekasvaram anuvartayanty anye, teṣām ūrṇoter vaktavyam eva, prorṇutaḥ, prorṇutavān.


ghoṣavattyoś ca kṛti. Kāt_4,6.80

ghoṣavati tau ca kṛtsaṃjñake neḍ bhavati, īśvaraḥ, dīpraḥ, śarmā, dīptiḥ, jāgartiḥ, buddhiḥ.
tik ca, tantiḥ, santiḥ.
kathaṃ nigṛhītiḥ, nipaṭhitiḥ, nikucitiḥ, ālocitiḥ, upasnihitiḥ, maṇḍūkaplutivādhikārād grahāder iḍ bhavati.
apacitir iti pūjāyāṃ niṣkṛtau ca.
kathaṃ śastram, āgamasyānityatvāt.
patram iti yugyaṃ patre [Kāt_4,2.32] iti vacanāt.


veṣusahalubharuṣariṣāṃ ti. Kāt_4,6.81

eṣāṃ takārādāv asārvadhātuka iḍ bhavati vā, eṣṭā, eṣitā.
soḍhā, sahitā.
lobdhā, lobhitā.
roṣṭā, roṣitā.
reṣṭā, reṣitā.
udanubandhaḥ kim? iṣa gatau, ābhīkṣṇya eṣitā nityam.


radhādibhyaś ca. Kāt_4,6.82

tīti na vartate pṛthagvacanāt.
ṭānubandhaliṅgād radhādibhyaś ca parasyāsārvadhātukasya vyañjanāder ayakārāder iḍ bhavati vā, ratsyati, radhiṣyati.
naṅkṣyati, naśiṣyati.
āvṛtkaraṇaṃ radhādiḥ, rarandhiva, rarandhima, iti srādiniyamān nityam iṭ. 


svaratisūtisūyatyūdanubandhāt. Kāt_4,6.83

svarateḥ sūteḥ sūyater ūdanubandhāc ca parasyāsārvadhātukasya vyañjanāder ayakārāder ādir iḍ bhavati vā, svartā, svaritā.
sotā, savitā.
suvates tu nityam, savitā.
nigoḍhā, nigūhitā.
vidhotā, vidhaviteti dhuñā dhūñā ca siddham.
svariṣyatīti paratvād vikalpo na syād vyavasthitavāvacanāt.
tathā svṛsūṅoś ca kānubandhe nityaṃ syāt, svṛtvā, sūtveti.
apatiniṣkuṣor iti [Kāt_4,6.90] vacanād niṣkuṣor veḍ astīti gamyate.
asārvadhātukasya vyañjanāder ayakārāder iti niṣkoṣṭā, niṣkoṣitā.


udanubandhapūkliśāṃ ktvi. Kāt_4,6.84

udanubandhāt puvaḥ kliśaś ca ktvīḍ bhavati vā, śamu, śāntvā, śamitvā.
pūṅ pūñ vā, pūtvā, pavitvā.
kliṣṭvā, kliśitvā.
ūdanubandhasya kliśaś ca prāpte vibhāṣā, puvaḥ kānubandhe 'prāpta eva.


jṝvraścor iṭ. Kāt_4,6.85

jṝvraścibhyāṃ ktvīḍ bhavati, jaritvā, jarītvā, vraścitvā.
lākṣaṇikatvād jṝṣa jīrtvā, vraścer vacanān nityam iḍ iti.
punar iḍgrahaṇam uttaratra vānivṛttyartham.


lubho vimohane. Kāt_4,6.86

vimohane lubhaḥ ktvīḍ bhavati, lubhitvā.
gārddhye tu, lubdhvā, lubhitvā.


kṣudhivasoś ca. Kāt_4,6.87

cakāreṇa lubho vimohana ity anukṛṣyata uttarārtham, kṣudhivasoś ca ktvīḍ bhavati, kṣudhitvā, uṣitvā, pratiṣedhabādhakam idam.


niṣṭhāyāṃ ca. Kāt_4,6.88

kṣudhivasibhyāṃ vimohane lubhaś ca niṣṭhāyām iḍ bhavati, kṣudhitaḥ, kṣudhitavān, uṣitaḥ, uṣitavān, lubhitaḥ, lubhitavān.
gārddhye vyāvṛttyā vibhāṣāpi bādhyate, lubdhaḥ, lubdhavān.


pūkliśor vā. Kāt_4,6.89

puvaḥ kliśaś ca niṣṭhāyām iḍ bhavati vā, pavitaḥ, pavitavān, pūtaḥ, pūtavān.
kliśa kliśū, kliśitaḥ, kliśitavān, kliṣṭaḥ, kliṣṭavān.


na ḍīśvīdanubandhaveṭām apatiniṣkuṣoḥ. Kāt_4,6.90

ebhyo dhātubhyaḥ patiniṣkuṣavarjitebhyo niṣṭhāyāṃ neḍ bhavati, uḍḍīnaḥ, uḍḍīnavān.
śūnaḥ, śūnavān.
dīpī, dīptaḥ, dīptavān.
olasjī, lagnaḥ, lagnavān.
lasjer odanubandhabalād iḍabhāve natvaṃ syāc ced īdanubandhaḥ kim? savikalpakaṃ vā jñāpakaṃ syād iti, tathā ḍī śvī ca kartavyau.
vikalpeṭāṃ ca, guhū, gūḍhaḥ, gūḍhavān.
śamu, śāntaḥ, śāntavān.
apatiniṣkuṣor iti kim? patitaḥ, patitavān, niṣkuṣitaḥ, niṣkuṣitavān.
kathaṃ daridritaḥ, daridritavān, ekasvaro 'tra smartavyaḥ, apatiniṣkuṣor iti paryudāsād vā.


ādanubandhāc ca. Kāt_4,6.91

ādanubandhāc ca dhātor niṣṭhāyāṃ neḍ bhavati, ñimidā, minnaḥ, minnavān.
ñikṣvidā, kṣviṇṇaḥ, kṣviṇṇavān.
cakāro 'nuktasamuccayārthaḥ, tena japivamibhyāṃ vā, japtaḥ, japitaḥ, vāntaḥ, vamitaḥ.
vyāṅbhyāṃ śvasaḥ, viśvastaḥ, viśvasitaḥ, āśvastaḥ, āśvasitaḥ.
kartari karmaṇi cāyaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ, bhāvādikarmaṇor veti vakṣyati.


bhāvādikarmaṇor vā. Kāt_4,6.92

ādanubandhād dhātor bhāva ādikriyāyāṃ ca niṣṭhāyām iḍ bhavati vā, minnaṃ meditam anena, praminnaḥ pramedito bhavān, veṭtvāt siddho yogavibhāgo jñāpayati yadarthasya vibhāṣā tadarthasyaiva pratiṣedha iti tena gamahanavidaviśadṛśāṃ vā [Kāt_4,6.77] iti sāhacaryāl lābhārthasya vider grahaṇe jñānārthasya pratiṣedho na syāt, viditaḥ, viditavān.


kṣubhivāhisvanidhvaniphaṇikaṣighuṣāṃ kte neḍ manthabhṛśamanastamo'nāyāsakṛcchrāviśabdaneṣu. Kāt_4,6.93

ebhyo manthādiṣv artheṣu kte neḍ bhavati yathāsaṃkhyam, kṣubdho manthaḥ, calito mantha ity arthaḥ, mantha iti dravadravyāloḍitāḥ saktava ucyante.
vāhṛ prayatne, vāḍhaṃ bhṛśam, atrāvṛttyātiśayo 'bhyupagamaś ca gṛhyate, na tu śīghrārthaḥ.
svāntaṃ manaḥ, vāhyeṣv(←p) avikṣiptam ity arthaḥ.
dhvāntaṃ tamaḥ.
phaṇa gatau, phāṇṭam, anāyāsaniryātatvāt sadyo bhiṣajoddhṛtauṣadhaṃ dravadravyam eveṣyate.
kaṣa śiṣa, kaṣṭo 'gniḥ, kaṣṭaḥ parvataḥ, kṛcchrahetutvāt kṛcchraṃ gahanam apy ucyate, kṛcchraṃ duḥkham(←daḥkham), sati mukhye gauṇe 'py abhidhānam.
ghuṣiraśabda iti bhvādau, ghuṣṭā rajjuḥ, ghuṣṭaṃ śarīram, ghuṣiraviśabdana iti curādau viśabdane tu syād iṭ, avaghuṣitaṃ vākyam āha, viśabdana iti pratiṣedhāc curādāv in syād vibhāṣayeti tenedaṃ siddham, mahīpālavacaḥ śrutvā jughuṣuḥ puṣpamānavāḥ, anekārthatvād bhauvādika eva vā viśabdane 'pi, svābhiprāyaṃ śabdenāviṣkṛtavanta ity arthaḥ.
manthādiṣv iti kim? kṣubhitaḥ, vāhitaḥ, svanitaḥ, dhvanitaḥ, phaṇitaḥ, kaṣitaḥ, ghuṣitaḥ.
tathā bhinnādhikaraṇe 'pi, kṣubhitaṃ manthena, vāhitaṃ bhṛśena, svanitaṃ manasā, dhvanitaṃ tamasā, phaṇitam anāyāsena, kaṣitaṃ kṛcchreṇa, ghuṣitaṃ śarīreṇa.
katham udghuṣṭaṃ kokilayeti prakṛtyarthaviśeṣaṇāt.
kathaṃ kṣubdhaḥ samudra ity upamānād bhaviṣyati.


lagnamliṣṭaviribdhāḥ saktāvispaṣṭasvareṣu. Kāt_4,6.94

lagnādayaḥ ktāntāḥ saktādiṣv artheṣu yathāsaṃkhyaṃ nipātyante, lage, lagnaṃ saktam, lagitam anyat.
mlecha, mliṣṭam avispaṣṭam, mlecchitam anyat.
rebhṛ, viribdhaḥ svaraḥ, svaro dhvanir atra, virebhitam anyat, anye tu viribhitam iti pratyudāharanti, ribhiṃ sautraṃ dhātuṃ matveti.
dhṛṣṭo viśastaḥ, dhṛṣer ādanubandhāt, śasoś codanubandhād veḍ iti pratiṣedhaḥ prāgalbhya eva rūḍhaḥ, anyo dharṣitaḥ, viśasita ity abhidhānān naño 'nityatvād vā.


parivṛḍhadṛḍhau prabhubalavatoḥ. Kāt_4,6.95

etau prabhubalavator arthayor yathāsaṃkhyaṃ nipātyete, paripūrvasya vṛṃher iḍbhāvo nalopaś ca, tathā dṛṃheś ca, vṛhadṛhau prakṛtyantare tayor apīty eke, parivṛḍhaḥ prabhuḥ, dṛḍho balavān, sthūlo 'pi, dṛḍho balavān evābhidhīyate.
kathaṃ parivṛḍhayya gataḥ, parivṛḍhād in samāsābhāvād yab na syāt, satyam, tatkarotīti siddhe saṃgrāmayuddha iti gaṇapāṭho jñāpayati, nāmamātrād in.
apacāyitaḥ, apacita iti cāyinā ciñā ca pūjāvṛttinā siddham.
kathaṃ vṛttaṃ pārāyaṇaṃ vipreṇa, vṛtto guṇaś chāttreṇeti, antarbhūte 'narthavṛtter bhaviṣyati, inantasyāpi, vartito guṇo 'neneti bhavitavyam iti matam, anye tv ino 'dhyayane vṛttam iti nipātayanti.


saṃnivibhyo 'rdeḥ. Kāt_4,6.96

saṃnivibhyaḥ parasyārdateḥ kte neḍ bhavati, samarṇṇaḥ, nyarṇṇaḥ, vyarṇṇaḥ.
niṣṭhāyām anipāteṣv ity anye.


sāmīpye 'bheḥ. Kāt_4,6.97

abheḥ parasyārdateḥ kte neḍ bhavati sāmīpye 'rthe, abhyarṇṇā senā, sāmīpya ity arthaḥ.
anatidūra ity eke 'bhidhānāt.


vā ruṣyamatvarasaṃghuṣāsvanām. Kāt_4,6.98

ebhyaḥ kte neḍ bhavati vā, ruṣṭaḥ, ruṣitaḥ, veṣusahalubharuṣety ādinā veṭtvāt pratiṣedhaḥ prāptaḥ.
ama gatau na tv ama roga inantatvāt, abhyāntaḥ, abhyamitaḥ.
tūrṇaḥ, tvaritaḥ, ādanubandhāc ceti pratiṣedhaḥ prāptaḥ.
saṃghuṣṭaṃ, saṃghuṣitaṃ vākyam āha.
saṃghuṣṭau, saṃghuṣitau damyau.
saṃpūrvo ghuṣir aviśabdane 'pi paratvād ayam eva.
āṅpūrvasya svana, āsvāntaḥ, āsvanito mṛdaṅgaḥ, āsvāntaṃ, āsvanitaṃ manaḥ, paratvān mano 'bhidhāne 'py ayam eva.


hṛṣer lomasu. Kāt_4,6.99

lomasu vartamānād hṛṣeḥ kte neḍ bhavati vā, hṛṣṭāni, hṛṣitāni lomāni.
hṛṣṭaṃ, hṛṣitaṃ lomabhiḥ.
hṛṣṭāḥ, hṛṣitāḥ keśāḥ.
hṛṣu ālīkya ity udanubandhatvād niṣṭhāyām aniṭ.
hṛṣa tuṣṭāv ity ayaṃ tu seṭ, ubhayor api vibhāṣeyam.
lomāny aṅgajāni mūrdhajāni ca gṛhyante, yathā loma nakhaṃ spṛṣṭvā śaucaṃ kartavyam iti.
hṛṣir lomasu vartamāno lomakartaka eva.
lomasv iti kim? hṛṣṭaś chāttra ity alīkārthasya, hṛṣitaś chāttra iti tuṣṭārthasya.
lomasv ity upalakṣaṇaṃ vismayapratighātayor vā syāt, hṛṣṭo hṛṣitaś chāttraḥ, vismita ity arthaḥ.
hṛṣṭā hṛṣitā dantāḥ, pratihatā ity arthaḥ.


dāntaśāntapūrṇadastaspaṣṭacchannajñaptāś cenantāḥ. Kāt_4,6.100

eta inantā vā nipātyante, dāntaḥ, damitaḥ.
śāntaḥ, śamitaḥ.
pūrī daivādikaś caurādikaś ca, pūrṇaḥ, pūritaḥ.
dasu, dastaḥ, dāsitaḥ.
spaṣṭaḥ, spāśitaḥ.
chada khaṭṭa saṃvaraṇe, channaḥ, chāditaḥ.
māraṇatoṣaṇaniśāmaneṣu jñā mānubandhaś ca, jñaptaḥ, jñapitaḥ, iṭpratiṣedha ino lug nipātyate, jñaper veṭtvād nityaṃ pratiṣedhe prāpte.


rān niṣṭhāto no 'pṝmūrchimadikhyādhyābhyaḥ. Kāt_4,6.101

rephāt parasya niṣṭhātakārasya nakāro bhavati, na tu pṝmūrchimadikhyādhyābhyaḥ, śīrṇaḥ, śīrṇavān.
gurī, avagūrṇaḥ, avagūrṇavān.
yadi raśrutir api syāt kṛtam iti na natvam ṛkārāvayavena vyavadhānāt, caritam ity atra niṣṭhāvayaveneṭā vyavadhānāt, kṛtasyāpatyaṃ kārttir ity asiddhaṃ bahiraṅgam antaraṅga iti.
pratiṣedhaḥ kim? pṝ, pūrtaḥ.
mūrchā, mūrtaḥ.
madikhyādhyābhyaḥ parābhyāṃ prāpte, mattaḥ, khyātaḥ, dhyātaḥ.


dād dasya ca. Kāt_4,6.102

dakārāt parasya niṣṭhātakārasya nakāro bhavati dakārasya ca, minnaḥ, minnavān.


āto 'ntaḥsthāsaṃyuktāt. Kāt_4,6.103

antaḥsthāsaṃyuktād ākārāt parasya niṣṭhātakārasya nakāro bhavati, glānaḥ, glānavān, viśrāṇaḥ, viśrāṇavān, mlānaḥ, mlānavān.
dhātvadhikārāt(←ºadhikāt), niryātaḥ, niryātavān.


lvādyodanubandhāc ca. Kāt_4,6.104

lūñādibhya odanubandhebhyaś ca parasya niṣṭhātakārasya nakāro bhavati, lūñ, lūnaḥ, lūnavān.
jyā, jīnaḥ, jīnavān.
rujo, rugnaḥ, rugnavān.
bhujo, bhugnaḥ, bhugnavān.
svādaya odanubandhāḥ, ṣūṅ prāṇiprasave, sūnaḥ, sūnavān.
dūṅ, dūnaḥ, dūnavān, gaṇakṛtasyānityatvāt.
pūño nāśe, pūnā yavāḥ, vinaṣṭā ity arthaḥ, nāśa iti kim? pūtaṃ dhānyam, kampitam ity arthaḥ.
dugvor dīghaś ca, vidūnaḥ, vidūnavān, vigūnaḥ, vigūnavān.
cakāro 'nuktasamuccayārthaḥ.
ṝlvādibhyaś ca kteḥ, kīrṇiḥ, gīrṇiḥ, lūniḥ, pūniḥ, dhūniḥ.
lyī ceti yāval lvādis tato vṛtkaraṇāt.
hājyāglābhyaś ca, hāniḥ, jyāniḥ, glāniḥ.


vraśceḥ ka ca. Kāt_4,6.105

vraśceḥ parasya niṣṭhātakārasya nakāro bhavati kādeśaś cānte, vraścer eva śrutatvāc chopadhasya vraścer dhuṭy antalope sati ṣatvabādhakaṃ katvaṃ syāt, vṛkṇaḥ, vṛkṇavān.


kṣer dīrghāt. Kāt_4,6.106

dīrghāntāt parasya kṣer niṣṭhātakārasya nakāro bhavati, kṣīṇaḥ, kṣīṇavān.
dīrghād iti kim? kṣitāyur jālmaḥ, kṣitakas tapasvī.


śyo 'sparśe. Kāt_4,6.107

asparśe vartamānāc chyāyater niṣṭhātakārasya nakāro bhavati, śīnaṃ ghṛtam, śīnavad ghṛtam.
asparśa iti prasajyo 'yaṃ nañ, śītaṃ jalam, guṇabhūto 'pi sparśo natvapratiṣedhasya saṃprasāraṇasya ca nimittam, na tu roge, tena pratiśīnam iti natvaṃ bhavaty eva.


anapādāne 'nceḥ. Kāt_4,6.108

anapādāne vartamānād añcateḥ parasya niṣṭhātakārasya nakāro bhavati, samaknaḥ, samaknavān, saṃsakta ity arthaḥ.
anapādāna iti kim? udaktam udakam, kūpād uddhṛtam ity arthaḥ.
vyaktam ity anje rūpam.
añcitaḥ, añcitavān iti, iṭā vyavahitatvāt, pūjāyām añcater iḍbhāvo nalopaś ca neṣyate.


avijigīṣāyāṃ divaḥ. Kāt_4,6.109

avijigīṣāyāṃ vartamānād divaḥ parasya niṣṭhātakārasya nakāro bhavati, ādyūnaḥ, ādyūnavān.
avijigīṣāyām iti kim? dyūtaṃ vartate, vijigīṣayā hy akṣapātaḥ kriyate.
sinoteḥ karmakartari grāse vaktavyam, sino grāsaḥ svayam eva, baddha ity arthaḥ.


hrīghrātrondanudavindāṃ vā. Kāt_4,6.110

ebhyaḥ parasya niṣṭhātakārasya nakāro bhavati vā, hrīṇaḥ, hrīṇavān, hrītaḥ, hrītavān.
ghrāṇaḥ, ghrāṇavān, ghrātaḥ, ghrātavān.
trāṇaḥ, trāṇavān, trātaḥ, trātavān.
undī, samunnaḥ, samunnavān, samuttaḥ, samuttavān.
nuda, nunnaḥ, nunnavān, nuttaḥ, nuttavān.
vida vicāre, vinnaḥ, vinnavān, vittaḥ, vittavān.
vyavasthitavibhāṣayā nityaṃ saṃjñāyām, devatrātaḥ.
tathā,

vicārārthād(←ºārdhād) vibhāṣaiva jñānārthān nityam iḍ yataḥ, 
bhogād anyatra lābhārthāt sattārthāc ca videḥ sadā.


kṣaiśuṣipacāṃ makavāḥ. Kāt_4,6.111

ebhyas tribhyo yathāsaṃkhyaṃ niṣṭhātakārasya makavā bhavanti, kṣāmaḥ, kṣāmavān.
śuṣkaḥ, śuṣkaṣān.
pakvaḥ, pakvavān.
dvayor vibhāṣayor madhye yo vidhiḥ sa nitya eva.


vā prastyo maḥ. Kāt_4,6.112

prapūrvasya styāyater vā niṣṭhātakārasya makāro bhavati, prastīmaḥ, prastīmavān, prastītaḥ, prastītavān, matvān nityaṃ saṃprasāraṇam.


nirvāṇo 'vāte. Kāt_4,6.113

nirvāṇa iti nipātyate vātaviṣayaś ced dhātvartho na bhavati, nirvāṇo 'gniḥ, dīptyuparame vartate.
nirvāṇo bhikṣuḥ, rāgādipraśamane 'tra.
avāta iti kim? nirvāto vātaḥ, virodhe 'tra.
kathaṃ nirvāṇo dīpo vātena, atra vātaḥ karaṇaṃ na tv ādhāraḥ, nirvātaṃ vāteneti bhāve 'pi vāta eva kartā.


bhittarṇavittāḥ śakalādhamarṇabhogeṣu. Kāt_4,6.114

bhittādayaḥ ktāntāḥ śakalādiṣv artheṣu yathāsaṃkhyaṃ nipātyante, bhittaṃ śakalam iti paryāyaḥ.
ṛ gatau, ṛṇaṃ śodhyam, ṛṇe 'dhamo 'dhamarṇaḥ, tadviṣaye nipātanam.
adhamarṇagrahaṇaṃ kālāntarādiviniyamopalakṣaṇaṃ tenottamarṇaviṣaye 'pi syāt.
vidḷ, vittaṃ dravyam, bhujyata iti bhoga ucyate, vittam iva vittam ity upacārāt pratīte 'py abhidhīyate.


anupasargāt phullakṣībakṛśollāghāḥ. Kāt_4,6.115

ete ktāntā nipātyante na ced upasargāt pare bhavanti, dala ñiphalā viśaraṇe niṣṭhātakārasya latvam, phullaḥ.
ktavantor api latvam icchanty anye, phullavān.
kṣībṛkṛśibhyām utpūrvāc ca lāgheḥ parasyaiva niṣṭhātakārasyaiva lopa iḍbhāvaś ca, kṣībaḥ, kṛśaḥ, ullāghaḥ.
anupasargād iti kim? praphultaḥ, prakṣībitaḥ, prakṛśitaḥ, prollāghitaḥ.
kathaṃ saṃpraphullaḥ, utpraphullaḥ, phulla vikasane 'cā siddham.
parikṛśa iti kena siddham, vacanaṃ tu rūpāntaraṃ syād iti.


avarṇād ūṭo vṛddhiḥ. Kāt_4,6.116

dhātor adhātor vā 'varṇāt parasyoṭo vṛddhir bhavati.
śava, śauḥ, śāvau, śāvaḥ.
dhāvu, dhautaḥ, dhautavān(←ghº).
avanam, ūtiḥ.
paṭotiḥ.
janān avati, janauḥ, janāvau.
ūṭa iti kim? adyoḍhā, katoḍhā.
aur iti siddhe vṛddhigrahaṇaṃ maṅgalārtham.


iti daurgasiṃhyāṃ vṛttau kṛtsu ṣaṣṭhaḥ pādaḥ samāptaḥ.

iti kātantraṃ samāptam.
